My Articles

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMjQgMjQiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHN0cm9rZT0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiBzdHJva2Utd2lkdGg9IjIiIHN0cm9rZS1saW5lY2FwPSJyb3VuZCIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgZGF0YS1ybnctaW50LWNsYXNzPSJuZWFyZXN0X19fNTc0LTEyMzYxXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNOSAxOGw2LTYtNi02Ij48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

<a href="https://www.gitbook.com/?utm_source=content&amp;utm_medium=trademark&amp;utm_campaign=-MjLjuvITJh8ZwT8mVxp" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1uwl36a r-z2wwpe r-1rasi3h r-1loqt21 r-18u37iz src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgNTEyIDUxMiIgZmlsbD0ibm9uZSIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItZXUza2Egci0xYW9ja2lkIiBzdHlsZT0idmVydGljYWwtYWxpZ246bWlkZGxlIj48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTIzMC40MzQgMzc5LjU1NGM4LjI1OSAwIDE0Ljk3OCA2LjcxOSAxNC45NzggMTQuOTc0IDAgOC4yNTYtNi43MTkgMTQuOTc0LTE0Ljk3OCAxNC45NzQtOC4yNTUgMC0xNC45NzQtNi43MTgtMTQuOTc0LTE0Ljk3NCAwLTguMjU1IDYuNzE5LTE0Ljk3NCAxNC45NzQtMTQuOTc0em0yMzUuMTg5LTkyLjc1OGMtOC4yNTkgMC0xNC45NzgtNi43MTktMTQuOTc4LTE0Ljk3NCAwLTguMjU5IDYuNzE5LTE0Ljk3OCAxNC45NzgtMTQuOTc4IDguMjU1IDAgMTQuOTc0IDYuNzE5IDE0Ljk3NCAxNC45NzggMCA4LjI1NS02LjcxOSAxNC45NzQtMTQuOTc0IDE0Ljk3NHptMC02MS4zNTFjLTI1LjU3MSAwLTQ2LjM3NyAyMC44MDUtNDYuMzc3IDQ2LjM3NyAwIDQuOTc5LjgyNyA5LjkzOCAyLjQ2IDE0Ljc1N0wyNjguNTAyIDM2OC4xM2MtOC43MDQtMTIuNTQzLTIyLjgxMi0xOS45NzktMzguMDY4LTE5Ljk3OS0xNy42NzYgMC0zMy43OTEgMTAuMTEzLTQxLjU4NiAyNS45MjRMNTEuMjExIDMwMS41MTRjLTE0LjU0LTcuNjQ2LTI1LjQyNS0zMS41OTUtMjQuMjctNTMuMzkyLjU5OC0xMS4zNzEgNC41My0yMC4xOTYgMTAuNTExLTIzLjYwNCAzLjgtMi4xNTcgOC4zNy0xLjk2OCAxMy4yMTQuNTdsLjkyLjQ4NWMzNi40NjQgMTkuMjEyIDE1NS44MjIgODIuMDc5IDE2MC44NDQgODQuNDEzIDcuNzU3IDMuNTg2IDEyLjA2OSA1LjA0MSAyNS4yNzktMS4yMjJsMjQ2LjcyMy0xMjguMzE3YzMuNjE1LTEuMzY1IDcuODMyLTQuODMgNy44MzItMTAuMDkxIDAtNy4zLTcuNTQ2LTEwLjE3Ny03LjU2OC0xMC4xNzctMTQuMDI2LTYuNzI5LTM1LjYwMS0xNi44MjctNTYuNjM5LTI2LjY3Ni00NC45NjUtMjEuMDU1LTk1LjkzMy00NC45MTktMTE4LjMxOC01Ni42MzktMTkuMzIzLTEwLjExNi0zNC44NzctMS41OS0zNy42NS4xMzVsLTUuMzkgMi42NjdDMTY1Ljk2NSAxMjkuNDgyIDMxLjE1NCAxOTYuMjQ4IDIzLjQ3OSAyMDAuOTE3IDkuNzM1IDIwOS4yOCAxLjIyNCAyMjUuOTQuMTIyIDI0Ni42MjVjLTEuNzIyIDMyLjc4OSAxNS4wMDcgNjYuOTY5IDM4LjkxNiA3OS41MTJsMTQ1LjUzNiA3NS4wNTdjMy4yNzkgMjIuNzA5IDIyLjgyNyAzOS43MTIgNDUuODYgMzkuNzEyIDI1LjMzNyAwIDQ1Ljk5Mi0yMC40MjUgNDYuMzc0LTQ1LjY3MmwxNjAuMjkyLTg2Ljg3YTQ2LjQxIDQ2LjQxIDAgMDAyOC41MjMgOS44MzVjMjUuNTcxIDAgNDYuMzc3LTIwLjgwNiA0Ni4zNzctNDYuMzc3IDAtMjUuNTcyLTIwLjgwNi00Ni4zNzctNDYuMzc3LTQ2LjM3N3oiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjwvc3ZnPg==" What is a Programming Language?

<span key="78f21454e55b4df5806d8bb65f684de4"><span offset-key="78f21454e55b4df5806d8bb65f684de4:0">A </span>**programming language**<span offset-key="78f21454e55b4df5806d8bb65f684de4:2"> is a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Formal_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="704a4eb72f7d4703b92fb725b970555f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="b9b51a206591443d88af631c2e00d97f"><span data-offset-key="b9b51a206591443d88af631c2e00d97f:0">formal language</span></span></span></a><span key="0d1a28bcdd1345b6853a50b5be0e403b"><span offset-key="0d1a28bcdd1345b6853a50b5be0e403b:0"> comprising a set of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Formal_language#Words_over_an_alphabet" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="33c59557b0c2459b95b7f55b3b56144a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="adf008b5519442d5a885e2ff8c0dc556"><span data-offset-key="adf008b5519442d5a885e2ff8c0dc556:0">strings</span></span></span></a><span key="409c149b9203409a91445e271ba4cb28"><span offset-key="409c149b9203409a91445e271ba4cb28:0"> that produce various kinds of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Machine_code" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="efb5673922cd40fa9f6b760d24692aec" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="76754df6d7c64c78b601f13144f1bbf4"><span data-offset-key="76754df6d7c64c78b601f13144f1bbf4:0">machine code output</span></span></span></a><span key="117da41715224b43a63eadda01202636"><span offset-key="117da41715224b43a63eadda01202636:0">. Programming languages are one kind of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5e0824a35a294c8584afda80d91dcb40" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="76192e3f1afb460d9573bbc3c370faa3"><span data-offset-key="76192e3f1afb460d9573bbc3c370faa3:0">computer language</span></span></span></a><span key="22f023f5a6aa44329111baae41631a01"><span offset-key="22f023f5a6aa44329111baae41631a01:0">, and are used in </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_programming" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="910fc6193a124e2f863ba90550dbfe77" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="28a5f9855f9d4e94a9f2637d31d98ae1"><span data-offset-key="28a5f9855f9d4e94a9f2637d31d98ae1:0">computer programming</span></span></span></a><span key="fd16411e46b1447b91ce388878566dfb"><span offset-key="fd16411e46b1447b91ce388878566dfb:0"> to implement </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algorithm" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="720e408c35534b1db386bf4798300c40" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="7c8f7f08191d4eef974e694860913d80"><span data-offset-key="7c8f7f08191d4eef974e694860913d80:0">algorithms</span></span></span></a><span key="3712604317e24e87b43061d6ee6e2e4c"><span offset-key="3712604317e24e87b43061d6ee6e2e4c:0">.</span></span>

<span key="edf19c4204d0463fb9f6161eae547e03"><span offset-key="edf19c4204d0463fb9f6161eae547e03:0">Most programming languages consist of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Machine_instruction" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="659581eda8694dfa98ee72610a811117" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="b3b6a2a8f7bf4488853a48f9da67addf"><span data-offset-key="b3b6a2a8f7bf4488853a48f9da67addf:0">instructions</span></span></span></a><span key="0abc18793dca43ebabd387e082334b93"><span offset-key="0abc18793dca43ebabd387e082334b93:0"> for </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="22e0192bf8fb4f20a0e74a4065855409" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="0981c9e4f4e04081932195e2e264608b"><span data-offset-key="0981c9e4f4e04081932195e2e264608b:0">computers</span></span></span></a><span key="9e15e34fc5b543f2b70c5a2ded6acc68"><span offset-key="9e15e34fc5b543f2b70c5a2ded6acc68:0">. There are programmable machines that use a set of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Domain-specific_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="eebdd0e43c374d169936085426de4be7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="55b5864ae3444ba78359e87865bd035e"><span data-offset-key="55b5864ae3444ba78359e87865bd035e:0">specific instructions</span></span></span></a><span key="293f2619061d42599a921e7fe074592f"><span offset-key="293f2619061d42599a921e7fe074592f:0">, rather than </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/General-purpose_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0f79f18e239040b58be6ceac22990c63" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="77128151d8b14753ab7746abb8e7f8ab"><span data-offset-key="77128151d8b14753ab7746abb8e7f8ab:0">general programming languages</span></span></span></a><span key="bfd55b2f34954991b8e1c3e77a105241"><span offset-key="bfd55b2f34954991b8e1c3e77a105241:0">. Since the early 1800s, programs have been used to direct the behavior of machines such as </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jacquard_loom" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f0234d6f041e40a19de2516cd75ac931" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="ed1a05dde17848919a39531c296a7ff8"><span data-offset-key="ed1a05dde17848919a39531c296a7ff8:0">Jacquard looms</span></span></span></a><span key="7c0f5dfecb3642ffb4d2a0fa2cceda29"><span offset-key="7c0f5dfecb3642ffb4d2a0fa2cceda29:0">, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Music_box" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5ccc6daf9d5e49c1920d86f804d95d7a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="f670fa47ddee47eb8cb9fd70f08412b0"><span data-offset-key="f670fa47ddee47eb8cb9fd70f08412b0:0">music boxes</span></span></span></a><span key="b8c0b1b8b8624406bb555203e22e5167"><span offset-key="b8c0b1b8b8624406bb555203e22e5167:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Player_piano" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="36f529cee8a6458ea18fec0e4999823a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="45b197a10a654671aa077b95e1241c52"><span data-offset-key="45b197a10a654671aa077b95e1241c52:0">player pianos</span></span></span></a><span key="bc5cff4ac47d48d5ae28481f4b3ad598"><span offset-key="bc5cff4ac47d48d5ae28481f4b3ad598:0">.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-1" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="61b7c244830645e4a795978f86779f6e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="602cffe005e84c11bbd77cd715b603f1"><span data-offset-key="602cffe005e84c11bbd77cd715b603f1:0">[1]</span></span></span></a><span key="c24f89d756b045b99c8427c582dba2ee"><span offset-key="c24f89d756b045b99c8427c582dba2ee:0"> The programs for these machines (such as a player piano's scrolls) did not produce different behavior in response to different inputs or conditions.</span></span>

<span key="03e06e7b9c2b4c54a237cde1fe46e318"><span offset-key="03e06e7b9c2b4c54a237cde1fe46e318:0">Thousands of different programming languages have been created, and more are being created every year. Many programming languages are written in an </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Imperative_programming" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bc87942714ed4d6cb6c2558f72e918c2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="976d8c09d5dc4d8c931be77b9fb6da1d"><span data-offset-key="976d8c09d5dc4d8c931be77b9fb6da1d:0">imperative</span></span></span></a><span key="3d7724cf885f444b9d1bbf6759cb3851"><span offset-key="3d7724cf885f444b9d1bbf6759cb3851:0"> form (i.e., as a sequence of operations to perform) while other languages use the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Declarative_programming" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="96df06941164410184c4cc9f2c1a2cdd" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="28d99172f2334e309168997bcfc4f7a4"><span data-offset-key="28d99172f2334e309168997bcfc4f7a4:0">declarative</span></span></span></a><span key="55f077ca56704f5aa8934763063ee0d3"><span offset-key="55f077ca56704f5aa8934763063ee0d3:0"> form (i.e. the desired result is specified, not how to achieve it).</span></span>

<span key="a04937eb9d644cf9863e7e5de04a8b0b"><span offset-key="a04937eb9d644cf9863e7e5de04a8b0b:0">The description of a programming language is usually split into the two components of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Syntax_(programming_languages)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="042accda934f4d2b9a0430160838e4dc" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="af7d974e2fab485eadc165cf68b421f4"><span data-offset-key="af7d974e2fab485eadc165cf68b421f4:0">syntax</span></span></span></a><span key="0eaa3c14f4fa4dd999012d4b30d9b86c"><span offset-key="0eaa3c14f4fa4dd999012d4b30d9b86c:0"> (form) and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Semantics_(computer_science)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="98086e3d0b4a478e9ef399527d9a9be4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="2d86c7af77d644edaa5900d997dc0cf7"><span data-offset-key="2d86c7af77d644edaa5900d997dc0cf7:0">semantics</span></span></span></a><span key="2adcede047284563bd57bce5a89401a3"><span offset-key="2adcede047284563bd57bce5a89401a3:0"> (meaning). Some languages are defined by a specification document (for example, the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1300033aadcf4fcaa4ad0bf05e3880ba" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="8409bcb7650b4287ae444cd2d90a5c3f"><span data-offset-key="8409bcb7650b4287ae444cd2d90a5c3f:0">C</span></span></span></a><span key="3d4d60fe05ea4e1ea28620ceeaecc2ba"><span offset-key="3d4d60fe05ea4e1ea28620ceeaecc2ba:0"> programming language is specified by an </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Organization_for_Standardization" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9bc8d9414afe4112a42c977034b62ded" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="e3914eb4fb7c46078328372ae7b88c90"><span data-offset-key="e3914eb4fb7c46078328372ae7b88c90:0">ISO</span></span></span></a><span key="78974196b3bf43dea956e848d600a233"><span offset-key="78974196b3bf43dea956e848d600a233:0"> Standard) while other languages (such as </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Perl" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a78853f293f54f6aa0569982686b3813" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="cf88e1d7bc844082a940492352f21321"><span data-offset-key="cf88e1d7bc844082a940492352f21321:0">Perl</span></span></span></a><span key="faa5249234624972a700949c85ed7814"><span offset-key="faa5249234624972a700949c85ed7814:0">) have a dominant </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language_implementation" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="198eec4feca442169eecdb3f12bdcd2f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="fff6ebb14c204128998f593d01a5b6c2"><span data-offset-key="fff6ebb14c204128998f593d01a5b6c2:0">implementation</span></span></span></a><span key="49204524ebd84a6dab8d3bdd8f5851a6"><span offset-key="49204524ebd84a6dab8d3bdd8f5851a6:0"> that is treated as a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Reference_implementation" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4cbfd71c1070457ba05f161324358749" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="7dd03787b0c64ead9625e6ffc2ef9abc"><span data-offset-key="7dd03787b0c64ead9625e6ffc2ef9abc:0">reference</span></span></span></a><span key="0a4a59842a5846318669b69dd49a377c"><span offset-key="0a4a59842a5846318669b69dd49a377c:0">. Some languages have both, with the basic language defined by a standard and extensions taken from the dominant implementation being common.</span></span>

<span key="b9276672c5cd472dafb1a9a61439b381"><span offset-key="b9276672c5cd472dafb1a9a61439b381:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language_theory" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="662c56ab1a2b4d1fa8ff260be5a6888a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="f3da46ef542a4d9ca49e1fbfb6be273b"><span data-offset-key="f3da46ef542a4d9ca49e1fbfb6be273b:0">Programming language theory</span></span></span></a><span key="c031bddd6473447789ea7ee97a60e45e"><span offset-key="c031bddd6473447789ea7ee97a60e45e:0"> is a subfield of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_science" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="aac01c06264f4a8abe9c683a2f80dc96" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="92a6443c65b44d19afc6aa04814d9d85"><span data-offset-key="92a6443c65b44d19afc6aa04814d9d85:0">computer science</span></span></span></a><span key="dd3a74e1afe94f318a7c84cc1df54975"><span offset-key="dd3a74e1afe94f318a7c84cc1df54975:0"> that deals with the design, implementation, analysis, characterization, and classification of programming languages.</span></span>

##

## 

<span key="ebe6e8bbcc454eab898a76240bdea6a7"><span offset-key="ebe6e8bbcc454eab898a76240bdea6a7:0">Definitions\[</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Programming_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="98c41a90e2d44451849186b0fba1bbb2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="e627fbc762ba43dba777933b9ee31472"><span data-offset-key="e627fbc762ba43dba777933b9ee31472:0">edit</span></span></span></a><span key="736dbcb32f7c450b80208b65bfcebb6f"><span offset-key="736dbcb32f7c450b80208b65bfcebb6f:0">\]</span></span>

<span key="c183664f270b4349980d70e03d7cb3b3"><span offset-key="c183664f270b4349980d70e03d7cb3b3:0">A programming language is a notation for writing </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_program" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="73597b4b556f4e1e98128c959ddeb69e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="1765bb49a79d432f8477477059a5f7a9"><span data-offset-key="1765bb49a79d432f8477477059a5f7a9:0">programs</span></span></span></a><span key="8a5ee13937ae4c94945c30705334d356"><span offset-key="8a5ee13937ae4c94945c30705334d356:0">, which are specifications of a computation or </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algorithm" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="125b747f38dc46e5a569c48bfa8dedda" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="0d9d31c9a98d40e5a307f60744f45d44"><span data-offset-key="0d9d31c9a98d40e5a307f60744f45d44:0">algorithm</span></span></span></a><span key="7eed497d10b24a869922872000d63132"><span offset-key="7eed497d10b24a869922872000d63132:0">.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-Aaby_2004-2" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ba6b4911677740c4ade63839d32acf58" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="c2c3612009bc4d1dae212f700e01a6fd"><span data-offset-key="c2c3612009bc4d1dae212f700e01a6fd:0">[2]</span></span></span></a><span key="719a2aff18be4f17a78f11adef321a73"><span offset-key="719a2aff18be4f17a78f11adef321a73:0"> Some authors restrict the term "programming language" to those languages that can express all possible algorithms.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-Aaby_2004-2" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8fb27136405e45288e1a674e02264ffa" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="bb3a5743dca0426cbb4f6a6f707a3cd9"><span data-offset-key="bb3a5743dca0426cbb4f6a6f707a3cd9:0">[2]</span></span></span></a><span key="fd5b03cf0cd54a1b81ef0e6dec37ba45"><span offset-key="fd5b03cf0cd54a1b81ef0e6dec37ba45:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-3" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f376b71ff8024052a7e54717de002daa" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="45ada6b1e92f45118312b95d9f8226ec"><span data-offset-key="45ada6b1e92f45118312b95d9f8226ec:0">[3]</span></span></span></a><span key="cddc361924e941da82a118e74a125834"><span offset-key="cddc361924e941da82a118e74a125834:0"> Traits often considered important for what constitutes a programming language include:Function and targetA computer programming language is a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Formal_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="354305b60eff4a8b850a500690e3fd6f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="d9b60053096f467c88dee529b790d6f4"><span data-offset-key="d9b60053096f467c88dee529b790d6f4:0">language</span></span></span></a><span key="5afed7105bea467f94a45d546c7b27d8"><span offset-key="5afed7105bea467f94a45d546c7b27d8:0"> used to write </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_program" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8b79d308e4084026b2706e0320caa2ff" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="3b80f66520b147ed838b093110e00067"><span data-offset-key="3b80f66520b147ed838b093110e00067:0">computer programs</span></span></span></a><span key="eea4949fd1b346e4aee79fba4bca519b"><span offset-key="eea4949fd1b346e4aee79fba4bca519b:0">, which involves a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="953f0b0e32554ada91b0a376c239ddce" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="722949a857d245f2981084dbb510ae62"><span data-offset-key="722949a857d245f2981084dbb510ae62:0">computer</span></span></span></a><span key="fd25f8ee94ca4ec69c263428da492b78"><span offset-key="fd25f8ee94ca4ec69c263428da492b78:0"> performing some kind of computation</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-sigplan-4" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="90d31498ed0a4fee8f6af1eb08f39b23" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="10162a191dc04e7ba15ca40b6025d556"><span data-offset-key="10162a191dc04e7ba15ca40b6025d556:0">[4]</span></span></span></a><span key="35f90f02dfb0450094ffdf940ad125fb"><span offset-key="35f90f02dfb0450094ffdf940ad125fb:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algorithm" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f55dff82418d4bdcaada5e565ec7b158" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="f288c149ed3445d4a93e067cb01527d0"><span data-offset-key="f288c149ed3445d4a93e067cb01527d0:0">algorithm</span></span></span></a><span key="4ca2364df7104dc2b875214d0338c0e7"><span offset-key="4ca2364df7104dc2b875214d0338c0e7:0"> and possibly control external devices such as </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Printer_(computing)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6de532ece7f545dda8af2b9eb8273598" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="9b569cde64ce4676b825fa487944180b"><span data-offset-key="9b569cde64ce4676b825fa487944180b:0">printers</span></span></span></a><span key="d2c12109ca0e452c8149e5fa5244f7dd"><span offset-key="d2c12109ca0e452c8149e5fa5244f7dd:0">, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Disk_drive" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bc51562f37e844e799feb6deb1bd4d21" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="67f29fff3000453d96f835c68ae8029b"><span data-offset-key="67f29fff3000453d96f835c68ae8029b:0">disk drives</span></span></span></a><span key="844c98208b3f432d94084135fcd97a93"><span offset-key="844c98208b3f432d94084135fcd97a93:0">, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robot" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c2a2bca409654427ba691fd5a0f2eb99" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="94e9d0bdd8e34da4982b044082fb38ec"><span data-offset-key="94e9d0bdd8e34da4982b044082fb38ec:0">robots</span></span></span></a><span key="af64f240791643b69ed4c60fbc3a611a"><span offset-key="af64f240791643b69ed4c60fbc3a611a:0">,</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-robots-5" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="506e2e024aae42008379cabfb60aed99" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="b8434b41ab0243068caab931f6879fdc"><span data-offset-key="b8434b41ab0243068caab931f6879fdc:0">[5]</span></span></span></a><span key="156ac67603f74dd9915c0e3db5e577db"><span offset-key="156ac67603f74dd9915c0e3db5e577db:0"> and so on. For example, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/PostScript" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4410121719e441eda793848079338c3c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="d59d15deba1d45299fd4f7427e427a74"><span data-offset-key="d59d15deba1d45299fd4f7427e427a74:0">PostScript</span></span></span></a><span key="6ae96af2a6e742cfbf03cd017ee549f5"><span offset-key="6ae96af2a6e742cfbf03cd017ee549f5:0"> programs are frequently created by another program to control a computer printer or display. More generally, a programming language may describe computation on some, possibly abstract, machine. It is generally accepted that a complete specification for a programming language includes a description, possibly idealized, of a machine or processor for that language.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-nara2-6" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="036fc82861d141cf94162b4df845f957" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="eb71296c5521409b960767ba2215fe53"><span data-offset-key="eb71296c5521409b960767ba2215fe53:0">[6]</span></span></span></a><span key="cb5cc472b3694de2b806aeff2963f3f6"><span offset-key="cb5cc472b3694de2b806aeff2963f3f6:0"> In most practical contexts, a programming language involves a computer; consequently, programming languages are usually defined and studied this way.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-7" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="dee6240d2ab74023ac110bec8e099cfa" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="1b87b5f2f4e0446b8e5e502d07901964"><span data-offset-key="1b87b5f2f4e0446b8e5e502d07901964:0">[7]</span></span></span></a><span key="9879bd324b954672a454266c65009ee3"><span offset-key="9879bd324b954672a454266c65009ee3:0"> Programming languages differ from </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Natural_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="474d6d82c93a4c2dbd2491ee036c1e39" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a950304e2bed4405b16fe5e91f9781fe"><span data-offset-key="a950304e2bed4405b16fe5e91f9781fe:0">natural languages</span></span></span></a><span key="55f1562ce8bd40578adf2f622914c8a6"><span offset-key="55f1562ce8bd40578adf2f622914c8a6:0"> in that natural languages are only used for interaction between people, while programming languages also allow humans to communicate instructions to machines.AbstractionsProgramming languages usually contain </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Abstraction_(computer_science)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d933641dbc0e4f0391c15eea67374941" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4d44582d54c74159bf919a80bf065fde"><span data-offset-key="4d44582d54c74159bf919a80bf065fde:0">abstractions</span></span></span></a><span key="16324b402237408f85824cb9555b2c6f"><span offset-key="16324b402237408f85824cb9555b2c6f:0"> for defining and manipulating </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_structure" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="cb89c9dee4794e6d8ee553a468419c1b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="19592e5ce73d453ba51befdb372fce0a"><span data-offset-key="19592e5ce73d453ba51befdb372fce0a:0">data structures</span></span></span></a><span key="71cd222141ba41b48661879b57d42614"><span offset-key="71cd222141ba41b48661879b57d42614:0"> or controlling the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Control_flow" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7d53f8dab1da448686e00ee5f4d50b3f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="76dac9b503f841d7a7e1108a29051ee2"><span data-offset-key="76dac9b503f841d7a7e1108a29051ee2:0">flow of execution</span></span></span></a><span key="1ecce21a61a04b9ebc56fb6bc8bf0f47"><span offset-key="1ecce21a61a04b9ebc56fb6bc8bf0f47:0">. The practical necessity that a programming language support adequate abstractions is expressed by the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Abstraction_principle_(programming)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="31d324120d134e8b9b4af2c489ace167" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="001be0219e94473db007e4c69aa23aca"><span data-offset-key="001be0219e94473db007e4c69aa23aca:0">abstraction principle</span></span></span></a><span key="aa2dec3f09554bdda866b9af8956a636"><span offset-key="aa2dec3f09554bdda866b9af8956a636:0">.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-8" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="11e8271f78b24452bf344717d96f3f6e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="6af365232e7741b6bce6968e04c7b10c"><span data-offset-key="6af365232e7741b6bce6968e04c7b10c:0">[8]</span></span></span></a><span key="9029543704cd4770b3467e6a3cc55568"><span offset-key="9029543704cd4770b3467e6a3cc55568:0"> This principle is sometimes formulated as a recommendation to the programmer to make proper use of such abstractions.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-9" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7abdfd04f9b743f29d78ff469e1a73be" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="0b2be6473d0a43b28c50daa04f443aab"><span data-offset-key="0b2be6473d0a43b28c50daa04f443aab:0">[9]</span></span></span></a><span key="0dee9719cbcc41e589a86e383ac1a197"><span offset-key="0dee9719cbcc41e589a86e383ac1a197:0">Expressive powerThe </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Theory_of_computation" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f49309cb45424c1aa2c644965236ae11" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="769454feabb94166a633ce78ab1c33f9"><span data-offset-key="769454feabb94166a633ce78ab1c33f9:0">theory of computation</span></span></span></a><span key="72a147e4d5374a9e95e4d2003e84f59b"><span offset-key="72a147e4d5374a9e95e4d2003e84f59b:0"> classifies languages by the computations they are capable of expressing. All </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turing_completeness" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="128a50b1fa664dd5b3be7edf74f53fac" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="ca58ebae7530434b8524a70c61bf07b8"><span data-offset-key="ca58ebae7530434b8524a70c61bf07b8:0">Turing-complete</span></span></span></a><span key="6cec30baead04adaa6ca3b8a8aa5a95e"><span offset-key="6cec30baead04adaa6ca3b8a8aa5a95e:0"> languages can implement the same set of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algorithm" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="535954f465af4cd899f5128c0e8bffdf" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="bd3fbd887f814042bff4b3dae651f59e"><span data-offset-key="bd3fbd887f814042bff4b3dae651f59e:0">algorithms</span></span></span></a><span key="b14651cce0de4a5491d6638d63a03b28"><span offset-key="b14651cce0de4a5491d6638d63a03b28:0">. </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SQL-92" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ba9a0153b11c43898e41b5a4c7f1d596" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="2d3144a8e262431eb0f6fe0c09bd61d3"><span data-offset-key="2d3144a8e262431eb0f6fe0c09bd61d3:0">ANSI/ISO SQL-92</span></span></span></a><span key="acd373f65bfa4e74ae42c3c2bab2721f"><span offset-key="acd373f65bfa4e74ae42c3c2bab2721f:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Charity_%28programming_language%29&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-offset-key="da43a6ee5e0448949611b39bb6a0392e:0">Charity</span></span></span></a><span key="0cc56e9fe9c64f3a8b509a69b11f7127"><span offset-key="0cc56e9fe9c64f3a8b509a69b11f7127:0"> are examples of languages that are not Turing complete, yet are often called programming languages.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-10" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2e158a630e5840dbbbb64444174dbf24" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="32ffca829c0c4fb18ae6605f53f49888"><span data-offset-key="32ffca829c0c4fb18ae6605f53f49888:0">[10]</span></span></span></a><span key="8e7632fd238f49c69174725c7bbba907"><span r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7c8c13ec18234e37b7f364a8368979ee" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span <span key="ccbf5f4e26fb4eef9d513ec8c8e1ec14"><span offset-key="ccbf5f4e26fb4eef9d513ec8c8e1ec14:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Markup_languages" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6f8fd59bbc0e42ecbfbb3af3bf7958ed" languages</span></span></span></a><span key="9587ff131c024f5baab94ae868dd7bf3"><span offset-key="9587ff131c024f5baab94ae868dd7bf3:0"> like </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/XML" data-key="5abef837300c45dfaaedeec6fa449b4c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="c343c5f6715840d78dec6a7f53aadc05"><span </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Troff" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a902dd815b7444ab8297ad99e1fa4181" css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="be316fd49f03461f8d332e2abb695a2e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="3668093e1ecc4370929860cbfd0aa797"><span data-offset-key="3668093e1ecc4370929860cbfd0aa797:0">structured data</span></span></span></a><span key="8eb1df93b6f0444fb96c377411c249a0"><span offset-key="8eb1df93b6f0444fb96c377411c249a0:0">, are not usually considered programming languages.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-12" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="92de11c16f52448486ddebefb5be6093" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span offset-key="cd6cf5865f1946d7be16e3c93f588feb:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-13" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="25a9e5d936a7458782f9bd23e2085bde" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="b5946aa8dc074e2898a430ca08880b9b"><span data-offset-key="b5946aa8dc074e2898a430ca08880b9b:0">[13]</span></span></span></a><span key="8ff7608e5dcb455b8188f890b767c1a7"><span offset-key="8ff7608e5dcb455b8188f890b767c1a7:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-14" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="912022ee392243c4b5f38104bae52984" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="ad132196be064fcdbd06f1be3ca48ffb"><span data-offset-key="ad132196be064fcdbd06f1be3ca48ffb:0">[14]</span></span></span></a><span key="579b55c2583a4556a1765d574b1e60c8"><span offset-key="579b55c2583a4556a1765d574b1e60c8:0"> Programming languages may, however, share the syntax with markup languages if a computational semantics is defined. </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/XSLT" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="20a7ee6ef3bc49f59356f3f9d8ba690a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="5bf982ec661e4cac81fd47a7a3c9d7d8"><span data-offset-key="5bf982ec661e4cac81fd47a7a3c9d7d8:0">XSLT</span></span></span></a><span key="ea9da2681b934ab0be590a1d54bb4999"><span offset-key="ea9da2681b934ab0be590a1d54bb4999:0">, for example, is a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turing_completeness" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="dd3292d57b0844058703c5f6048e0de7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4d8173e3206646c683c7a145c25b1548"><span data-offset-key="4d8173e3206646c683c7a145c25b1548:0">Turing complete</span></span></span></a><span key="e6c07c98fe1e42a5ac4b921b7bb34a3d"><span offset-key="e6c07c98fe1e42a5ac4b921b7bb34a3d:0"> language entirely using XML syntax.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-15" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2921f1f7456f4fe18e6d3f4196441745" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="fa6bd4815bb94fa4b92b25067d21cd98"><span data-offset-key="fa6bd4815bb94fa4b92b25067d21cd98:0">[15]</span></span></span></a><span key="3224fc8f8d334c93946588d527837b06"><span offset-key="3224fc8f8d334c93946588d527837b06:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-16" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="de463133c31b449eb60ebb133dd0c2f2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="c341ac3cf5d14a77a9933f8d5c6be67d"><span data-offset-key="c341ac3cf5d14a77a9933f8d5c6be67d:0">[16]</span></span></span></a><span key="f02348919f554ddd954bbb84118e1d72"><span offset-key="f02348919f554ddd954bbb84118e1d72:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-17" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="343293a5c75241d791694b478055de24" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="3b0f9fdaa3794d70956bba6e0ba6f148"><span data-offset-key="3b0f9fdaa3794d70956bba6e0ba6f148:0">[17]</span></span></span></a><span key="6fb56df6da2548d18bf63792b5180a34"><span offset-key="6fb56df6da2548d18bf63792b5180a34:0"> Moreover, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/LaTeX" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="35ef19bd839248548898ad3ca927a674" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="011491b8a1d84c3aa7d2019ba6431519"><span data-offset-key="011491b8a1d84c3aa7d2019ba6431519:0">LaTeX</span></span></span></a><span key="cd8f566958e0494d93e7bfe1db07095d"><span offset-key="cd8f566958e0494d93e7bfe1db07095d:0">, which is mostly used for structuring documents, also contains a Turing complete subset.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-Oetiker_et_Al.,_2017-18" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="15b3b1bc94b943e5a4903cc09f4e654a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="089d05ab05a9479598f026ba43c29254"><span data-offset-key="089d05ab05a9479598f026ba43c29254:0">[18]</span></span></span></a><span key="4bf76dd047174e9690bb070d412f2078"><span offset-key="4bf76dd047174e9690bb070d412f2078:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-19" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0e9198fcc29146ba8d0bdcb4138b5b3d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="b964ea051965475284f83f78e7ec2d96"><span data-offset-key="b964ea051965475284f83f78e7ec2d96:0">[19]</span></span></span></a><span key="ebf7c72f06f449aaa83e9c524ddb3b93"><span offset-key="ebf7c72f06f449aaa83e9c524ddb3b93:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="d3bce10be72e419b943e86e3e0e7e298"><span offset-key="d3bce10be72e419b943e86e3e0e7e298:0">The term computer language is sometimes used interchangeably with programming language.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-20" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a69243b7e310477fb7441e24161b08ac" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="99a54a42dbba4f8cb1bd7300dd1cbc55"><span data-offset-key="99a54a42dbba4f8cb1bd7300dd1cbc55:0">[20]</span></span></span></a><span key="e0ecde295bd44bafa543a50f8752b171"><span offset-key="e0ecde295bd44bafa543a50f8752b171:0"> However, the usage of both terms varies among authors, including the exact scope of each. One usage describes programming languages as a subset of computer languages.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-21" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="aaf1e482504e416b9a0619841d3d36d7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="1977b5eab4bd485aab401e70430fcbc9"><span data-offset-key="1977b5eab4bd485aab401e70430fcbc9:0">[21]</span></span></span></a><span key="93af058e22b9409e93bce07deeb29361"><span offset-key="93af058e22b9409e93bce07deeb29361:0"> Similarly, languages used in computing that have a different goal than expressing computer programs are generically designated computer languages. For instance, markup languages are sometimes referred to as computer languages to emphasize that they are not meant to be used for programming.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-22" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="36a6538796ec40b2a3f63a71e4f530b5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="0390d14148094bbeb227cd439b30bfad"><span data-offset-key="0390d14148094bbeb227cd439b30bfad:0">[22]</span></span></span></a><span key="0e495414eda844af826b828568def165"><span offset-key="0e495414eda844af826b828568def165:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="e45339bc852641669daab89d1391cd83"><span offset-key="e45339bc852641669daab89d1391cd83:0">Another usage regards programming languages as theoretical constructs for programming </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Abstract_machine" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="748bb5b0e98548909c61ad888b05a7b4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="7b46dd27eb1d4c32a68186a390a59a3e"><span data-offset-key="7b46dd27eb1d4c32a68186a390a59a3e:0">abstract machines</span></span></span></a><span key="8e211c7a8c5f4777b835e4989cca40f8"><span offset-key="8e211c7a8c5f4777b835e4989cca40f8:0">, and computer languages as the subset thereof that runs on physical computers, which have finite hardware resources.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-23" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="32fccd57263a4b84b13e9f2ef88ceba4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a42c2a5017724f929df41b649011be94"><span data-offset-key="a42c2a5017724f929df41b649011be94:0">[23]</span></span></span></a><span key="cb3e2b17fb7f4e1cbf5b4f0d73214440"><span offset-key="cb3e2b17fb7f4e1cbf5b4f0d73214440:0"> </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_C._Reynolds" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="55438c8947884ae7a8e649ee199f91da" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="3c02315e120046c98baf8acb4ce90cf1"><span data-offset-key="3c02315e120046c98baf8acb4ce90cf1:0">John C. Reynolds</span></span></span></a><span key="841417d96fbd45c19b7990ab23dd1a6f"><span offset-key="841417d96fbd45c19b7990ab23dd1a6f:0"> emphasizes that </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Formal_specification" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9e96638ccad848e5ab2859b1cb587c0f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="1697a979a19043a780cec44953f92a25"><span data-offset-key="1697a979a19043a780cec44953f92a25:0">formal specification</span></span></span></a><span key="03fcf683f9c04f31acc9a16afc213b50"><span offset-key="03fcf683f9c04f31acc9a16afc213b50:0"> languages are just as much programming languages as are the languages intended for execution. He also argues that textual and even graphical input formats that affect the behavior of a computer are programming languages, despite the fact they are commonly not Turing-complete, and remarks that ignorance of programming language concepts is the reason for many flaws in input formats.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-24" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1b9c164b4a4d45f4b06ba7e33cb48ffb" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="9c3d1b614181452aa7ad45b6bac8349c"><span data-offset-key="9c3d1b614181452aa7ad45b6bac8349c:0">[24]</span></span></span></a><span key="b92e705497e243c28f2a4a4f5a66a68d"><span offset-key="b92e705497e243c28f2a4a4f5a66a68d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="79ac336e2e24471f8f8e5fadbe910e42"><span offset-key="79ac336e2e24471f8f8e5fadbe910e42:0">History\[</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Programming_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3696083776f741d092398e3439f08fb8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="ebdddefe71ee488eb49fb44748934e84"><span data-offset-key="ebdddefe71ee488eb49fb44748934e84:0">edit</span></span></span></a><span key="b6635eea742e43a48d202d71b1566ce1"><span offset-key="b6635eea742e43a48d202d71b1566ce1:0">\]</span></span>

<span key="8d313cb2131c46e2bd891db8682b6273"><span offset-key="8d313cb2131c46e2bd891db8682b6273:0">Main article: </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/History_of_programming_languages" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d241694028ad479cb0e5cf06f825d42e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="13afa376661a4fcba25ed0e8de685326"><span data-offset-key="13afa376661a4fcba25ed0e8de685326:0">History of programming languages</span></span></span></a><span key="bdfdd952e5304456951a68989b22a0bf"><span offset-key="bdfdd952e5304456951a68989b22a0bf:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

### 

<span key="d8ddf31fef734520b8f39c5c748d93a5"><span offset-key="d8ddf31fef734520b8f39c5c748d93a5:0">Early developments\[</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Programming_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="93b6748d9f854b19bb80c8b0a01a32ca" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="6644e3c51a8b4596b6f855ef8efeef8a"><span data-offset-key="6644e3c51a8b4596b6f855ef8efeef8a:0">edit</span></span></span></a><span key="42382bbc59ca4f558ee7f95d3ebc3d57"><span offset-key="42382bbc59ca4f558ee7f95d3ebc3d57:0">\]</span></span>

<span key="ab340bc8f7294b388bb6c45790b19fc1"><span offset-key="ab340bc8f7294b388bb6c45790b19fc1:0">Very early computers, such as </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Colossus_computer" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="195d6d58bece41fc9d578a6c9a4e52b2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4ad96b3602424f20888a441683ee1403"><span data-offset-key="4ad96b3602424f20888a441683ee1403:0">Colossus</span></span></span></a><span key="fba00136f3b04bc19d138fee960786f6"><span offset-key="fba00136f3b04bc19d138fee960786f6:0">, were programmed without the help of a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stored_program" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f89b8821c4cf4b5b9c6e6072877bc9e9" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="2464e7e5746d4ac98571cb60d87dee0e"><span data-offset-key="2464e7e5746d4ac98571cb60d87dee0e:0">stored program</span></span></span></a><span key="250a453379c747bab27f9ac13bc81a72"><span offset-key="250a453379c747bab27f9ac13bc81a72:0">, by modifying their circuitry or setting banks of physical controls.</span></span>

<span key="87f9b021f1c04c0c986879ffe23f4541"><span offset-key="87f9b021f1c04c0c986879ffe23f4541:0">Slightly later, programs could be written in </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Machine_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6123b1e7f1a04db7be6de206b7db4437" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="eb1a4cefa2564afd8951e9b1cb8c0a4d"><span data-offset-key="eb1a4cefa2564afd8951e9b1cb8c0a4d:0">machine language</span></span></span></a><span key="3f4959578112446b85650bae018488bb"><span offset-key="3f4959578112446b85650bae018488bb:0">, where the programmer writes each instruction in a numeric form the hardware can execute directly. For example, the instruction to add the value in two memory locations might consist of 3 numbers: an "opcode" that selects the "add" operation, and two memory locations. The programs, in decimal or binary form, were read in from </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Punched_card" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1a662c01bebd44cc8556412524b9e1e7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="06c8b5349be64d288cdfd834e6e17750"><span data-offset-key="06c8b5349be64d288cdfd834e6e17750:0">punched cards</span></span></span></a><span key="9f3297a59e754f4fb483f1314ee66363"><span offset-key="9f3297a59e754f4fb483f1314ee66363:0">, paper tape, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Magnetic_tape_data_storage" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9aee9c18de4448eba4ba392e55492247" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="d381201f3fb6422cb4c6a7c391d4fd7c"><span data-offset-key="d381201f3fb6422cb4c6a7c391d4fd7c:0">magnetic tape</span></span></span></a><span key="542ff26bdaba4b81b3cf1724734d33dd"><span offset-key="542ff26bdaba4b81b3cf1724734d33dd:0"> or toggled in on switches on the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Front_panel" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bdee7409a676406f82fe162c0b2a044b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="37cf6530ea9c4443bff99b0280c478d7"><span data-offset-key="37cf6530ea9c4443bff99b0280c478d7:0">front panel</span></span></span></a><span key="b689bc36332f434b91d371e42ea85c67"><span offset-key="b689bc36332f434b91d371e42ea85c67:0"> of the computer. Machine languages were later termed </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First-generation_programming_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e44b439b9d0b46409decfb6bc0461ff4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a67fec87aa9e4798bee46a6367b613d4"><span data-offset-key="a67fec87aa9e4798bee46a6367b613d4:0">first-generation programming languages</span></span></span></a><span key="5601c260732e4bf09c48de78cc4f93b2"><span offset-key="5601c260732e4bf09c48de78cc4f93b2:0"> (1GL).</span></span>

<span key="5b3503fa6a74480084c8d076be4dec64"><span offset-key="5b3503fa6a74480084c8d076be4dec64:0">The next step was the development of the so-called </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Second-generation_programming_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6ecdc63801114e4d8166c135d5e20032" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="1880f050fe814f13959da0ab92afd8ef"><span data-offset-key="1880f050fe814f13959da0ab92afd8ef:0">second-generation programming languages</span></span></span></a><span key="673cb6edd1d4441db89aaea4719aaca7"><span offset-key="673cb6edd1d4441db89aaea4719aaca7:0"> (2GL) or </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Assembly_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="375ac63cd9114cf181c3afcc41fce54e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="8700a3ca8c9d4f1cb1bb4694e031a03a"><span data-offset-key="8700a3ca8c9d4f1cb1bb4694e031a03a:0">assembly languages</span></span></span></a><span key="76ffb656ff344a9dbeeaa671f2859227"><span offset-key="76ffb656ff344a9dbeeaa671f2859227:0">, which were still closely tied to the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Instruction_set_architecture" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a5fe5a20eab5481299e496ec956f140b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a6949c1251c34a779567570fcbe6e15b"><span data-offset-key="a6949c1251c34a779567570fcbe6e15b:0">instruction set architecture</span></span></span></a><span key="3655e87f5128474c823517fed3aa871d"><span offset-key="3655e87f5128474c823517fed3aa871d:0"> of the specific computer. These served to make the program much more human-readable and relieved the programmer of tedious and error-prone address calculations.</span></span>

<span key="d577a0386bfc42748ce74a687dde1a3a"><span offset-key="d577a0386bfc42748ce74a687dde1a3a:0">The first </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/High-level_programming_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6859b3a901c3456caf609de3f172e633" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="db827ee6a51241d0b68fa757a193f543"><span data-offset-key="db827ee6a51241d0b68fa757a193f543:0">high-level programming languages</span></span></span></a><span key="39cfcb6805f5470f8c6e3b5b396f9548"><span offset-key="39cfcb6805f5470f8c6e3b5b396f9548:0">, or </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Third-generation_programming_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="07ae63c93be643cfa0151897c219e53b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="624afd6b217e4ebea357f1858d623b5f"><span data-offset-key="624afd6b217e4ebea357f1858d623b5f:0">third-generation programming languages</span></span></span></a><span key="afb48c9b90da4b53b1c312e74a74a0d5"><span offset-key="afb48c9b90da4b53b1c312e74a74a0d5:0"> (3GL), were written in the 1950s. An early high-level programming language to be designed for a computer was </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Plankalk%C3%BCl" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="353ac42cbf20412c8fea1c889e296504" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="ed5f87c623724bbc8b972321a7ceaa84"><span data-offset-key="ed5f87c623724bbc8b972321a7ceaa84:0">Plankalkül</span></span></span></a><span key="b53b0b8ace5242a3a46f0d64d0910c09"><span offset-key="b53b0b8ace5242a3a46f0d64d0910c09:0">, developed for the German </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Z3_(computer)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="914c942915be40eeb715af31b6848cba" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="9f36a4952ae84c09a986bb47aad858f3"><span data-offset-key="9f36a4952ae84c09a986bb47aad858f3:0">Z3</span></span></span></a><span key="d9f08264ea1646328bf9171a05c57943"><span offset-key="d9f08264ea1646328bf9171a05c57943:0"> by </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Konrad_Zuse" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e0bef27f0c414cc299d1f81996ce61b9" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="0d00a96b673b4d36a22fc6af0dbbd68a"><span data-offset-key="0d00a96b673b4d36a22fc6af0dbbd68a:0">Konrad Zuse</span></span></span></a><span key="2d44ff1d5193481d84d7f4b7e446a8d9"><span offset-key="2d44ff1d5193481d84d7f4b7e446a8d9:0"> between 1943 and 1945. However, it was not implemented until 1998 and 2000.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-25" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="39c8f816814d444b9904e07b003d5919" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="30a6f8ccea6d476588ac7a8a21f99c74"><span data-offset-key="30a6f8ccea6d476588ac7a8a21f99c74:0">[25]</span></span></span></a><span key="9745e2419186400ab126675c459b2937"><span offset-key="9745e2419186400ab126675c459b2937:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="3226e0a023e44e4997c9bf2302d71998"><span offset-key="3226e0a023e44e4997c9bf2302d71998:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Mauchly" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3c476a27770545738bce19cb8b33d830" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="8f124b3898f84ef7a635b293155d8c89"><span data-offset-key="8f124b3898f84ef7a635b293155d8c89:0">John Mauchly</span></span></span></a><span key="6667a883380a4e1198275d87657bea02"><span offset-key="6667a883380a4e1198275d87657bea02:0">'s </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Short_Code_(computer_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c1841dd62dbe4ca19575ad183dab199d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="c2685a3701714888a95265681a283646"><span data-offset-key="c2685a3701714888a95265681a283646:0">Short Code</span></span></span></a><span key="8718019947714990a328c90422889a71"><span offset-key="8718019947714990a328c90422889a71:0">, proposed in 1949, was one of the first high-level languages ever developed for an </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Electronic_computer" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="64c3d63fb35245dba43fb6841895d430" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="1f54655a1781481695907bc4b4b9a472"><span data-offset-key="1f54655a1781481695907bc4b4b9a472:0">electronic computer</span></span></span></a><span key="1e7528bc1c054edaaa1b944d88c130c4"><span offset-key="1e7528bc1c054edaaa1b944d88c130c4:0">.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-Sebesta-26" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8e1493aed038406bb754ca7d0f0f19fa" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4a044a8295e3440abb8d0a332838b298"><span data-offset-key="4a044a8295e3440abb8d0a332838b298:0">[26]</span></span></span></a><span key="0b3b53e9ab86427e845cab5c11a29e54"><span offset-key="0b3b53e9ab86427e845cab5c11a29e54:0"> Unlike </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Machine_code" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0b3e95b6401d401a843c249bcfb9087a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="619d561ea5324adc9a93ba88033403f0"><span data-offset-key="619d561ea5324adc9a93ba88033403f0:0">machine code</span></span></span></a><span key="d5e95c3b65e54d9bb2f8e8333a1ce0cb"><span offset-key="d5e95c3b65e54d9bb2f8e8333a1ce0cb:0">, Short Code statements represented mathematical expressions in understandable form. However, the program had to be translated into machine code every time it ran, making the process much slower than running the equivalent machine code.</span></span>

<span key="253f4aa831fb4c6dbf930b095c01c0a9"><span offset-key="253f4aa831fb4c6dbf930b095c01c0a9:0">At the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/University_of_Manchester" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4251ca71078647fda04bd0988e30f374" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a215dde5755d4ac0a49f1a1acd8dc444"><span data-offset-key="a215dde5755d4ac0a49f1a1acd8dc444:0">University of Manchester</span></span></span></a><span key="e04e3ac165194a5eb451cbf0b6b8c969"><span offset-key="e04e3ac165194a5eb451cbf0b6b8c969:0">, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alick_Glennie" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4fd0afbb88c5424f86b79beac85ad152" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="dee48ceb32b8430f819a18abd8c23a1e"><span data-offset-key="dee48ceb32b8430f819a18abd8c23a1e:0">Alick Glennie</span></span></span></a><span key="4eaf8c690744491ca0f4110d244593f9"><span offset-key="4eaf8c690744491ca0f4110d244593f9:0"> developed </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Autocode" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="31ac011d02f74d79abd800aacc44a74e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="0cc6413f1e744d2b948676e4bb5af206"><span data-offset-key="0cc6413f1e744d2b948676e4bb5af206:0">Autocode</span></span></span></a><span key="50e6ddd61bbc485d8f52d43d097924e5"><span offset-key="50e6ddd61bbc485d8f52d43d097924e5:0"> in the early 1950s. As a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/High-level_programming_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="30e8cef0e3c1447d994d7f15ff04e4c3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="145a3f30a01c4e1c98a312725df1f54f"><span data-offset-key="145a3f30a01c4e1c98a312725df1f54f:0">programming language</span></span></span></a><span key="ee3ca17723f3431fb55433b13ef5885a"><span offset-key="ee3ca17723f3431fb55433b13ef5885a:0">, it used a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Compiler" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="99cafe27488942ed98d30c7c2f37bffe" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="e972f150affa49fe861a204ccf138f1a"><span data-offset-key="e972f150affa49fe861a204ccf138f1a:0">compiler</span></span></span></a><span key="b29e96144acd48b9ac01ed4e441e743e"><span offset-key="b29e96144acd48b9ac01ed4e441e743e:0"> to automatically convert the language into machine code. The first code and compiler was developed in 1952 for the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Manchester_Mark_1" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7af7b62184db46c6b8fb14b0b83d774d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="e6836951bec34ce88a0e94a0bbe249f9"><span data-offset-key="e6836951bec34ce88a0e94a0bbe249f9:0">Mark 1</span></span></span></a><span key="49783cc84b9d4e9698e2e6d08c6ab770"><span offset-key="49783cc84b9d4e9698e2e6d08c6ab770:0"> computer at the University of Manchester and is considered to be the first </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Compiler" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b6803e891cb94caebd6879d127cb6b30" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="3711d918319c4a82a4890435a58489bc"><span data-offset-key="3711d918319c4a82a4890435a58489bc:0">compiled</span></span></span></a><span key="b7623ccc07df47ecae2e99c8d35d89c0"><span offset-key="b7623ccc07df47ecae2e99c8d35d89c0:0"> high-level programming language.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-27" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d1fc8176b20d44f4b720dc6ff693275a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="cd162852154342199ffbbf3b9bbd4852"><span data-offset-key="cd162852154342199ffbbf3b9bbd4852:0">[27]</span></span></span></a><span key="721eb854e5384338a5263f81d54a0ccd"><span offset-key="721eb854e5384338a5263f81d54a0ccd:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-28" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="52424992c28644d4ae2f210a9d7b82e0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4c2ae1963ba54771b58b97846a0f0acb"><span data-offset-key="4c2ae1963ba54771b58b97846a0f0acb:0">[28]</span></span></span></a><span key="9aadc7b7a8f3472eb99b3cde6bb288f3"><span offset-key="9aadc7b7a8f3472eb99b3cde6bb288f3:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="b98ed7d1479c46c1858f14cd7f8caf00"><span offset-key="b98ed7d1479c46c1858f14cd7f8caf00:0">The second autocode was developed for the Mark 1 by </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tony_Brooker" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="39c8363c07064f049955e3ba38a7f33b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="c8087d5a14394022bc1e18aa9e426b6f"><span data-offset-key="c8087d5a14394022bc1e18aa9e426b6f:0">R. A. Brooker</span></span></span></a><span key="3f8efc81a2d1450e9dd5d71fccb1eafe"><span offset-key="3f8efc81a2d1450e9dd5d71fccb1eafe:0"> in 1954 and was called the "Mark 1 Autocode". Brooker also developed an autocode for the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ferranti_Mercury" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2b0e306a4ff9434c96ca2644a6bfd7a9" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="b986e2d5951e4b0e979bced51b4c1f20"><span data-offset-key="b986e2d5951e4b0e979bced51b4c1f20:0">Ferranti Mercury</span></span></span></a><span key="68e12b40362648018a4d9e054f420f78"><span offset-key="68e12b40362648018a4d9e054f420f78:0"> in the 1950s in conjunction with the University of Manchester. The version for the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/EDSAC" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="98019de231ee4d088106870138b30fe6" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="2b0a4fba340842bc8e0b4297d62bfd49"><span data-offset-key="2b0a4fba340842bc8e0b4297d62bfd49:0">EDSAC 2</span></span></span></a><span key="ad8dc096b899461ca203574c2ec4fd43"><span offset-key="ad8dc096b899461ca203574c2ec4fd43:0"> was devised by </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/David_Hartley_(computer_scientist)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="483080e9c7764d629481c2b793416ec8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="528e1ec6286b42398b8a1dcbc7144049"><span data-offset-key="528e1ec6286b42398b8a1dcbc7144049:0">D. F. Hartley</span></span></span></a><span key="363301f3490b482c9a6bf510b30116cd"><span offset-key="363301f3490b482c9a6bf510b30116cd:0"> of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/University_of_Cambridge_Mathematical_Laboratory" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="abcb6d9fb1b54cc4a5251d2afbf3e22e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a57c204771e34b078de3d8cc9e7d876d"><span data-offset-key="a57c204771e34b078de3d8cc9e7d876d:0">University of Cambridge Mathematical Laboratory</span></span></span></a><span key="4c5e8d9856ee4e5ebf4ed9257af13263"><span offset-key="4c5e8d9856ee4e5ebf4ed9257af13263:0"> in 1961. Known as EDSAC 2 Autocode, it was a straight development from Mercury Autocode adapted for local circumstances and was noted for its object code optimisation and source-language diagnostics which were advanced for the time. A contemporary but separate thread of development, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Atlas_Autocode" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c7779472ae5b41388b87e533b43f1190" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="003dc8e992cf4f1a865cf15438d845a9"><span data-offset-key="003dc8e992cf4f1a865cf15438d845a9:0">Atlas Autocode</span></span></span></a><span key="4feae13f10574919b751ef30c3ac34d2"><span offset-key="4feae13f10574919b751ef30c3ac34d2:0"> was developed for the University of Manchester </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Atlas_Computer_(Manchester)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="679655d2f8574766b6a077b390614408" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="91eb9af7ce5e4c4795bc2d86d55e6569"><span data-offset-key="91eb9af7ce5e4c4795bc2d86d55e6569:0">Atlas 1</span></span></span></a><span key="13c0694315fe42d8a948a2cfdf0e3c91"><span offset-key="13c0694315fe42d8a948a2cfdf0e3c91:0"> machine.</span></span>

<span key="7c7dc37b144d40f4b32bc5d824d25304"><span offset-key="7c7dc37b144d40f4b32bc5d824d25304:0">In 1954, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/FORTRAN" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ef4d9ef969f34066af452e76ef1343da" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="dae00ca039974088947f86cae0ffb09a"><span data-offset-key="dae00ca039974088947f86cae0ffb09a:0">FORTRAN</span></span></span></a><span key="3728bb5c1f80402ba5e43f2e6981d113"><span offset-key="3728bb5c1f80402ba5e43f2e6981d113:0"> was invented at IBM by </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Backus" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c62f9d6b2a384229b07415a2e8030dac" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="6b12246635ed4b7695d3b5544231caa0"><span data-offset-key="6b12246635ed4b7695d3b5544231caa0:0">John Backus</span></span></span></a><span key="77f01fb67427498daef73677592c8b23"><span offset-key="77f01fb67427498daef73677592c8b23:0">. It was the first widely used </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/High-level_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8caafeab10ad432e865b28ae000dfce3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="21acf47b19af4c4f9615b9902085e278"><span data-offset-key="21acf47b19af4c4f9615b9902085e278:0">high-level general purpose programming language</span></span></span></a><span key="6a0ef21c1d634057b11fd66708119b2c"><span offset-key="6a0ef21c1d634057b11fd66708119b2c:0"> to have a functional implementation, as opposed to just a design on paper.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-29" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8b8e84ab8ed5445c83ddb78be357c39b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="52eabea8748448c0b36a1995e6f238ee"><span data-offset-key="52eabea8748448c0b36a1995e6f238ee:0">[29]</span></span></span></a><span key="85a908da026c48a9b1131f0759844938"><span offset-key="85a908da026c48a9b1131f0759844938:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-30" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f2722035564b442f960577de25971419" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="879b047a3e6a44caabd39b0af3db3b74"><span data-offset-key="879b047a3e6a44caabd39b0af3db3b74:0">[30]</span></span></span></a><span key="3d3446c90bce4157bbe0442d8260e0de"><span offset-key="3d3446c90bce4157bbe0442d8260e0de:0"> It is still a popular language for </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/High-performance_computing" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6735c6e7d82a41aeb7ab6fc05b0a3ca6" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="665cb78235ad435ba0316df9d3aaf167"><span data-offset-key="665cb78235ad435ba0316df9d3aaf167:0">high-performance computing</span></span></span></a><span key="d10e3c5703e44b94aa55126abfcc3dad"><span offset-key="d10e3c5703e44b94aa55126abfcc3dad:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-hpc-31" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6fb4ddf4cfca4051b8cc2739ecc773e7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="ddbfcb78fc274614a6bbfc4cbb74d5c8"><span data-offset-key="ddbfcb78fc274614a6bbfc4cbb74d5c8:0">[31]</span></span></span></a><span key="952c53dd64514df1bb44366e15465c1c"><span offset-key="952c53dd64514df1bb44366e15465c1c:0"> and is used for programs that benchmark and rank the world's </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/TOP500" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="457bcc2020f14b489735682579b0b2ef" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="bc8d02e6fcaf451da4dd802bdaf54c8d"><span data-offset-key="bc8d02e6fcaf451da4dd802bdaf54c8d:0">fastest supercomputers</span></span></span></a><span key="6ff93996a0254d50a65d4c964d884ca8"><span offset-key="6ff93996a0254d50a65d4c964d884ca8:0">.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-32" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="582075a94e1f4374b7af16d73112c39a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="2904e72272684a25b887259c51abd814"><span data-offset-key="2904e72272684a25b887259c51abd814:0">[32]</span></span></span></a><span key="fb798cc679554394b15ea74105d0f608"><span offset-key="fb798cc679554394b15ea74105d0f608:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="8d96fe7170474bfdb6767c00fdc547e7"><span offset-key="8d96fe7170474bfdb6767c00fdc547e7:0">Another early programming language was devised by </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Grace_Hopper" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="84155e9102bc4a1884de024ebead8327" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="f987f34108f14deca9e87201241205a9"><span data-offset-key="f987f34108f14deca9e87201241205a9:0">Grace Hopper</span></span></span></a><span key="60c9a1410e854f46902e75defbd9376c"><span offset-key="60c9a1410e854f46902e75defbd9376c:0"> in the US, called </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/FLOW-MATIC" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c5857f4542cc4bef8eb31b8d48cacd4d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="ad02fc178b064544a485f3f6d3d22020"><span data-offset-key="ad02fc178b064544a485f3f6d3d22020:0">FLOW-MATIC</span></span></span></a><span key="e789ec5f3847440d81deb17a2d8011af"><span offset-key="e789ec5f3847440d81deb17a2d8011af:0">. It was developed for the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/UNIVAC_I" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="104a0cf6904644e6a50282cc29f69b34" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="d286628e44db46dfb414e49640d7fe71"><span data-offset-key="d286628e44db46dfb414e49640d7fe71:0">UNIVAC I</span></span></span></a><span key="a29d52b1107048d3999a8d1b5b03d047"><span offset-key="a29d52b1107048d3999a8d1b5b03d047:0"> at </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Remington_Rand" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a06ecdca580147b7a76523aff26a7ed8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="2cf82ac5bc094d5981df318500f7edfb"><span data-offset-key="2cf82ac5bc094d5981df318500f7edfb:0">Remington Rand</span></span></span></a><span key="db9b8ee2f5dc40789d5f793f0dab5a72"><span offset-key="db9b8ee2f5dc40789d5f793f0dab5a72:0"> during the period from 1955 until 1959. Hopper found that business data processing customers were uncomfortable with mathematical notation, and in early 1955, she and her team wrote a specification for an </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="32c0c91889b943d8ac47a5c3dc02941c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="f68ddffb08c04047901a47aa188b5d6e"><span
