data-offset-key="f68ddffb08c04047901a47aa188b5d6e:0">English</span></span></span></a><span key="197633e315354095b6e7d3a9f20f459b"><span offset-key="197633e315354095b6e7d3a9f20f459b:0"> programming language and implemented a prototype.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-33" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="facb3e6f14a44455a77bc3dc4efb74d0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="b198c3f06288458bb339c6212692703b"><span data-offset-key="b198c3f06288458bb339c6212692703b:0">[33]</span></span></span></a><span key="aa777021723f47f99cd7f7565da1b6fe"><span offset-key="aa777021723f47f99cd7f7565da1b6fe:0"> The FLOW-MATIC compiler became publicly available in early 1958 and was substantially complete in 1959.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-34" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="06ca5242bf8248fea99957d924168c3a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="cf62df93cedb4a61b3316a4436db6fad"><span data-offset-key="cf62df93cedb4a61b3316a4436db6fad:0">[34]</span></span></span></a><span key="b794dd652c924059b2d1faa982fd8914"><span offset-key="b794dd652c924059b2d1faa982fd8914:0"> FLOW-MATIC was a major influence in the design of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/COBOL" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6d29383443b842b7b7fe86b8956261de" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="91533a21e8f147629815cc89aa72e19d"><span data-offset-key="91533a21e8f147629815cc89aa72e19d:0">COBOL</span></span></span></a><span key="b23886a555af4104829d480cc77222cf"><span offset-key="b23886a555af4104829d480cc77222cf:0">, since only it and its direct descendant </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/AIMACO" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d7b36cb73f0a42568e3dfa634d61e1ea" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="af5e8a485ac148a9b60dc27533f61715"><span data-offset-key="af5e8a485ac148a9b60dc27533f61715:0">AIMACO</span></span></span></a><span key="6b9116fa311b45cdb0f05e0e6d9c46a5"><span offset-key="6b9116fa311b45cdb0f05e0e6d9c46a5:0"> were in actual use at the time.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-35" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="dfbf9ad1be084782bb2f62ee1539722e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="bd8172beec364f59b1bf025e0a412371"><span data-offset-key="bd8172beec364f59b1bf025e0a412371:0">[35]</span></span></span></a><span key="e88f1bf109944593894b1b6994068457"><span offset-key="e88f1bf109944593894b1b6994068457:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

### 

<span key="5641263d3e644cb5bd05bdc98118f50b"><span offset-key="5641263d3e644cb5bd05bdc98118f50b:0">Refinement\[</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Programming_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="16c2467f97424dd89f3980e7e053f797" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="18af8c956ba04606b09e97eedf1ffd2b"><span data-offset-key="18af8c956ba04606b09e97eedf1ffd2b:0">edit</span></span></span></a><span key="bb7c969b275348cbb7f7a77f2abd5e6f"><span offset-key="bb7c969b275348cbb7f7a77f2abd5e6f:0">\]</span></span>

<span key="6d4d97938fc746b38c573c293ae3be47"><span offset-key="6d4d97938fc746b38c573c293ae3be47:0">The increased use of high-level languages introduced a requirement for </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low-level_programming_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e18461ebe13d4d3e93c009ef4a32324e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="284459091a914532a365060b1ee7e054"><span data-offset-key="284459091a914532a365060b1ee7e054:0">low-level programming languages</span></span></span></a><span key="28b82c8629094fa9add71210ae8f55e6"><span offset-key="28b82c8629094fa9add71210ae8f55e6:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/System_programming_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3dea651c64b24b1fb34ff490d125d39f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="0a73d71b2f98434dbec2a56c93ca8f8d"><span data-offset-key="0a73d71b2f98434dbec2a56c93ca8f8d:0">system programming languages</span></span></span></a><span key="e8e007d6d3d3486589a3d80d6989a8ae"><span offset-key="e8e007d6d3d3486589a3d80d6989a8ae:0">. These languages, to varying degrees, provide facilities between assembly languages and high-level languages. They can be used to perform tasks that require direct access to hardware facilities but still provide higher-level control structures and error-checking.</span></span>

<span key="5e755199a7d043dfb653d787c857c052"><span offset-key="5e755199a7d043dfb653d787c857c052:0">The period from the 1960s to the late 1970s brought the development of the major language paradigms now in use:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="36631ae8258b4babae977c622639367b"><span offset-key="36631ae8258b4babae977c622639367b:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/APL_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="90eb88eb24b44fcea67dd028fc1da4b0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="d4ca3e926c0c44a7becd92a853c2bb94"><span data-offset-key="d4ca3e926c0c44a7becd92a853c2bb94:0">APL</span></span></span></a><span key="f7e62c900c5146f4a484e8f2b7018334"><span offset-key="f7e62c900c5146f4a484e8f2b7018334:0"> introduced </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Array_programming" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="300a15c32b2e42b9bcdce66246ebc165" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4fad0fcbf5c645a39c4055f6da8ab849"><span data-offset-key="4fad0fcbf5c645a39c4055f6da8ab849:0">array programming</span></span></span></a><span key="e6740d449950496da43f04d3285a39ff"><span offset-key="e6740d449950496da43f04d3285a39ff:0"> and influenced </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Functional_programming" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9c003fcfbe874df481eda44cacfa6794" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="46a2d1e2746e4adc98213013419418ba"><span data-offset-key="46a2d1e2746e4adc98213013419418ba:0">functional programming</span></span></span></a><span key="90a52b7778dd42af8b2a5d2e5ddd1d6a"><span offset-key="90a52b7778dd42af8b2a5d2e5ddd1d6a:0">.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-36" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="552a257deaa64154971ac748377aa4c6" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="2879052f557447e783dcfaca60c25dad"><span data-offset-key="2879052f557447e783dcfaca60c25dad:0">[36]</span></span></span></a><span key="b985e35231cc43a791b905d053c66951"><span offset-key="b985e35231cc43a791b905d053c66951:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="8b7a0758887b48f1b80932c04e274da8"><span offset-key="8b7a0758887b48f1b80932c04e274da8:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ALGOL" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="410de2c67dd442b793e80a192aba0dea" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="3a1fbf7227cd4dc78f312bf5ffbf5ad1"><span data-offset-key="3a1fbf7227cd4dc78f312bf5ffbf5ad1:0">ALGOL</span></span></span></a><span key="561556eb0b61434a94e9b2685e12ad35"><span offset-key="561556eb0b61434a94e9b2685e12ad35:0"> refined both structured procedural programming and the discipline of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language_specification" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9e6705a86d9a4a4a8251a745cac3e7ba" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="57879260902e4a5aae87c0d63f9105e1"><span data-offset-key="57879260902e4a5aae87c0d63f9105e1:0">language specification</span></span></span></a><span key="d1528693eb0048d6b5b70a76e2148fb4"><span offset-key="d1528693eb0048d6b5b70a76e2148fb4:0">; the "Revised Report on the Algorithmic Language </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ALGOL_60" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="09f8223f90464131bed1162283fb8dbf" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a8a1845c32bf4da2acbb957b9db3f97e"><span data-offset-key="a8a1845c32bf4da2acbb957b9db3f97e:0">ALGOL 60</span></span></span></a><span key="7995eff400ab402ebb7ec8cc9d78ff02"><span offset-key="7995eff400ab402ebb7ec8cc9d78ff02:0">" became a model for how later language specifications were written.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="3343dde8ad7345daaf1bd8eea5c4e41f"><span offset-key="3343dde8ad7345daaf1bd8eea5c4e41f:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lisp_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6e99e42c538749f7913ec113c718a1cb" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="f75b5b76a2d043fd94627d0a57db8fc2"><span data-offset-key="f75b5b76a2d043fd94627d0a57db8fc2:0">Lisp</span></span></span></a><span key="3030aa278d0146a4b8ae53452791cc14"><span offset-key="3030aa278d0146a4b8ae53452791cc14:0">, implemented in 1958, was the first dynamically typed </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Functional_programming" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4547b2f3a1384e79a871235325c42a44" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4a95bf1577de44ab940ee0de73ec96fc"><span data-offset-key="4a95bf1577de44ab940ee0de73ec96fc:0">functional programming</span></span></span></a><span key="846147bcdab9433abbe7f8958b9ed544"><span offset-key="846147bcdab9433abbe7f8958b9ed544:0"> language.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="e85c163cb5294406b43c4468637736f3"><span offset-key="e85c163cb5294406b43c4468637736f3:0">In the 1960s, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Simula" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="26019a7af52b40899f03aed87106b5a1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="e2114d75f9e24eccbf4f23f975817f1e"><span data-offset-key="e2114d75f9e24eccbf4f23f975817f1e:0">Simula</span></span></span></a><span key="a59a74d34d814f29b482286f6b03fa53"><span offset-key="a59a74d34d814f29b482286f6b03fa53:0"> was the first language designed to support </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Object-oriented_programming" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="847273db24be4d4ebf92a064d3c74f62" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="9cff3f9cbab546fda27a0af5b15ccf9f"><span data-offset-key="9cff3f9cbab546fda27a0af5b15ccf9f:0">object-oriented programming</span></span></span></a><span key="1e619c1430d0444c913745a8efe6ddda"><span offset-key="1e619c1430d0444c913745a8efe6ddda:0">; in the mid-1970s, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Smalltalk" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="058f14b3d3eb47a995aabd7ffce92cb0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="5d57c15d3d404a51a21b0629f11a3879"><span data-offset-key="5d57c15d3d404a51a21b0629f11a3879:0">Smalltalk</span></span></span></a><span key="7e9ee04a4afc465e8f7ad0c0204c7d75"><span offset-key="7e9ee04a4afc465e8f7ad0c0204c7d75:0"> followed with the first "purely" object-oriented language.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="dd132e4d5f234d7ba4a9eb33d24a9682"><span offset-key="dd132e4d5f234d7ba4a9eb33d24a9682:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f5995b166782455bb2fd71424bcae58d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="ac1837d0b7034b7fa36de1c2bb51b12a"><span data-offset-key="ac1837d0b7034b7fa36de1c2bb51b12a:0">C</span></span></span></a><span key="8dbe517c60854b3e8a2eed5d7436dcb7"><span offset-key="8dbe517c60854b3e8a2eed5d7436dcb7:0"> was developed between 1969 and 1973 as a system programming language for the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Unix" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="99dfc53869054f62bd2d71528de69c6d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="9405ec45db21475abf3cf2bb846e4858"><span data-offset-key="9405ec45db21475abf3cf2bb846e4858:0">Unix</span></span></span></a><span key="286b669de3f54013a212ef08b35b2e24"><span offset-key="286b669de3f54013a212ef08b35b2e24:0"> operating system and remains popular.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-37" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="669272fcdaba486ca02f7c9d0aad08e0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="aab56f4bcac14096acefe250835d3ffc"><span data-offset-key="aab56f4bcac14096acefe250835d3ffc:0">[37]</span></span></span></a><span key="e014337f830e42968483265b3bf56edc"><span offset-key="e014337f830e42968483265b3bf56edc:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="921d0db8cb3f40e1ba5d28bff7e9e981"><span offset-key="921d0db8cb3f40e1ba5d28bff7e9e981:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Prolog" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="601f923cd76343a19d699baa22507fb0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="231ff1886fa84391af0399edaf2605ff"><span data-offset-key="231ff1886fa84391af0399edaf2605ff:0">Prolog</span></span></span></a><span key="7f1b2e3af7574b749df782cefb7782b0"><span offset-key="7f1b2e3af7574b749df782cefb7782b0:0">, designed in 1972, was the first </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Logic_programming" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="407aad82b74448e88fc1efc870ddd95a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="3d4900765e9744e4a6ee2286523e1912"><span data-offset-key="3d4900765e9744e4a6ee2286523e1912:0">logic programming</span></span></span></a><span key="0cb6d7f5cd0a40bb88f5fc4bbba7e24d"><span offset-key="0cb6d7f5cd0a40bb88f5fc4bbba7e24d:0"> language.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSIgc3R5bGU9ImhlaWdodDoxMnB4O3ZlcnRpY2FsLWFsaWduOm1pZGRsZTt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm" />

    <span key="e866336e704e4d77a379628c0c86e220"><span offset-key="e866336e704e4d77a379628c0c86e220:0">In 1978, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ML_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="cb562896d4584207bc33f61d5d55d923" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="8ccd9f041e47471587d27bdfea79f6a1"><span data-offset-key="8ccd9f041e47471587d27bdfea79f6a1:0">ML</span></span></span></a><span key="58b7a73562ca455f9c9c32d9bfd0336a"><span offset-key="58b7a73562ca455f9c9c32d9bfd0336a:0"> built a polymorphic type system on top of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lisp_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4aaff9d3c57144b1a67cd0ec6596544b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="b5b3e59fa628407ca9c2e452e086b20e"><span data-offset-key="b5b3e59fa628407ca9c2e452e086b20e:0">Lisp</span></span></span></a><span key="eac3103e1e12479c951e71b69e91a590"><span offset-key="eac3103e1e12479c951e71b69e91a590:0">, pioneering </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_system" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9f4b7ef811fb4cce931c058b6f20f5af" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="9a8dd46ee589444b98c4ca106ed6ae7b"><span data-offset-key="9a8dd46ee589444b98c4ca106ed6ae7b:0">statically typed</span></span></span></a><span key="95d7992bbefe41b18756d4203591f868"><span offset-key="95d7992bbefe41b18756d4203591f868:0"> </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Functional_programming" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c8e3c38f2a9a43d898a1f8e832ebb8d3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="3690234323494427a050d6e57b838d10"><span data-offset-key="3690234323494427a050d6e57b838d10:0">functional programming</span></span></span></a><span key="8d8f31ecfd674642bf76839f1403106c"><span offset-key="8d8f31ecfd674642bf76839f1403106c:0"> languages.</span></span>

<span key="946da6d2c314492cbc51cbae168165cb"><span offset-key="946da6d2c314492cbc51cbae168165cb:0">Each of these languages spawned descendants, and most modern programming languages count at least one of them in their ancestry.</span></span>

<span key="30d8e53a5faf4857b31368cbbd8e9574"><span offset-key="30d8e53a5faf4857b31368cbbd8e9574:0">The 1960s and 1970s also saw considerable debate over the merits of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Structured_programming" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ed310b097d7640e4af560fefb6fcccb4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="6eef11430b764b059eeb85ecfa60e921"><span data-offset-key="6eef11430b764b059eeb85ecfa60e921:0">structured programming</span></span></span></a><span key="baf20d66dbb84539aca31d8bf5025c41"><span offset-key="baf20d66dbb84539aca31d8bf5025c41:0">, and whether programming languages should be designed to support it.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-38" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5783d91874464601b8cdae9e9c9c34b0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="9c79c690270f4b5ab44fca4c7df6e95c"><span data-offset-key="9c79c690270f4b5ab44fca4c7df6e95c:0">[38]</span></span></span></a><span key="bddd06fa8aa84612b1b03ccfcdd64713"><span offset-key="bddd06fa8aa84612b1b03ccfcdd64713:0"> </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edsger_W._Dijkstra" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b7d0176b53a14058877ee8074fee3b19" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="405b272bce0c499d8e52c7256b0128eb"><span data-offset-key="405b272bce0c499d8e52c7256b0128eb:0">Edsger Dijkstra</span></span></span></a><span key="272a7b0ed7cd4b2fa3e36e1acfe3e173"><span offset-key="272a7b0ed7cd4b2fa3e36e1acfe3e173:0">, in a famous 1968 letter published in the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Communications_of_the_ACM" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="933c4e4c1e4d4f6abd6a6d6a3ef4024e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a44452d89fad4ed38b876622fe741ef7"><span data-offset-key="a44452d89fad4ed38b876622fe741ef7:0">Communications of the ACM</span></span></span></a><span key="f7e4ba5e01eb4bc9974b44349cd5c37c"><span offset-key="f7e4ba5e01eb4bc9974b44349cd5c37c:0">, argued that </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Goto" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ce658393da184838a556c2a21fab7cfd" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="c1a783634c254d8bbe4d338cc00f557f"><span data-offset-key="c1a783634c254d8bbe4d338cc00f557f:0">Goto</span></span></span></a><span key="8ab3d4d0f07f4c788f20efdff57bb473"><span offset-key="8ab3d4d0f07f4c788f20efdff57bb473:0"> statements should be eliminated from all "higher level" programming languages.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-39" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3aa0cb5f9fe8431fb2451587c79f0825" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="45a1682f0638417f9e81089afe7bb056"><span data-offset-key="45a1682f0638417f9e81089afe7bb056:0">[39]</span></span></span></a><span key="92f2bbf07440454ebc868a3f23dfb551"><span offset-key="92f2bbf07440454ebc868a3f23dfb551:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

### 

<span key="b4ec6d65d2aa4f38b6ef19c2235707ba"><span offset-key="b4ec6d65d2aa4f38b6ef19c2235707ba:0">Consolidation and growth\[</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Programming_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1ebfb34a6f034ff8b72a84ff6ce75f3a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="6c01233bb3e84c9caec68c6eb70f203d"><span data-offset-key="6c01233bb3e84c9caec68c6eb70f203d:0">edit</span></span></span></a><span key="a24f57757ff247da848a98c4a9d05a09"><span offset-key="a24f57757ff247da848a98c4a9d05a09:0">\]</span></span>

<span key="d7de0f46e7c744ecb62de53dfa080b0d"><span offset-key="d7de0f46e7c744ecb62de53dfa080b0d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Bangalore_India_Tech_books_for_sale_IMG_5261.jpg" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8e9f018dc108456e9ca7721def2402c1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="e175d494687e4478b193238452eae332"><span data-offset-key="e175d494687e4478b193238452eae332:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><span data-slate-void="true" data-key="ea3de13caab14e81911524468b9b64b2"><span></span></span></span></a>

<span key="33cea31cc9b34f61a211ca25681d3b08"><span offset-key="33cea31cc9b34f61a211ca25681d3b08:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><span key="cc358f72bb8d4fe88dfee8528e669663"><span offset-key="cc358f72bb8d4fe88dfee8528e669663:0">A selection of textbooks that teach programming, in languages both popular and obscure. These are only a few of the thousands of programming languages and dialects that have been designed in history.</span></span>

<span key="550b87393bfa4c78a95a3fc6a012e5d5"><span offset-key="550b87393bfa4c78a95a3fc6a012e5d5:0">The 1980s were years of relative consolidation. </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C%2B%2B" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4e570ad51c624819a25f83e3c950edde" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="d777267f21984974aad8fadfe3292234"><span data-offset-key="d777267f21984974aad8fadfe3292234:0">C++</span></span></span></a><span key="4ccf1289b83b4134bf29d76bdf64ad3a"><span offset-key="4ccf1289b83b4134bf29d76bdf64ad3a:0"> combined object-oriented and systems programming. The United States government standardized </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ada_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ddf88c546a734fcbab290797e057fb60" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a57690cf61734e11877fa5c4bbec59d3"><span data-offset-key="a57690cf61734e11877fa5c4bbec59d3:0">Ada</span></span></span></a><span key="61d78a78cf254f498c53f79850a142e3"><span offset-key="61d78a78cf254f498c53f79850a142e3:0">, a systems programming language derived from </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pascal_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="78b59c4b7ec3485591e58e22c809eb26" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="e487489163684bbe98f7485b0d3e326e"><span data-offset-key="e487489163684bbe98f7485b0d3e326e:0">Pascal</span></span></span></a><span key="1d1a432491ed4ef5a240f6ee34891fe0"><span offset-key="1d1a432491ed4ef5a240f6ee34891fe0:0"> and intended for use by defense contractors. In Japan and elsewhere, vast sums were spent investigating the so-called </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fifth-generation_programming_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b56b6075ba8e4ff89bfb055d325e4b35" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="c99d7e083d2c40dfa3e4d1fd0f7c59ce"><span data-offset-key="c99d7e083d2c40dfa3e4d1fd0f7c59ce:0">"fifth-generation" languages</span></span></span></a><span key="9c263576b25c44a08b03c64be9ed5cfb"><span offset-key="9c263576b25c44a08b03c64be9ed5cfb:0"> that incorporated logic programming constructs.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-40" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="472079e7c9f0459fb95c830a77cc89ef" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="ce3b120fc75a42fdbc7a17e4d7567677"><span data-offset-key="ce3b120fc75a42fdbc7a17e4d7567677:0">[40]</span></span></span></a><span key="4f032ed1aefd4f57bab867f016198c16"><span offset-key="4f032ed1aefd4f57bab867f016198c16:0"> The functional languages community moved to standardize </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ML_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5765f53acd8342d9b89141b302f28cab" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a9eaa0964eb84b1e9a9c41e2a43959f5"><span data-offset-key="a9eaa0964eb84b1e9a9c41e2a43959f5:0">ML</span></span></span></a><span key="d158c1d4237841d0b212877cce69ae35"><span offset-key="d158c1d4237841d0b212877cce69ae35:0"> and Lisp. Rather than inventing new paradigms, all of these movements elaborated upon the ideas invented in the previous decades.</span></span>

<span key="e48724676fd34d84896f44e94e1d5d86"><span offset-key="e48724676fd34d84896f44e94e1d5d86:0">One important trend in language design for programming large-scale systems during the 1980s was an increased focus on the use of modules or large-scale organizational units of code. </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Modula-2" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6e672b8f0d4645e787c8c9efea25d807" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="7fddb4b5b1df40169ec7f0853d087dbc"><span data-offset-key="7fddb4b5b1df40169ec7f0853d087dbc:0">Modula-2</span></span></span></a><span key="a207cd1929274444ba752fe953cfeb55"><span offset-key="a207cd1929274444ba752fe953cfeb55:0">, Ada, and ML all developed notable module systems in the 1980s, which were often wedded to </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Generic_programming" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="65c0ac5dd9fa4ded80d549a879b1a922" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a5a4a1f6b726447baa6a2de908c2a1c2"><span data-offset-key="a5a4a1f6b726447baa6a2de908c2a1c2:0">generic programming</span></span></span></a><span key="32f4439a24284cf693db24b78af3f479"><span offset-key="32f4439a24284cf693db24b78af3f479:0"> constructs.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-41" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="95c584d1becd4a7393a58e096557f747" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="00fdf2c4bfe64a67a8aec39d5a0bb69e"><span data-offset-key="00fdf2c4bfe64a67a8aec39d5a0bb69e:0">[41]</span></span></span></a><span key="ea3a0827e3534201adbc25926c80f336"><span offset-key="ea3a0827e3534201adbc25926c80f336:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="052f94186c4e454cb884e79e2bfd987a"><span offset-key="052f94186c4e454cb884e79e2bfd987a:0">The rapid growth of the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b467031f173b460e882f80e22ce0ab74" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="e148243e51e94a85a57658ea4800d6bf"><span data-offset-key="e148243e51e94a85a57658ea4800d6bf:0">Internet</span></span></span></a><span key="53ce9bc99c5e4d0481423b97aced24e8"><span offset-key="53ce9bc99c5e4d0481423b97aced24e8:0"> in the mid-1990s created opportunities for new languages. </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Perl" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3f85297b7db244b8817109d1ba9bc13b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="021e53e6353640ddaea1f972d71d1d14"><span data-offset-key="021e53e6353640ddaea1f972d71d1d14:0">Perl</span></span></span></a><span key="fff0a16521cf48ce82bbcbab0318df4f"><span offset-key="fff0a16521cf48ce82bbcbab0318df4f:0">, originally a Unix scripting tool first released in 1987, became common in dynamic </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Website" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c4727f0134d046df9db062e150d0a644" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="8d51d77e578e4a54b6ba3db93dffc0f8"><span data-offset-key="8d51d77e578e4a54b6ba3db93dffc0f8:0">websites</span></span></span></a><span key="7402c59600894405a27bdf829e5e6122"><span offset-key="7402c59600894405a27bdf829e5e6122:0">. </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Java_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7d88ad529bfd448e9dde27ca020ddda1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="3685401374184de493ed4852bc8521f0"><span data-offset-key="3685401374184de493ed4852bc8521f0:0">Java</span></span></span></a><span key="b06cfae7806b43b7b21a9aaadb1e91ce"><span offset-key="b06cfae7806b43b7b21a9aaadb1e91ce:0"> came to be used for server-side programming, and bytecode virtual machines became popular again in commercial settings with their promise of "</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Write_once,_run_anywhere" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="956bded2ddb44831bb130da478707951" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="5e0baf0b25874a4daec9f63c99355770"><span data-offset-key="5e0baf0b25874a4daec9f63c99355770:0">Write once, run anywhere</span></span></span></a><span key="baeb1260db4043da8da5b92193a18426"><span offset-key="baeb1260db4043da8da5b92193a18426:0">" (</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/UCSD_Pascal" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1cd6731189d147cfa82edc822d84e6bc" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="c5fd9d2757c54c4284aafd486ded686f"><span data-offset-key="c5fd9d2757c54c4284aafd486ded686f:0">UCSD Pascal</span></span></span></a><span key="af7dd9bc984b4255bd3a8c85b412e594"><span offset-key="af7dd9bc984b4255bd3a8c85b412e594:0"> had been popular for a time in the early 1980s). These developments were not fundamentally novel; rather, they were refinements of many existing languages and paradigms (although their syntax was often based on the C family of programming languages).</span></span>

<span key="9dc6d45b65c643b9b64d34a9f09f430e"><span offset-key="9dc6d45b65c643b9b64d34a9f09f430e:0">Programming language evolution continues, in both industry and research. Current directions include security and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Reliability_verification" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b7cbfe01378544c3a86f135fac6dc4dd" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="1cc50931485d479bbab34a841a7e4814"><span data-offset-key="1cc50931485d479bbab34a841a7e4814:0">reliability verification</span></span></span></a><span key="789486ff77844b19b924fdc14fc9f32f"><span offset-key="789486ff77844b19b924fdc14fc9f32f:0">, new kinds of modularity (</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mixin" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fe2888d6dd5849e3b490926b9c5c365b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="411798dacb5e4991b9c6d8c60869ccfc"><span data-offset-key="411798dacb5e4991b9c6d8c60869ccfc:0">mixins</span></span></span></a><span key="18b21ac3118d4b5da987e4d3cb6b3d38"><span offset-key="18b21ac3118d4b5da987e4d3cb6b3d38:0">, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Delegation_(programming)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3f09da661a5146c5b0beadff0d4b6c4a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="9d54d15903b4436e9a44cc19dd3f7340"><span data-offset-key="9d54d15903b4436e9a44cc19dd3f7340:0">delegates</span></span></span></a><span key="da6148dff40e440a838d62d6f69b3ad4"><span offset-key="da6148dff40e440a838d62d6f69b3ad4:0">, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aspect-oriented_programming" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="93fdb2f488e34129a1d1ba5dfd97816a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a821c919e25e4f02945222a2bf102493"><span data-offset-key="a821c919e25e4f02945222a2bf102493:0">aspects</span></span></span></a><span key="3688fc59cbc141c0ae2b2f4de2b90672"><span offset-key="3688fc59cbc141c0ae2b2f4de2b90672:0">), and database integration such as Microsoft's </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Language_Integrated_Query" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ee942d28fbbb44358489f9314c968e62" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4f5d64f77c0f43b493c9d6b0553b03b7"><span data-offset-key="4f5d64f77c0f43b493c9d6b0553b03b7:0">LINQ</span></span></span></a><span key="eced2d5d102940569fd6dad7de8e496e"><span offset-key="eced2d5d102940569fd6dad7de8e496e:0">.</span></span>

<span key="a9263f1d11e24d10822d0c62f759db76"><span offset-key="a9263f1d11e24d10822d0c62f759db76:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fourth-generation_programming_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="87a920b4234641438a8df88c2af3ef69" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="aabf75de55ad42b483e5d52266c213b5"><span data-offset-key="aabf75de55ad42b483e5d52266c213b5:0">Fourth-generation programming languages</span></span></span></a><span key="77c5479dbc1a4547a4e21d71537ba6c5"><span offset-key="77c5479dbc1a4547a4e21d71537ba6c5:0"> (4GL) are computer programming languages that aim to provide a higher level of abstraction of the internal computer hardware details than 3GLs. </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fifth-generation_programming_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3cf8499cdad54a21b70b8b985a0ba1b3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="acadaaecfe8149a5be5aed43980ea89e"><span data-offset-key="acadaaecfe8149a5be5aed43980ea89e:0">Fifth-generation programming languages</span></span></span></a><span key="a788879dc6404ddc807c78f5433b8822"><span offset-key="a788879dc6404ddc807c78f5433b8822:0"> (5GL) are programming languages based on solving problems using constraints given to the program, rather than using an </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algorithm" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="af134769b4b64ee08855f396fc5e7104" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="578fa0f5e6f44c54a3c3329641fbb354"><span data-offset-key="578fa0f5e6f44c54a3c3329641fbb354:0">algorithm</span></span></span></a><span key="226f2ab3edc5471b805542f4171fd83e"><span offset-key="226f2ab3edc5471b805542f4171fd83e:0"> written by a programmer.</span></span>

## 

<span key="cd0fbb1a02d848439075083921676fa4"><span offset-key="cd0fbb1a02d848439075083921676fa4:0">Elements\[</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Programming_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="287dd55eac334479b5811ad81df03d0d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4184dcf018694ecaa3838dd29b6c79b9"><span data-offset-key="4184dcf018694ecaa3838dd29b6c79b9:0">edit</span></span></span></a><span key="9ec92c5e710f4e65931d45cde6ff0e34"><span offset-key="9ec92c5e710f4e65931d45cde6ff0e34:0">\]</span></span>

<span key="d4e9b7b154f94448879e5e148be8ee2c"><span offset-key="d4e9b7b154f94448879e5e148be8ee2c:0">All programming languages have some </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Language_primitive" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="50d77cbd2c5247a8ab160e7375f78896" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="e74f394d179940678cceed43f0e5cfd4"><span data-offset-key="e74f394d179940678cceed43f0e5cfd4:0">primitive</span></span></span></a><span key="7555d9b0ac004b9ba98ccd3026d5181c"><span offset-key="7555d9b0ac004b9ba98ccd3026d5181c:0"> building blocks for the description of data and the processes or transformations applied to them (like the addition of two numbers or the selection of an item from a collection). These primitives are defined by syntactic and semantic rules which describe their structure and meaning respectively.</span></span>

### 

<span key="b6551a78490e4768ba798220eadae6fe"><span offset-key="b6551a78490e4768ba798220eadae6fe:0">Syntax\[</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Programming_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c55162f4f3d049d08cdbe50bda1a2152" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="258711abd8bb40be915be3466d07dbb9"><span data-offset-key="258711abd8bb40be915be3466d07dbb9:0">edit</span></span></span></a><span key="9841e07ebf344d658ddfb2308b322566"><span offset-key="9841e07ebf344d658ddfb2308b322566:0">\]</span></span>

<span key="9cf4756ca3284c37a3f94520cde1d8a0"><span offset-key="9cf4756ca3284c37a3f94520cde1d8a0:0">Main article: </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Syntax_(programming_languages)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6159a3d4a33d4363be011cfa78c6e680" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="b65ff3c1ed8a4631b77c7d4d8c072739"><span data-offset-key="b65ff3c1ed8a4631b77c7d4d8c072739:0">Syntax (programming languages)</span></span></span></a><span key="cfe4ef63a81848e8a30e64d1dc7afbcf"><span offset-key="cfe4ef63a81848e8a30e64d1dc7afbcf:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Python_add5_parse.png" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1aa02e39460f40958ecea0408a67395d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="d9b408a5b58c41a4979587dfa3c7c04f"><span data-offset-key="d9b408a5b58c41a4979587dfa3c7c04f:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><span data-slate-void="true" data-key="54712be0287b41228c5ac84ffb1b2ff0"><span></span></span></span></a>

<span key="ea820b29a99641b5b6d8a1a7043744d9"><span offset-key="ea820b29a99641b5b6d8a1a7043744d9:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><span key="5d5134939877429eac84817cd94b39c9"><span offset-key="5d5134939877429eac84817cd94b39c9:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Parse_tree" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="264c7b8246db4b7bab0fa6c14d8990d4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="eae5a4357d5845aebbf903a59266bd31"><span data-offset-key="eae5a4357d5845aebbf903a59266bd31:0">Parse tree</span></span></span></a><span key="7bb686b8ad0e429e998166496bde23fc"><span offset-key="7bb686b8ad0e429e998166496bde23fc:0"> of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Python_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="865ff7a0c9f8499abb8ef9dcc5c79dac" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="dbae2663e95147019ea6f1cf25f9b1d9"><span data-offset-key="dbae2663e95147019ea6f1cf25f9b1d9:0">Python code</span></span></span></a><span key="985ae641ba234e06ae76fdefc2fe0b48"><span offset-key="985ae641ba234e06ae76fdefc2fe0b48:0"> with inset tokenization</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Python_add5_syntax.svg" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f3740ee94bf84d13a7cd6d451efc275f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="8cc698fb743d425690d6a1857a09c792"><span data-offset-key="8cc698fb743d425690d6a1857a09c792:0"><span data-slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><span data-slate-void="true" data-key="d08b4976df37437f8342e60aee66c0c9"><span></span></span></span></a>

<span key="1119594289cf47ddbc7e9fbe2bc0a267"><span offset-key="1119594289cf47ddbc7e9fbe2bc0a267:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><span key="d551766368b540e7b9aa3df1373e92b5"><span offset-key="d551766368b540e7b9aa3df1373e92b5:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Syntax_highlighting" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4bf8a33c4418414ebe0f7f8febea31bf" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="069a207ad026454ead99863f783f2166"><span data-offset-key="069a207ad026454ead99863f783f2166:0">Syntax highlighting</span></span></span></a><span key="5288167e7cdb4f989416722239b20584"><span offset-key="5288167e7cdb4f989416722239b20584:0"> is often used to aid programmers in recognizing elements of source code. The language above is </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Python_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="528e90628b534639977cbad76d4f3b54" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="994f8500e3434cf89712fba93a1b929b"><span data-offset-key="994f8500e3434cf89712fba93a1b929b:0">Python</span></span></span></a><span key="b0de07d658774ce5b80362205c329b73"><span offset-key="b0de07d658774ce5b80362205c329b73:0">.</span></span>

<span key="2366b305e3b141ab8094d59a7654348a"><span offset-key="2366b305e3b141ab8094d59a7654348a:0">A programming language's surface form is known as its </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Syntax_(programming_languages)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e0c7b0946d534fa4b0711a66d133fd98" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="f9dfd25f5dd147a2a7f90cd5b946ff98"><span data-offset-key="f9dfd25f5dd147a2a7f90cd5b946ff98:0">syntax</span></span></span></a><span key="b46c55f73c9a48b79224399d2be0672f"><span offset-key="b46c55f73c9a48b79224399d2be0672f:0">. Most programming languages are purely textual; they use sequences of text including words, numbers, and punctuation, much like written natural languages. On the other hand, there are some programming languages which are more </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Visual_programming_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="58f2f2feb7ac4928a440cf30d6a08a4b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="76645119b0484947bda9e82d95b4811e"><span data-offset-key="76645119b0484947bda9e82d95b4811e:0">graphical</span></span></span></a><span key="963dc9c1ab6c4ee1828a821b0325e34f"><span offset-key="963dc9c1ab6c4ee1828a821b0325e34f:0"> in nature, using visual relationships between symbols to specify a program.</span></span>

<span key="f3c3944d739043fe8d31001dbc29b9fe"><span offset-key="f3c3944d739043fe8d31001dbc29b9fe:0">The syntax of a language describes the possible combinations of symbols that form a syntactically correct program. The meaning given to a combination of symbols is handled by semantics (either </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Formal_semantics_of_programming_languages" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6eefd9b099ac4862993064c789e956cf" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="3ffb4e0c006e49a189f5161e7a5e115e"><span data-offset-key="3ffb4e0c006e49a189f5161e7a5e115e:0">formal</span></span></span></a><span key="aa8c8e1c59a149a9b86689861f0c8e93"><span offset-key="aa8c8e1c59a149a9b86689861f0c8e93:0"> or hard-coded in a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Reference_implementation_(computing)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="51a14cc16bca44a8bdc9b6aa5bdf02f7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="12ea658ebe4d4a0aafb9175f51baa7d9"><span data-offset-key="12ea658ebe4d4a0aafb9175f51baa7d9:0">reference implementation</span></span></span></a><span key="864fad5f48eb4dffa0991b9e794f1cd5"><span offset-key="864fad5f48eb4dffa0991b9e794f1cd5:0">). Since most languages are textual, this article discusses textual syntax.</span></span>

<span key="7ca0ae12506949708c56e666bdfb4b43"><span offset-key="7ca0ae12506949708c56e666bdfb4b43:0">Programming language syntax is usually defined using a combination of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Regular_expression" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2aeff372d7b14385941ee5c59226b0ed" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="b8554b18b6cb4151af9bc33f2e9a16f5"><span data-offset-key="b8554b18b6cb4151af9bc33f2e9a16f5:0">regular expressions</span></span></span></a><span key="91a33ae3a5ed4b7eb5889d88fafa6688"><span offset-key="91a33ae3a5ed4b7eb5889d88fafa6688:0"> (for </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lexical_analysis" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fc9bc6e6d6fb4b2e9230c68723899247" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="d58ba03723a34db19f8a3461adbdef4d"><span data-offset-key="d58ba03723a34db19f8a3461adbdef4d:0">lexical</span></span></span></a><span key="bc69fa288fee4192bd0252102cb58565"><span offset-key="bc69fa288fee4192bd0252102cb58565:0"> structure) and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Backus%E2%80%93Naur_form" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="82ca6ae0a298496689b19fb12f4449fe" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="271643b2560d4b9593a7b6d818979506"><span data-offset-key="271643b2560d4b9593a7b6d818979506:0">Backus–Naur form</span></span></span></a><span key="39a04b4533d74f70b7b236de889ecbba"><span offset-key="39a04b4533d74f70b7b236de889ecbba:0"> (for </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Context-free_grammar" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3b7e14c8f7d3440797b7646b2739eda2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="34a3cf25f19140d49cbfd9d152c55ddf"><span data-offset-key="34a3cf25f19140d49cbfd9d152c55ddf:0">grammatical</span></span></span></a><span key="407a07eb347f422582f7e7512eb49f4e"><span offset-key="407a07eb347f422582f7e7512eb49f4e:0"> structure). Below is a simple grammar, based on </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lisp_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1724298bd506499f8bb5bbcb70ccc26b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="15549ad443fe4adbbd2a037b5f79d699"><span data-offset-key="15549ad443fe4adbbd2a037b5f79d699:0">Lisp</span></span></span></a><span key="7723f63828d44413a64e498dc71a3815"><span offset-key="7723f63828d44413a64e498dc71a3815:0">:</span></span>

1

<span key="6a6016cdb095430f8b6eee31b872e5d1"><span offset-key="6a6016cdb095430f8b6eee31b872e5d1:0">expression ::= atom | list</span></span>

2

<span key="f09e8f6c2a354d9f9243acd3d890cc40"><span offset-key="f09e8f6c2a354d9f9243acd3d890cc40:0">atom ::= number | symbol</span></span>

3

<span key="9d342a16abb842d087b2a6050c2f24fb"><span offset-key="9d342a16abb842d087b2a6050c2f24fb:0">number ::= \[+-\]?\['0'-'9'\]+</span></span>

4

<span key="574f722a63724ec5893020fab8a93370"><span offset-key="574f722a63724ec5893020fab8a93370:0">symbol ::= \['A'-'Z''a'-'z'\].\*</span></span>

5

<span key="4e51f87611fe48b2926752039e979397"><span offset-key="4e51f87611fe48b2926752039e979397:0">list ::= '(' expression\* ')'</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMjM2MV8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjciIHN0eWxlPSJ2ZXJ0aWNhbC1hbGlnbjptaWRkbGU7d2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7" />

Copied!

<span key="8b5c39fe1fe34571837cd587e01a2ed2"><span offset-key="8b5c39fe1fe34571837cd587e01a2ed2:0">This grammar specifies the following:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="69f32539a0704749adb4782dfcbe7d12"><span offset-key="69f32539a0704749adb4782dfcbe7d12:0">an expression is either an atom or a list;</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="82f08fcb7e9c4b6085d1093578205c29"><span offset-key="82f08fcb7e9c4b6085d1093578205c29:0">an atom is either a number or a symbol;</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="7f9a970198534dafbec723c04a7152f8"><span offset-key="7f9a970198534dafbec723c04a7152f8:0">a number is an unbroken sequence of one or more decimal digits, optionally preceded by a plus or minus sign;</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="b5293046aeb64a57b28335678f6e8560"><span offset-key="b5293046aeb64a57b28335678f6e8560:0">a symbol is a letter followed by zero or more of any characters (excluding whitespace); and</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="500bcf553bc04bfc9c694437f7373869"><span offset-key="500bcf553bc04bfc9c694437f7373869:0">a list is a matched pair of parentheses, with zero or more expressions inside it.</span></span>

<span key="41967bf60b9f476abf91337eacd10c14"><span offset-key="41967bf60b9f476abf91337eacd10c14:0">The following are examples of well-formed token sequences in this grammar: </span>`12345`<span offset-key="41967bf60b9f476abf91337eacd10c14:2">, </span>`()`<span offset-key="41967bf60b9f476abf91337eacd10c14:4"> and </span>`(a b c232 (1))`<span offset-key="41967bf60b9f476abf91337eacd10c14:6">.</span></span>

<span key="03a89b6203674acf81f16d159f4de1bf"><span offset-key="03a89b6203674acf81f16d159f4de1bf:0">Not all syntactically correct programs are semantically correct. Many syntactically correct programs are nonetheless ill-formed, per the language's rules; and may (depending on the language specification and the soundness of the implementation) result in an error on translation or execution. In some cases, such programs may exhibit </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Undefined_behavior" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bb836c4425b34ceb8a49d27fb5cf6f5f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="e3d7faa99f2444f09b3fc6baebf88ecc"><span data-offset-key="e3d7faa99f2444f09b3fc6baebf88ecc:0">undefined behavior</span></span></span></a><span key="d174a0d35af64f1c99eb07fff25c885a"><span offset-key="d174a0d35af64f1c99eb07fff25c885a:0">. Even when a program is well-defined within a language, it may still have a meaning that is not intended by the person who wrote it.</span></span>

<span key="43c5e1456b2d45bd95b101dc9285d295"><span offset-key="43c5e1456b2d45bd95b101dc9285d295:0">Using </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Natural_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8d9027aceb8448dbbb7d29b061ff8fa9" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="82cddafdf4d34f72a7d3cc4fa7d6a08e"><span data-offset-key="82cddafdf4d34f72a7d3cc4fa7d6a08e:0">natural language</span></span></span></a><span key="7dfcc73573bc45a1a135e949925bd871"><span offset-key="7dfcc73573bc45a1a135e949925bd871:0"> as an example, it may not be possible to assign a meaning to a grammatically correct sentence or the sentence may be false:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="5b91422e5ca14c61909958c6a33a29e2"><span offset-key="5b91422e5ca14c61909958c6a33a29e2:0">"</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Colorless_green_ideas_sleep_furiously" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7a366b1778d54032a5b5887bf5673b45" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="787988b8fe524d6391cf7e859ff4990f"><span data-offset-key="787988b8fe524d6391cf7e859ff4990f:0">Colorless green ideas sleep furiously</span></span></span></a><span key="c09976f1afde4dbba698cd208bb7b57e"><span offset-key="c09976f1afde4dbba698cd208bb7b57e:0">." is grammatically well-formed but has no generally accepted meaning.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="74b00274157043f08f3ed0564f8b83da"><span offset-key="74b00274157043f08f3ed0564f8b83da:0">"John is a married bachelor." is grammatically </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Well-formedness" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e33f1b8fcaae461ba472c89f5fedd3a6" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="60e0fca1d12440ea831c1f81107f725e"><span data-offset-key="60e0fca1d12440ea831c1f81107f725e:0">well-formed</span></span></span></a><span key="4b966b90b25c4d17a8d9d169aed0671f"><span offset-key="4b966b90b25c4d17a8d9d169aed0671f:0"> but expresses a meaning that cannot be true.</span></span>

<span key="8be47aa280694e5eaba6860941312ec0"><span offset-key="8be47aa280694e5eaba6860941312ec0:0">The following </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7cf130ac4d164149bca67c9e0d959d50" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="d707a83e51ef431fa3c4ccf7b1249504"><span data-offset-key="d707a83e51ef431fa3c4ccf7b1249504:0">C language</span></span></span></a><span key="05d701dfe9494a6b9f7706f6b016a2f5"><span offset-key="05d701dfe9494a6b9f7706f6b016a2f5:0"> fragment is syntactically correct, but performs operations that are not semantically defined (the operation </span>`*p >> 4`<span offset-key="05d701dfe9494a6b9f7706f6b016a2f5:2"> has no meaning for a value having a complex type and </span>`p->im`<span offset-key="05d701dfe9494a6b9f7706f6b016a2f5:4"> is not defined because the value of </span>`p`<span offset-key="05d701dfe9494a6b9f7706f6b016a2f5:6"> is the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Null_pointer" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9c8e3e427cfe43e09fb71af9625dda96" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="858ce250432242988cee07a2010a0489"><span data-offset-key="858ce250432242988cee07a2010a0489:0">null pointer</span></span></span></a><span key="220696f42daf4d11bfbfdacefee15e84"><span offset-key="220696f42daf4d11bfbfdacefee15e84:0">):</span></span>

1

<span key="be83a54cad8747cca19be8223e841ff6"><span offset-key="be83a54cad8747cca19be8223e841ff6:0">complex \*p = NULL;</span></span>

2

<span key="8cb2465693e04a68a2616ec3e9b56698"><span offset-key="8cb2465693e04a68a2616ec3e9b56698:0">complex abs\_p = sqrt(\*p &gt;&gt; 4 + p->im);</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3NC0xMjM2MV8iIGNsYXNzPSJyLWg3Z2RvYiByLTEwcHR1bjcgci0xdnppOHhpIiBzdHlsZT0id2lkdGg6MTZweCI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIC41QS41LjUgMCAwMS41IDBoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNVY0aC0xVjFIMXY5aDN2MUguNWEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUtLjVWLjV6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTUgNS41YS41LjUgMCAwMS41LS41aDEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS41LjV2MTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LjVoLTEwYS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNXYtMTB6TTYgNnY5aDlWNkg2eiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="3c651c73328842d689cf4d66cbfdf5d2"><span offset-key="3c651c73328842d689cf4d66cbfdf5d2:0">If the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_declaration" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c3e8c47e753a44458bcbabfee7b35fdc" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="ab353c9466884db88cadff0d8dabb103"><span data-offset-key="ab353c9466884db88cadff0d8dabb103:0">type declaration</span></span></span></a><span key="468b0e1b50b548df9d64c6b2e3e5f1db"><span offset-key="468b0e1b50b548df9d64c6b2e3e5f1db:0"> on the first line were omitted, the program would trigger an error on undefined variable "p" during compilation. However, the program would still be syntactically correct since type declarations provide only semantic information.</span></span>

<span key="7bd911de555547a6927b3e6823e41542"><span offset-key="7bd911de555547a6927b3e6823e41542:0">The grammar needed to specify a programming language can be classified by its position in the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chomsky_hierarchy" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="afce984c044a48018e48c8a2b3b55c69" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a7ad84b586cf4070896dd9b8d2159454"><span data-offset-key="a7ad84b586cf4070896dd9b8d2159454:0">Chomsky hierarchy</span></span></span></a><span key="8671d8edfbe2442c8bea38b3aeb6ebca"><span offset-key="8671d8edfbe2442c8bea38b3aeb6ebca:0">. The syntax of most programming languages can be specified using a Type-2 grammar, i.e., they are </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Context-free_grammar" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9386efa339e54474bae387da387fd195" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="48dee5e6a86d49378b0a1112cc4da2dd"><span data-offset-key="48dee5e6a86d49378b0a1112cc4da2dd:0">context-free grammars</span></span></span></a><span key="ebeb0ea1d409440eb61a1bec5843a7bf"><span offset-key="ebeb0ea1d409440eb61a1bec5843a7bf:0">.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-42" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="408be59f94bf413e8cc7522ac597ef0c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="cf70a4068c5c496595014f8a7bffa7de"><span data-offset-key="cf70a4068c5c496595014f8a7bffa7de:0">[42]</span></span></span></a><span key="22021c2b153a42b1a13462b4aec893f6"><span offset-key="22021c2b153a42b1a13462b4aec893f6:0"> Some languages, including Perl and Lisp, contain constructs that allow execution during the parsing phase. Languages that have constructs that allow the programmer to alter the behavior of the parser make syntax analysis an </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Undecidable_problem" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c40a66fb6b23484e951eea6c007b1682" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4d3cbea014b14acb81f6c974b41bdb50"><span data-offset-key="4d3cbea014b14acb81f6c974b41bdb50:0">undecidable problem</span></span></span></a><span key="7096583fcc2a42669bcac25961b86397"><span offset-key="7096583fcc2a42669bcac25961b86397:0">, and generally blur the distinction between parsing and execution.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-43" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d01f3ab5accf4f8b8ef51ce691ee4666" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="b1c54cce64c144bb8a0d91c7d19cff4a"><span data-offset-key="b1c54cce64c144bb8a0d91c7d19cff4a:0">[43]</span></span></span></a><span key="9eb1fce436a643d3b0bf251df093799d"><span offset-key="9eb1fce436a643d3b0bf251df093799d:0"> In contrast to </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lisp_macro" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="03d2cab996c24269a8771591f9cef2fb" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="ab1d03e92d6e4b89993f9b5f8f9a3618"><span data-offset-key="ab1d03e92d6e4b89993f9b5f8f9a3618:0">Lisp's macro system</span></span></span></a><span key="c2a72a0f488645f79f02575ed083c3d3"><span offset-key="c2a72a0f488645f79f02575ed083c3d3:0"> and Perl's </span>`BEGIN`<span offset-key="c2a72a0f488645f79f02575ed083c3d3:2"> blocks, which may contain general computations, C macros are merely string replacements and do not require code execution.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-44" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="81cd58837fd045af921c5bf8cd4e78ab" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="59ca87f904b94eebbf7a2ec3f9608b6d"><span data-offset-key="59ca87f904b94eebbf7a2ec3f9608b6d:0">[44]</span></span></span></a><span key="6fc884be0a164c6896b0ddbec24ebe74"><span offset-key="6fc884be0a164c6896b0ddbec24ebe74:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

### 

<span key="58ac479ed9054be68f211cbeac5c60bd"><span offset-key="58ac479ed9054be68f211cbeac5c60bd:0">Semantics\[</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Programming_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3a3c041470884ff4a6bf1b02063c1c38" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="8466e327381b43d9b95bce81514a8cea"><span data-offset-key="8466e327381b43d9b95bce81514a8cea:0">edit</span></span></span></a><span key="151a8b93e6844e06b6a35cf351aa520f"><span offset-key="151a8b93e6844e06b6a35cf351aa520f:0">\]</span></span>

<span key="037c130c1fc94c8a94fa7dce5a972606"><span offset-key="037c130c1fc94c8a94fa7dce5a972606:0">The term </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Semantics#Computer_science" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f0d2b7d00436454e9604979f799d1200" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="6982b992d1bd4d5d93761317e4842dd1"><span data-offset-key="6982b992d1bd4d5d93761317e4842dd1:0">semantics</span></span></span></a><span key="4371629123ed4b0f9d141d3312919684"><span offset-key="4371629123ed4b0f9d141d3312919684:0"> refers to the meaning of languages, as opposed to their form (</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#Syntax" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3fbc1281798d474fb71de5262086058d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="455b342f23c64deaac600a4200b780dc"><span data-offset-key="455b342f23c64deaac600a4200b780dc:0">syntax</span></span></span></a><span key="140654068b3744f2b98e2e75840f13f9"><span offset-key="140654068b3744f2b98e2e75840f13f9:0">).</span></span>

<span key="7ecbcb6df46642c4b0706dfa70475c3a">**Static semantics\[edit\]**</span>

<span key="1095e425fcc34a418a2a395a7d90896d"><span offset-key="1095e425fcc34a418a2a395a7d90896d:0">The static semantics defines restrictions on the structure of valid texts that are hard or impossible to express in standard syntactic formalisms.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-Aaby_2004-2" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="75bd2ea4a0a4474893daad059266d553" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="2129cdaf86f7429d89c0f0a2ee0e0c02"><span data-offset-key="2129cdaf86f7429d89c0f0a2ee0e0c02:0">[2]</span></span></span></a><span key="f59bb92ef3074487bae8e4a3f848b6e8"><span offset-key="f59bb92ef3074487bae8e4a3f848b6e8:0"> For compiled languages, static semantics essentially include those semantic rules that can be checked at compile time. Examples include checking that every </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Identifier" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e94798c187b64aa5abad1ce9480be3bb" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="cfdbe4abd5094e2daa00e4ebc4e210be"><span data-offset-key="cfdbe4abd5094e2daa00e4ebc4e210be:0">identifier</span></span></span></a><span key="0dceccce15304607a239e2af6d27a6b8"><span offset-key="0dceccce15304607a239e2af6d27a6b8:0"> is declared before it is used (in languages that require such declarations) or that the labels on the arms of a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Case_statement" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="791ee46c426343c1a6efa4fb95b075ef" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="0593bd9cbfcb4163987df4e1900917d8"><span data-offset-key="0593bd9cbfcb4163987df4e1900917d8:0">case statement</span></span></span></a><span key="1fbc3e39700c414ca4bf1c59d995afc5"><span offset-key="1fbc3e39700c414ca4bf1c59d995afc5:0"> are distinct.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-45" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="547559a0ca574861b8b985016f2394fe" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="e3a2676500db44ffb91c805d01f1c33d"><span data-offset-key="e3a2676500db44ffb91c805d01f1c33d:0">[45]</span></span></span></a><span key="47094e736a3240aeb7f9268c68af7955"><span offset-key="47094e736a3240aeb7f9268c68af7955:0"> Many important restrictions of this type, like checking that identifiers are used in the appropriate context (e.g. not adding an integer to a function name), or that </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Subroutine" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e3658ea1203d471c8c3d12e372c785eb" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="680cdbb570e7423bb0adadf659a448b8"><span data-offset-key="680cdbb570e7423bb0adadf659a448b8:0">subroutine</span></span></span></a><span key="7c24e5f0542a49199291c4959280aa23"><span offset-key="7c24e5f0542a49199291c4959280aa23:0"> calls have the appropriate number and type of arguments, can be enforced by defining them as rules in a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Logic" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="99a041f295f64aec994eb7065ae72964" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="c3718e7ad35543ac8b8fce1ec639765f"><span data-offset-key="c3718e7ad35543ac8b8fce1ec639765f:0">logic</span></span></span></a><span key="abd59e34b5ec4cb98c4e62fa13222cfd"><span offset-key="abd59e34b5ec4cb98c4e62fa13222cfd:0"> called a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_system" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3ae5146d8f7540aebb81025f6ebd54b9" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="1aa82d7c0f3a4bd5a4c674aed47c138e"><span data-offset-key="1aa82d7c0f3a4bd5a4c674aed47c138e:0">type system</span></span></span></a><span key="4fba47a07a8b44f99edbd3850d0b28df"><span offset-key="4fba47a07a8b44f99edbd3850d0b28df:0">. Other forms of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Static_code_analysis" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9466a02da0864d7c8955c98b096bc5f2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="d2ac4063f1f748daa000d479145c052e"><span data-offset-key="d2ac4063f1f748daa000d479145c052e:0">static analyses</span></span></span></a><span key="45d1168cd0004f418d2cd2ce9cdc712a"><span offset-key="45d1168cd0004f418d2cd2ce9cdc712a:0"> like </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_flow_analysis" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e93b59c452db4257ad7398ac1788890f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="cae73107e9e9400f937e4472bb3cdb79"><span data-offset-key="cae73107e9e9400f937e4472bb3cdb79:0">data flow analysis</span></span></span></a><span key="119375d8eef24518aae2bc6f342881b9"><span offset-key="119375d8eef24518aae2bc6f342881b9:0"> may also be part of static semantics. Newer programming languages like </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Java_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1d111cf4fa67411b842b25ab1176de46" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="79873b842974467883b7b557d92d2592"><span data-offset-key="79873b842974467883b7b557d92d2592:0">Java</span></span></span></a><span key="6e4f7a352feb4fc3af0d9bf5b0de663e"><span offset-key="6e4f7a352feb4fc3af0d9bf5b0de663e:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C_Sharp_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="405b7891e3ac4990a297ecec3726959a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="02d7dbc0dc7a431ea80eaac6a8b39db3"><span data-offset-key="02d7dbc0dc7a431ea80eaac6a8b39db3:0">C#</span></span></span></a><span key="7452c1778d584de4a19c1a21e3d9d57d"><span offset-key="7452c1778d584de4a19c1a21e3d9d57d:0"> have </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Definite_assignment_analysis" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2fda99b441d5454b89d5ba286ce805b0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4163821a114649488764d0a8e63a8689"><span data-offset-key="4163821a114649488764d0a8e63a8689:0">definite assignment analysis</span></span></span></a><span key="53d6e6faf4034907b6d0a26d591665f4"><span offset-key="53d6e6faf4034907b6d0a26d591665f4:0">, a form of data flow analysis, as part of their static semantics.</span></span>

<span key="09a92d6153b840b69ccdc1e1eb9abe6a">**Dynamic semantics\[edit\]**</span>

<span key="bbfde78aa24a44758e5c97471c51af86"><span offset-key="bbfde78aa24a44758e5c97471c51af86:0">Main article: </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Semantics_of_programming_languages" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3bdde3c556cd4dea8b53742ac0dcc3a7" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="52e996655be24a5282ad0a8ca83064f4"><span data-offset-key="52e996655be24a5282ad0a8ca83064f4:0">Semantics of programming languages</span></span></span></a><span key="be5d98bacb0a476eaa64b769c422b040"><span offset-key="be5d98bacb0a476eaa64b769c422b040:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="1f3c5fddedf448fba9b2885597b6ef40"><span offset-key="1f3c5fddedf448fba9b2885597b6ef40:0">Once data has been specified, the machine must be instructed to perform operations on the data.
