For example, the semantics may define the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Evaluation_strategy" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3336aab30ee74bb3baead1ec449dc448" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="d7a844e60b0c4b96bd2e95d2c6660915"><span data-offset-key="d7a844e60b0c4b96bd2e95d2c6660915:0">strategy</span></span></span></a><span key="a49aae70297f4a918a1e5eb058e7602f"><span offset-key="a49aae70297f4a918a1e5eb058e7602f:0"> by which expressions are evaluated to values, or the manner in which </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Control_flow" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="866d6d313d6d4563a8219e8668445753" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="bbfd6524b70949a080b9e7242a1261ab"><span data-offset-key="bbfd6524b70949a080b9e7242a1261ab:0">control structures</span></span></span></a><span key="40ad87ad869c4b5f8108d984cb200182"><span offset-key="40ad87ad869c4b5f8108d984cb200182:0"> conditionally execute </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Statement_(computer_science)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2cdab8f11a984d639ae83aee4bd2c8f3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="acd0f862fbbd4435beac615d5816165b"><span data-offset-key="acd0f862fbbd4435beac615d5816165b:0">statements</span></span></span></a><span key="6743ada1e9114b25826f0fc7eb39b15c"><span offset-key="6743ada1e9114b25826f0fc7eb39b15c:0">. The dynamic semantics (also known as execution semantics) of a language defines how and when the various constructs of a language should produce a program behavior. There are many ways of defining execution semantics. Natural language is often used to specify the execution semantics of languages commonly used in practice. A significant amount of academic research went into </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Formal_semantics_of_programming_languages" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6a71d2763969435cb12db7602e455191" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="ce26514e38be42768725e3d4b11c0299"><span data-offset-key="ce26514e38be42768725e3d4b11c0299:0">formal semantics of programming languages</span></span></span></a><span key="09db6a033e2c4384833f052dc587aff6"><span offset-key="09db6a033e2c4384833f052dc587aff6:0">, which allow execution semantics to be specified in a formal manner. Results from this field of research have seen limited application to programming language design and implementation outside academia.</span></span>

### 

<span key="ffad9384bdb14b149ce59b2c961d1d28"><span offset-key="ffad9384bdb14b149ce59b2c961d1d28:0">Type system\[</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Programming_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d287391f68ee461eb669f13bab35ae41" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="e96a632b43654a5788c09236e11d3158"><span data-offset-key="e96a632b43654a5788c09236e11d3158:0">edit</span></span></span></a><span key="29321ea01e0943178525682cddf186bb"><span offset-key="29321ea01e0943178525682cddf186bb:0">\]</span></span>

<span key="708f4a9286b14f8abbca3c0e5a4edbbd"><span offset-key="708f4a9286b14f8abbca3c0e5a4edbbd:0">Main articles: </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_type" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1f0ab540a21b4615b97a8888eb25557c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="5dbe351089d347c58bb5e10eb7f2b011"><span data-offset-key="5dbe351089d347c58bb5e10eb7f2b011:0">Data type</span></span></span></a><span key="b2078798038240a6a4f2f8df056086f1"><span offset-key="b2078798038240a6a4f2f8df056086f1:0">, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_system" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5769c381da5c44c3a748db0e04008608" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="d693db52c34e43d5bc1f781901c761b6"><span data-offset-key="d693db52c34e43d5bc1f781901c761b6:0">Type system</span></span></span></a><span key="6186a34985e24ef38b7ee63d33984a2d"><span offset-key="6186a34985e24ef38b7ee63d33984a2d:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_safety" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a77ece36e3884a9a90280d9856716d00" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="018e5505a4cd44dd8e0932bb1603b907"><span data-offset-key="018e5505a4cd44dd8e0932bb1603b907:0">Type safety</span></span></span></a><span key="4d1d8fd4832440a185f6f536a4585a9c"><span offset-key="4d1d8fd4832440a185f6f536a4585a9c:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="8fabe96b1c204720ae884cb834e87abe"><span offset-key="8fabe96b1c204720ae884cb834e87abe:0">A type system defines how a programming language classifies values and expressions into types, how it can manipulate those types and how they interact. The goal of a type system is to verify and usually enforce a certain level of correctness in programs written in that language by detecting certain incorrect operations. Any </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Decidability_(logic)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5f968bcee2a4421cbf7607be074ae8eb" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="d35a76c07caa44868cb3a1a9033c59c0"><span data-offset-key="d35a76c07caa44868cb3a1a9033c59c0:0">decidable</span></span></span></a><span key="cd144601167242008513f1ce9da03735"><span offset-key="cd144601167242008513f1ce9da03735:0"> type system involves a trade-off: while it rejects many incorrect programs, it can also prohibit some correct, albeit unusual programs. In order to bypass this downside, a number of languages have type loopholes, usually unchecked </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_conversion#Explicit_type_conversion" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="696dc5a5d8544de9aa39b921f4ef965d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="9d7d4b04050a4806a4c2619272397fcd"><span data-offset-key="9d7d4b04050a4806a4c2619272397fcd:0">casts</span></span></span></a><span key="ba5d99fe96dd44768ef0faa3a3f48d54"><span offset-key="ba5d99fe96dd44768ef0faa3a3f48d54:0"> that may be used by the programmer to explicitly allow a normally disallowed operation between different types. In most typed languages, the type system is used only to </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_checking" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2c346571929542fca51ba229bfbfbff5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="0dd46a3ebc684b67b1917bd5a558cf08"><span data-offset-key="0dd46a3ebc684b67b1917bd5a558cf08:0">type check</span></span></span></a><span key="8a29b09bfc90462e8afab0db427c452e"><span offset-key="8a29b09bfc90462e8afab0db427c452e:0"> programs, but a number of languages, usually functional ones, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_inference" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5db84da0ddcf4a719ee6ab311fec46d3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="c66b8afbccc84d1ea91a31add3577db9"><span data-offset-key="c66b8afbccc84d1ea91a31add3577db9:0">infer types</span></span></span></a><span key="84ce8ce3760742db9900adfee7f32912"><span offset-key="84ce8ce3760742db9900adfee7f32912:0">, relieving the programmer from the need to write type annotations. The formal design and study of type systems is known as </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_theory" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="907f4226879741dcbe78ceff7af0301d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="f498cd8eb87d43e69ff8bf347d8cd77e"><span data-offset-key="f498cd8eb87d43e69ff8bf347d8cd77e:0">type theory</span></span></span></a><span key="8cb8f41504f14bc28be577043cfdc80f"><span offset-key="8cb8f41504f14bc28be577043cfdc80f:0">.</span></span>

<span key="9c2c307bddf04bd5af9304187f138250">**Typed versus untyped languages\[edit\]**</span>

<span key="3eb2bbc2bf584a01ba2c4eb2e28b7f8c"><span offset-key="3eb2bbc2bf584a01ba2c4eb2e28b7f8c:0">A language is typed if the specification of every operation defines types of data to which the operation is applicable.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-typing-46" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ffd68d624f7d4648a12398b111181b4a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="d4b23a2bcfab4ffb835d1fa9e31d626e"><span data-offset-key="d4b23a2bcfab4ffb835d1fa9e31d626e:0">[46]</span></span></span></a><span key="8de8ae92f1b54d2ea1a3d293bc2ec99f"><span offset-key="8de8ae92f1b54d2ea1a3d293bc2ec99f:0"> For example, the data represented by </span>`"this text between the quotes"`<span offset-key="8de8ae92f1b54d2ea1a3d293bc2ec99f:2"> is a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/String_literal" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b497d33ff7eb43fb8ad53413e8ecdd29" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4f614f0113e44ee7ab366eee4fcb2fb7"><span data-offset-key="4f614f0113e44ee7ab366eee4fcb2fb7:0">string</span></span></span></a><span key="263976b4514440f2a0295eaa9c3b6cc0"><span offset-key="263976b4514440f2a0295eaa9c3b6cc0:0">, and in many programming languages dividing a number by a string has no meaning and will not be executed. The invalid operation may be detected when the program is compiled ("static" type checking) and will be rejected by the compiler with a compilation error message, or it may be detected while the program is running ("dynamic" type checking), resulting in a run-time </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Exception_handling" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="230af27cf79d448d95973e53f8b4e12d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="88e052deaa44448cbb2849e4eec7e050"><span data-offset-key="88e052deaa44448cbb2849e4eec7e050:0">exception</span></span></span></a><span key="e8c7d0a177d7402c83933c72330df4e5"><span offset-key="e8c7d0a177d7402c83933c72330df4e5:0">. Many languages allow a function called an exception handler to handle this exception and, for example, always return "-1" as the result.</span></span>

<span key="7477f362b4a543d88b51fd452b579b89"><span offset-key="7477f362b4a543d88b51fd452b579b89:0">A special case of typed languages are the single-typed languages. These are often scripting or markup languages, such as </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/REXX" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="eda97a01ab5b4760b72e627e39bfed2e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="704b0f4250fd4188b7fd107099a0664a"><span data-offset-key="704b0f4250fd4188b7fd107099a0664a:0">REXX</span></span></span></a><span key="7bd76f39aeb94370a5f4f0c29310694d"><span offset-key="7bd76f39aeb94370a5f4f0c29310694d:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Standard_Generalized_Markup_Language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="abc67b76eb834ded9dd493bcf88c76ac" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="0cc58f92bf1d485196bcc45db332cdda"><span data-offset-key="0cc58f92bf1d485196bcc45db332cdda:0">SGML</span></span></span></a><span key="1f2c144699c24403bfeee22b936982d2"><span offset-key="1f2c144699c24403bfeee22b936982d2:0">, and have only one data type\[</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Accuracy_dispute#Disputed_statement" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="354be0c2a3104ffcad308c68edad1596" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="c17373a781664c9ba2c63a9a9a873d4e"><span data-offset-key="c17373a781664c9ba2c63a9a9a873d4e:0">dubious</span></span></span></a><span key="9bf4292d23df451ab9f245c16ea70dbc"><span offset-key="9bf4292d23df451ab9f245c16ea70dbc:0"> – </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Talk:Programming_language#Dubious" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0c1e54af891e4a449e41dd32c6fc315d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="3f46f5aee41e442590d8e90b2a1a402e"><span data-offset-key="3f46f5aee41e442590d8e90b2a1a402e:0">discuss</span></span></span></a><span key="dd99f18862434f119b838bf0acf58f4c"><span offset-key="dd99f18862434f119b838bf0acf58f4c:0">\]–—most commonly character strings which are used for both symbolic and numeric data.</span></span>

<span key="62fd0d32122c470188989423e20e9bcd"><span offset-key="62fd0d32122c470188989423e20e9bcd:0">In contrast, an untyped language, such as most </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Assembly_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f629f21350ff45ae825afb435e425016" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="95fe4d3a48ec41ffb632cb5eb873c3ae"><span data-offset-key="95fe4d3a48ec41ffb632cb5eb873c3ae:0">assembly languages</span></span></span></a><span key="b294bf728c9041a2ab2948338b72ec18"><span offset-key="b294bf728c9041a2ab2948338b72ec18:0">, allows any operation to be performed on any data, generally sequences of bits of various lengths.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-typing-46" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b0d2d598051b4d089e25807be7af0d78" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="7fe21d05284d4f31bc9a4ce365692bfc"><span data-offset-key="7fe21d05284d4f31bc9a4ce365692bfc:0">[46]</span></span></span></a><span key="792f615ac574400889155b36118ab374"><span offset-key="792f615ac574400889155b36118ab374:0"> High-level untyped languages include </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/BCPL" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="09fe55b01936481c9551875b7f5f1eeb" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="0a220d7e9e4b4b8ab1e8ce9e93ef133a"><span data-offset-key="0a220d7e9e4b4b8ab1e8ce9e93ef133a:0">BCPL</span></span></span></a><span key="e83a283a792d4df0a3e68dd61e3507fb"><span offset-key="e83a283a792d4df0a3e68dd61e3507fb:0">, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tcl" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3ee697b0e387433fb796479e0a5ccbbb" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="893696ed3b4247769fb009eb001c6c6e"><span data-offset-key="893696ed3b4247769fb009eb001c6c6e:0">Tcl</span></span></span></a><span key="a387d520642441aeb0d0f053a7aabc26"><span offset-key="a387d520642441aeb0d0f053a7aabc26:0">, and some varieties of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Forth_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7058a9d78bd54c28a62facda5b6583e0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="5534aa1487c54bf9ac6147bf932c6213"><span data-offset-key="5534aa1487c54bf9ac6147bf932c6213:0">Forth</span></span></span></a><span key="56941217d4f54ae690eedfca7d3c0e52"><span offset-key="56941217d4f54ae690eedfca7d3c0e52:0">.</span></span>

<span key="efca49d6d3da4086a327803ffb3eb54e"><span offset-key="efca49d6d3da4086a327803ffb3eb54e:0">In practice, while few languages are considered typed from the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_theory" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="dd535b9dce1e447ab4b6785a78e764a9" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="fc0e574728264eff84e8c76964ce20ac"><span data-offset-key="fc0e574728264eff84e8c76964ce20ac:0">type theory</span></span></span></a><span key="f6de788b63cf4052a17586e621578fa0"><span offset-key="f6de788b63cf4052a17586e621578fa0:0"> (verifying or rejecting all operations), most modern languages offer a degree of typing.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-typing-46" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="702b20f0f96c449ba2314b3b8b635f84" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="251975f8f68e4edd8507ba19aae50c94"><span data-offset-key="251975f8f68e4edd8507ba19aae50c94:0">[46]</span></span></span></a><span key="afca5a78f47a4cd3ac0981e92218877b"><span offset-key="afca5a78f47a4cd3ac0981e92218877b:0"> Many production languages provide means to bypass or subvert the type system, trading type-safety for finer control over the program's execution (see </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_conversion#Explicit_type_conversion" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="af81346c79534005b346709b473809ba" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="2caf442202ca427fb2a0edb840a056da"><span data-offset-key="2caf442202ca427fb2a0edb840a056da:0">casting</span></span></span></a><span key="7be894fff3964290967db632163c516e"><span offset-key="7be894fff3964290967db632163c516e:0">).</span></span>

<span key="5b71437ba2804250b5b53babf9ddb6ca">**Static versus dynamic typing\[edit\]**</span>

<span key="89832450439e4a2badb46c166c2f9bc5"><span offset-key="89832450439e4a2badb46c166c2f9bc5:0">In </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_system" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="91d0e9fd3f7b42229c29b90474cfca22" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="f5f993591265408298acd39574b9818f"><span data-offset-key="f5f993591265408298acd39574b9818f:0">static typing</span></span></span></a><span key="7e91fcae53444bf58dda023901dd4f07"><span offset-key="7e91fcae53444bf58dda023901dd4f07:0">, all expressions have their types determined prior to when the program is executed, typically at compile-time. For example, 1 and (2+2) are integer expressions; they cannot be passed to a function that expects a string, or stored in a variable that is defined to hold dates.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-typing-46" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3de2731ac05948dbbf7ad0e5ae394fc3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a1e5c3d66e3d4e3d921419bb6e5939b8"><span data-offset-key="a1e5c3d66e3d4e3d921419bb6e5939b8:0">[46]</span></span></span></a><span key="8d2b3efddf5140bd84d9a94024264879"><span offset-key="8d2b3efddf5140bd84d9a94024264879:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="6d5933c9df7a49d38f433eeca0b66b42"><span offset-key="6d5933c9df7a49d38f433eeca0b66b42:0">Statically typed languages can be either </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Manifest_typing" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b3ca0d93e9f34ebebf5cdb25dbbf68a8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="d93c208e9622423ab60387f5ab8473c5"><span data-offset-key="d93c208e9622423ab60387f5ab8473c5:0">manifestly typed</span></span></span></a><span key="461c9ca42c3f42db842a05a45c0ef79b"><span offset-key="461c9ca42c3f42db842a05a45c0ef79b:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_inference" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a306747dc21c4cf7beea34f6aab88ac3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="3ce04d7e34284e798627e4d3321d4bc9"><span data-offset-key="3ce04d7e34284e798627e4d3321d4bc9:0">type-inferred</span></span></span></a><span key="071a462d81e4426c9a70adcdf50c45f9"><span offset-key="071a462d81e4426c9a70adcdf50c45f9:0">. In the first case, the programmer must explicitly write types at certain textual positions (for example, at variable </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Declaration_(computer_science)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="28fb6b2197a54f2ca24c72cf36585dea" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="1c3de62a9adf44ba982b0b215be4bee5"><span data-offset-key="1c3de62a9adf44ba982b0b215be4bee5:0">declarations</span></span></span></a><span key="af2ddbfb6a8e441d91dcafc6699bb474"><span offset-key="af2ddbfb6a8e441d91dcafc6699bb474:0">). In the second case, the compiler infers the types of expressions and declarations based on context. Most mainstream statically typed languages, such as </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C%2B%2B" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5c2c5ffb55164dad921e8cdcee8484a6" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="174db8bd48f44f45af4d4c112baef011"><span data-offset-key="174db8bd48f44f45af4d4c112baef011:0">C++</span></span></span></a><span key="c099c389f8924fadac5bbcd76a8cbe89"><span offset-key="c099c389f8924fadac5bbcd76a8cbe89:0">, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C_Sharp_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1fff9c9ec09f4e06808afe79bc86be62" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4aaf718aa0a94b0e8de581cad003b55e"><span data-offset-key="4aaf718aa0a94b0e8de581cad003b55e:0">C#</span></span></span></a><span key="d9be48bc4b6445279b0bdcdc81892396"><span offset-key="d9be48bc4b6445279b0bdcdc81892396:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Java_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b9ff926d50c84bef884348644ced23ff" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a60c80ac36bf4271a5a0443dc25a9504"><span data-offset-key="a60c80ac36bf4271a5a0443dc25a9504:0">Java</span></span></span></a><span key="8317c80fa6164dcf83c92d3e08610a1f"><span offset-key="8317c80fa6164dcf83c92d3e08610a1f:0">, are manifestly typed. Complete type inference has traditionally been associated with less mainstream languages, such as </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Haskell_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="66800474924447fbb589a44fa3626413" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a2733e00385c450a907b9f2b98c9fedc"><span data-offset-key="a2733e00385c450a907b9f2b98c9fedc:0">Haskell</span></span></span></a><span key="8a16d9789d7444528045fd0005eff0ed"><span offset-key="8a16d9789d7444528045fd0005eff0ed:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ML_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3c6bcdfa03b1418092098320d6aa6a3e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="c172400644184e0f81599e6a14661c1e"><span data-offset-key="c172400644184e0f81599e6a14661c1e:0">ML</span></span></span></a><span key="b325bd63525043efbcef67d390c3c81d"><span offset-key="b325bd63525043efbcef67d390c3c81d:0">. However, many manifestly typed languages support partial type inference; for example, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C%2B%2B" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="39bac31d23384d5dbda45e60c09fdfb1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="bcf897da80624b26a71c9d0ebba96470"><span data-offset-key="bcf897da80624b26a71c9d0ebba96470:0">C++</span></span></span></a><span key="09732d44d69948ea9539eac5cadb5e48"><span offset-key="09732d44d69948ea9539eac5cadb5e48:0">, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Java_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="06205366a836417a886e86f5471756ce" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="9d5ac66db8874fb1897f14551b3c9ab1"><span data-offset-key="9d5ac66db8874fb1897f14551b3c9ab1:0">Java</span></span></span></a><span key="c6d69015e9fd4687b68406f812c20479"><span offset-key="c6d69015e9fd4687b68406f812c20479:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C_Sharp_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7bc6f96f9f0b4a52af405a229bd02614" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="2ba9d0aa1b824817b9f008194f000f6e"><span data-offset-key="2ba9d0aa1b824817b9f008194f000f6e:0">C#</span></span></span></a><span key="26b7dbbb09a341959a86bf4591e6fedf"><span offset-key="26b7dbbb09a341959a86bf4591e6fedf:0"> all infer types in certain limited cases.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-47" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="56ab50d854874075b4bb60324b0c792f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="be923957ac6c481d8453c433da597578"><span data-offset-key="be923957ac6c481d8453c433da597578:0">[47]</span></span></span></a><span key="943c1ed5d2e74cd4a80b7700650d6da5"><span offset-key="943c1ed5d2e74cd4a80b7700650d6da5:0"> Additionally, some programming languages allow for some types to be automatically converted to other types; for example, an int can be used where the program expects a float.</span></span>

<span key="ad5f844c86334d9cbba29524874bd551"><span offset-key="ad5f844c86334d9cbba29524874bd551:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_system" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2507ae14279f4c4e907b1706bcf2b648" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="5a5358a339ae435280553f3aa7196a6c"><span data-offset-key="5a5358a339ae435280553f3aa7196a6c:0">Dynamic typing</span></span></span></a><span key="abb42c171e1148959a763750e02b4708"><span offset-key="abb42c171e1148959a763750e02b4708:0">, also called latent typing, determines the type-safety of operations at run time; in other words, types are associated with run-time values rather than textual expressions.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-typing-46" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="dddb5c946de9467ebe11de29e396f4be" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="9a5b2b9898014836800b4306653297bb"><span data-offset-key="9a5b2b9898014836800b4306653297bb:0">[46]</span></span></span></a><span key="c434f377b936429e85a9ddbddc88ac01"><span offset-key="c434f377b936429e85a9ddbddc88ac01:0"> As with type-inferred languages, dynamically typed languages do not require the programmer to write explicit type annotations on expressions. Among other things, this may permit a single variable to refer to values of different types at different points in the program execution. However, type </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Software_bug" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ff338e377d5a484c81e7d4d62448f57d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="806fb2a7f6d84cd48eb64754b1da076f"><span data-offset-key="806fb2a7f6d84cd48eb64754b1da076f:0">errors</span></span></span></a><span key="a617e5ecdacb47909f1d1adf7a03363f"><span offset-key="a617e5ecdacb47909f1d1adf7a03363f:0"> cannot be automatically detected until a piece of code is actually executed, potentially making </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Debugging" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="cf5ba9313f364d8f99577344082102c3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="099d248ab7744c9aa6bc56e9a8717b00"><span data-offset-key="099d248ab7744c9aa6bc56e9a8717b00:0">debugging</span></span></span></a><span key="ee850fb0e4c54f408b35f73e9576c9f7"><span offset-key="ee850fb0e4c54f408b35f73e9576c9f7:0"> more difficult. </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lisp_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="30041a477268440b87b2a83aa25f2709" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="5abce34c456f4d12b974729a4f4aaab5"><span data-offset-key="5abce34c456f4d12b974729a4f4aaab5:0">Lisp</span></span></span></a><span key="bf9df16aeb9448288bece2b9f760c4f6"><span offset-key="bf9df16aeb9448288bece2b9f760c4f6:0">, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Smalltalk" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e7b66cda56ef444b97675b7f4aaa01fc" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a1c30c7f23a143459f66cb9313da5429"><span data-offset-key="a1c30c7f23a143459f66cb9313da5429:0">Smalltalk</span></span></span></a><span key="73632e7ff9544a4a9ff9c4d02e14353d"><span offset-key="73632e7ff9544a4a9ff9c4d02e14353d:0">, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Perl" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a844686eda0c4431be6c8f4af286da4c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="e5fbc519f7b7497d9b0ddd233115959e"><span data-offset-key="e5fbc519f7b7497d9b0ddd233115959e:0">Perl</span></span></span></a><span key="d03b2102154340f4ae6b1c55e6266f84"><span offset-key="d03b2102154340f4ae6b1c55e6266f84:0">, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Python_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="838f3d2ef5294e3aa0bfa17aa7a6b632" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="2b31460b968640dfbf652be733c5f14a"><span data-offset-key="2b31460b968640dfbf652be733c5f14a:0">Python</span></span></span></a><span key="0abfc94b0d2c4dab84c6cf1d2f3fab35"><span offset-key="0abfc94b0d2c4dab84c6cf1d2f3fab35:0">, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/JavaScript" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bd91de71e2b5456885fbb1eeadd7c738" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="6bcdd59b868a4599a650b1c92893a1c6"><span data-offset-key="6bcdd59b868a4599a650b1c92893a1c6:0">JavaScript</span></span></span></a><span key="f27609d6aa3b4b3ea8a40bc6c2329d31"><span offset-key="f27609d6aa3b4b3ea8a40bc6c2329d31:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ruby_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f65185608a124d63a98b7deefccdce14" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="206d827b5b1045b18bd31c7d9324017b"><span data-offset-key="206d827b5b1045b18bd31c7d9324017b:0">Ruby</span></span></span></a><span key="c69ef8c65d254d91bb8c89338042b811"><span offset-key="c69ef8c65d254d91bb8c89338042b811:0"> are all examples of dynamically typed languages.</span></span>

<span key="fc6ab45dc4f649a084aedb73c857b3dc">**Weak and strong typing\[edit\]**</span>

<span key="d65afb93f58c49eba4c61d1811c820dc"><span offset-key="d65afb93f58c49eba4c61d1811c820dc:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Weak_typing" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="961b7dba90904e81bf1402f4cc4ebff4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="c3bbc972cf2e4e50b3e61abdf8a9fd52"><span data-offset-key="c3bbc972cf2e4e50b3e61abdf8a9fd52:0">Weak typing</span></span></span></a><span key="2d94aa4b37384e3ebe8608e47808d878"><span offset-key="2d94aa4b37384e3ebe8608e47808d878:0"> allows a value of one type to be treated as another, for example treating a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/String_(computer_science)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="cd0718da19664faca131e6100e632588" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a87bbeb1d0ac464a8a380b66c0897ab6"><span data-offset-key="a87bbeb1d0ac464a8a380b66c0897ab6:0">string</span></span></span></a><span key="affee60c74504a2abdccbcc216c2916a"><span offset-key="affee60c74504a2abdccbcc216c2916a:0"> as a number.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-typing-46" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="29b8edc934af40cbbcbd1c863bdd981c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a2b10e1ef5734b48bfcc24492082bfe6"><span data-offset-key="a2b10e1ef5734b48bfcc24492082bfe6:0">[46]</span></span></span></a><span key="fb3db3c637d24d42bc332374c6388f0e"><span offset-key="fb3db3c637d24d42bc332374c6388f0e:0"> This can occasionally be useful, but it can also allow some kinds of program faults to go undetected at </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Compile_time" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3ea47e62ff0a483294f58adf9d606cef" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="6bf01294bada456f895b4d7ebf4d9b2e"><span data-offset-key="6bf01294bada456f895b4d7ebf4d9b2e:0">compile time</span></span></span></a><span key="8b981b0506c64c609b34bd1ba30a68a1"><span offset-key="8b981b0506c64c609b34bd1ba30a68a1:0"> and even at </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Run_time_(program_lifecycle_phase)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a2160ba4d0c1449d952225b892a9c3f3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="22aa5f54552742faaafa24d2e348cf10"><span data-offset-key="22aa5f54552742faaafa24d2e348cf10:0">run time</span></span></span></a><span key="49815938270f4f078824ac1a14d9304c"><span offset-key="49815938270f4f078824ac1a14d9304c:0">.</span></span>

<span key="1f57e7276c28444f9c147faa54ed1a73"><span offset-key="1f57e7276c28444f9c147faa54ed1a73:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Strongly_typed_programming_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6273bd0f547a404faf5dce15fc93d6e5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="fd51e0601bec4add92c588c1076c6869"><span data-offset-key="fd51e0601bec4add92c588c1076c6869:0">Strong typing</span></span></span></a><span key="df99606f8e834b3b88ebe6be5483b720"><span offset-key="df99606f8e834b3b88ebe6be5483b720:0"> prevents these program faults. An attempt to perform an operation on the wrong type of value raises an error.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-typing-46" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="98572a83ce724fa9b4494594ca6ed01e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="f2906f912c024117bef5a1b1ae963b8c"><span data-offset-key="f2906f912c024117bef5a1b1ae963b8c:0">[46]</span></span></span></a><span key="7427cad842274d87b1d1408852c8d0be"><span offset-key="7427cad842274d87b1d1408852c8d0be:0"> Strongly typed languages are often termed type-safe or </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Type_safety" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a4a3a175ee764a5d80e71dc778046687" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="71e7d2573dd64134985452c0466a3132"><span data-offset-key="71e7d2573dd64134985452c0466a3132:0">safe</span></span></span></a><span key="45b5c7c1b06e4ca18d5a797cf582dcef"><span offset-key="45b5c7c1b06e4ca18d5a797cf582dcef:0">.</span></span>

<span key="96a421078fbb4017af28880899f087ad"><span offset-key="96a421078fbb4017af28880899f087ad:0">An alternative definition for "weakly typed" refers to languages, such as </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Perl" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9bbca5fabf2c4d3299f7496edfeb1c55" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="b3bef288c061419291811517fc0179f7"><span data-offset-key="b3bef288c061419291811517fc0179f7:0">Perl</span></span></span></a><span key="35502752f39747c18bbd7b9d9d3e2249"><span offset-key="35502752f39747c18bbd7b9d9d3e2249:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/JavaScript" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="dfa2cbd5e53f4e59940e94210fa94d13" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="07a8948f11d14da7a8b9a3c95aa3d73a"><span data-offset-key="07a8948f11d14da7a8b9a3c95aa3d73a:0">JavaScript</span></span></span></a><span key="ac664e29b5094f5b9bc2a5e2c6ee0131"><span offset-key="ac664e29b5094f5b9bc2a5e2c6ee0131:0">, which permit a large number of implicit type conversions. In JavaScript, for example, the expression </span>`2 * x`<span offset-key="ac664e29b5094f5b9bc2a5e2c6ee0131:2"> implicitly converts </span>`x`<span offset-key="ac664e29b5094f5b9bc2a5e2c6ee0131:4"> to a number, and this conversion succeeds even if </span>`x`<span offset-key="ac664e29b5094f5b9bc2a5e2c6ee0131:6"> is </span>`null`<span offset-key="ac664e29b5094f5b9bc2a5e2c6ee0131:8">, </span>`undefined`<span offset-key="ac664e29b5094f5b9bc2a5e2c6ee0131:10">, an </span>`Array`<span offset-key="ac664e29b5094f5b9bc2a5e2c6ee0131:12">, or a string of letters. Such implicit conversions are often useful, but they can mask programming errors. Strong and static are now generally considered orthogonal concepts, but usage in the literature differs. Some use the term strongly typed to mean strongly, statically typed, or, even more confusingly, to mean simply statically typed. Thus </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="cc1445f718c24a668b78b43cbd22500b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="d0462a3e67f8446fb12a8cfa62770436"><span data-offset-key="d0462a3e67f8446fb12a8cfa62770436:0">C</span></span></span></a><span key="5ed3059950b24d579dc11c5354172e7c"><span offset-key="5ed3059950b24d579dc11c5354172e7c:0"> has been called both strongly typed and weakly, statically typed.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-48" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3fcae49d50ca4848a2adb422b88b8516" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="b12c5b50377d43028cd6e3740e543822"><span data-offset-key="b12c5b50377d43028cd6e3740e543822:0">[48]</span></span></span></a><span key="1f13871c68ec46dc897dba9d4a4fc270"><span offset-key="1f13871c68ec46dc897dba9d4a4fc270:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-49" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="cc2cd05946f04919872982da42612420" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="c5e8b4d2ee2747ff8d2500537a8c22a7"><span data-offset-key="c5e8b4d2ee2747ff8d2500537a8c22a7:0">[49]</span></span></span></a><span key="62be86e84f314177b2f0f9755c4de0f2"><span offset-key="62be86e84f314177b2f0f9755c4de0f2:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="8357c968c1b143e98d178446490aa97c"><span offset-key="8357c968c1b143e98d178446490aa97c:0">It may seem odd to some professional programmers that C could be "weakly, statically typed". However, notice that the use of the generic pointer, the </span>**void\***<span offset-key="8357c968c1b143e98d178446490aa97c:2"> pointer, does allow for casting of pointers to other pointers without needing to do an explicit cast. This is extremely similar to somehow casting an array of bytes to any kind of datatype in C without using an explicit cast, such as </span>`(int)`<span offset-key="8357c968c1b143e98d178446490aa97c:4"> or </span>`(char)`<span offset-key="8357c968c1b143e98d178446490aa97c:6">.</span></span>

### 

<span key="b7f55f4414394b7c89695e0825d17aaa"><span offset-key="b7f55f4414394b7c89695e0825d17aaa:0">Standard library and run-time system\[</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Programming_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ad1c4c2312fb4028871f716cc13a24ab" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="51e25cc72f2f4fea88c8d8fbd9c1c92a"><span data-offset-key="51e25cc72f2f4fea88c8d8fbd9c1c92a:0">edit</span></span></span></a><span key="8c368ea146f04a69b65bbeb4e12c9116"><span offset-key="8c368ea146f04a69b65bbeb4e12c9116:0">\]</span></span>

<span key="f94f521435624c1d9247fd34a656e142"><span offset-key="f94f521435624c1d9247fd34a656e142:0">Main article: </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Standard_library" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="27a7216c71704068a278df0f88ad227c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="f7382fb59e394eb385512d8b54819b1f"><span data-offset-key="f7382fb59e394eb385512d8b54819b1f:0">Standard library</span></span></span></a><span key="d567deae14df4f7fa53dd7e1119a0b36"><span offset-key="d567deae14df4f7fa53dd7e1119a0b36:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="98c3ec3f8b374f81a81c67301533c272"><span offset-key="98c3ec3f8b374f81a81c67301533c272:0">Most programming languages have an associated core </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Library_(computing)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f6117a0906bf44ef88a4b83816f1c959" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="c7e96f42094346fbba7704f016862c1f"><span data-offset-key="c7e96f42094346fbba7704f016862c1f:0">library</span></span></span></a><span key="31b79666de0c40a9b51eec567afa763a"><span offset-key="31b79666de0c40a9b51eec567afa763a:0"> (sometimes known as the 'standard library', especially if it is included as part of the published language standard), which is conventionally made available by all implementations of the language. Core libraries typically include definitions for commonly used algorithms, data structures, and mechanisms for input and output.</span></span>

<span key="dd53e33dcb0844378a8360f14ab18751"><span offset-key="dd53e33dcb0844378a8360f14ab18751:0">The line between a language and its core library differs from language to language. In some cases, the language designers may treat the library as a separate entity from the language. However, a language's core library is often treated as part of the language by its users, and some language specifications even require that this library be made available in all implementations. Indeed, some languages are designed so that the meanings of certain syntactic constructs cannot even be described without referring to the core library. For example, in </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Java_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="81d916c28d9b4c8aa2a3224824b05a61" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="3b8d40049564409c87052851158cbba0"><span data-offset-key="3b8d40049564409c87052851158cbba0:0">Java</span></span></span></a><span key="6e2e21bf6d4d458ca7fe760abf3a5ff4"><span offset-key="6e2e21bf6d4d458ca7fe760abf3a5ff4:0">, a string literal is defined as an instance of the </span>`java.lang.String`<span offset-key="6e2e21bf6d4d458ca7fe760abf3a5ff4:2"> class; similarly, in </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Smalltalk" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d0bf1c0da373417b8394c06c6958b677" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="0ef2d48ae59c4e4997cadb7d939f9823"><span data-offset-key="0ef2d48ae59c4e4997cadb7d939f9823:0">Smalltalk</span></span></span></a><span key="c0e28d279c1d477ea952a7be3a6435c5"><span offset-key="c0e28d279c1d477ea952a7be3a6435c5:0">, an </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anonymous_function" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="91982f1bdf014601bf2765e053073530" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="0b9bba13ad9a42db8195ae5de2bee346"><span data-offset-key="0b9bba13ad9a42db8195ae5de2bee346:0">anonymous function</span></span></span></a><span key="ff4e3b6d9e73454f9825066e92e013c4"><span offset-key="ff4e3b6d9e73454f9825066e92e013c4:0"> expression (a "block") constructs an instance of the library's </span>`BlockContext`<span offset-key="ff4e3b6d9e73454f9825066e92e013c4:2"> class. Conversely, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scheme_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2f65dce8ff8d4df4aaba6b170ced0ca4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="6e691bd812f0440d93dcd8ea6b97ce3c"><span data-offset-key="6e691bd812f0440d93dcd8ea6b97ce3c:0">Scheme</span></span></span></a><span key="90e8d91581db43e1884a73ee38c935b9"><span offset-key="90e8d91581db43e1884a73ee38c935b9:0"> contains multiple coherent subsets that suffice to construct the rest of the language as library macros, and so the language designers do not even bother to say which portions of the language must be implemented as language constructs, and which must be implemented as parts of a library.</span></span>

## 

<span key="1f67c0bf56354cbc8a7e7180f1cb4f9e"><span offset-key="1f67c0bf56354cbc8a7e7180f1cb4f9e:0">Design and implementation\[</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Programming_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="767fc6b854034d108b1398969f27a231" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="1078fd2bb5cb484aa40b8c274e15a980"><span data-offset-key="1078fd2bb5cb484aa40b8c274e15a980:0">edit</span></span></span></a><span key="84a1f198e8c348de9d2eae7d8951994a"><span offset-key="84a1f198e8c348de9d2eae7d8951994a:0">\]</span></span>

<span key="68ecbe26ab8548a49acdd48f973646f6"><span offset-key="68ecbe26ab8548a49acdd48f973646f6:0">Programming languages share properties with natural languages related to their purpose as vehicles for communication, having a syntactic form separate from its semantics, and showing language families of related languages branching one from another.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-Fischer-50" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="31f022c7ab9f4451a5df4d0da6b15322" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="385ba0b14d584293a46a00dcfc441f66"><span data-offset-key="385ba0b14d584293a46a00dcfc441f66:0">[50]</span></span></span></a><span key="7f09a44989cc4645b1a8501e5b0d814d"><span offset-key="7f09a44989cc4645b1a8501e5b0d814d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-levenez-51" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9baea73cfdcc435898e52b8b7f3a67e0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="be6817d4521d48f787541d08a45198f1"><span data-offset-key="be6817d4521d48f787541d08a45198f1:0">[51]</span></span></span></a><span key="04f323b4291243188a9805155782be90"><span offset-key="04f323b4291243188a9805155782be90:0"> But as artificial constructs, they also differ in fundamental ways from languages that have evolved through usage. A significant difference is that a programming language can be fully described and studied in its entirety since it has a precise and finite definition.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-52" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9cc489f8b39346c0947c3a32f5b2ccde" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="090856e43b294d57ad659fab8620fd93"><span data-offset-key="090856e43b294d57ad659fab8620fd93:0">[52]</span></span></span></a><span key="df632bd35c224aa78c580b9f9ce8a1c8"><span offset-key="df632bd35c224aa78c580b9f9ce8a1c8:0"> By contrast, natural languages have changing meanings given by their users in different communities. While </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Constructed_languages" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="377d51140ed8437fa5db24d21a461122" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="d0cb1bacec694e5ab3de1f31c8c38456"><span data-offset-key="d0cb1bacec694e5ab3de1f31c8c38456:0">constructed languages</span></span></span></a><span key="bcc64caa016d4d8f9602dd6d1412aa9e"><span offset-key="bcc64caa016d4d8f9602dd6d1412aa9e:0"> are also artificial languages designed from the ground up with a specific purpose, they lack the precise and complete semantic definition that a programming language has.</span></span>

<span key="59cd6244dad8478b8a7d9be94cd53022"><span offset-key="59cd6244dad8478b8a7d9be94cd53022:0">Many programming languages have been designed from scratch, altered to meet new needs, and combined with other languages. Many have eventually fallen into disuse. Although there have been attempts to design one "universal" programming language that serves all purposes, all of them have failed to be generally accepted as filling this role.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-53" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="215b25dd83d94e2e9da81ec4d70257db" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="9bce04596d5b4bd8841fdbfee2315180"><span data-offset-key="9bce04596d5b4bd8841fdbfee2315180:0">[53]</span></span></span></a><span key="6b817c4723f345138b884defac55902e"><span offset-key="6b817c4723f345138b884defac55902e:0"> The need for diverse programming languages arises from the diversity of contexts in which languages are used:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="1115872d47894bf2baecbe427aae418c"><span offset-key="1115872d47894bf2baecbe427aae418c:0">Programs range from tiny scripts written by individual hobbyists to huge systems written by hundreds of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programmer" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ca991a393b124c8b88242feab93e2eae" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="effc91d0f00a40f38b4be0a8c8ef6e7e"><span data-offset-key="effc91d0f00a40f38b4be0a8c8ef6e7e:0">programmers</span></span></span></a><span key="60c147be75844fa8a0cc19a09b1bed65"><span offset-key="60c147be75844fa8a0cc19a09b1bed65:0">.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="b96767829f1e46088802cc9cf329f8cd"><span offset-key="b96767829f1e46088802cc9cf329f8cd:0">Programmers range in expertise from novices who need simplicity above all else to experts who may be comfortable with considerable complexity.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="98929e54a11244f6898d565161cc748d"><span offset-key="98929e54a11244f6898d565161cc748d:0">Programs must balance speed, size, and simplicity on systems ranging from </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Microcontroller" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1f39cb675477483eb7e648880c7b0f23" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="2e991f8d4838439997abbac6a5217e7a"><span data-offset-key="2e991f8d4838439997abbac6a5217e7a:0">microcontrollers</span></span></span></a><span key="e93e88a410f44ed2898bad7a6280fe7c"><span offset-key="e93e88a410f44ed2898bad7a6280fe7c:0"> to </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Supercomputer" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="912c5ffd2ef044f395f13c7cc5d46f2c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="10d4cf2a0e4648919a1b47cdea252a96"><span data-offset-key="10d4cf2a0e4648919a1b47cdea252a96:0">supercomputers</span></span></span></a><span key="820504ebcfc64fa3811be6f0ead8b295"><span offset-key="820504ebcfc64fa3811be6f0ead8b295:0">.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="07ffb827a108446e90a34c1eb5635372"><span offset-key="07ffb827a108446e90a34c1eb5635372:0">Programs may be written once and not change for generations, or they may undergo continual modification.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="5b25214ad3b34218b8957981ece826f5"><span offset-key="5b25214ad3b34218b8957981ece826f5:0">Programmers may simply differ in their tastes: they may be accustomed to discussing problems and expressing them in a particular language.</span></span>

<span key="66f1f0e2a6c3443fb3b9cc3ba4736f22"><span offset-key="66f1f0e2a6c3443fb3b9cc3ba4736f22:0">One common trend in the development of programming languages has been to add more ability to solve problems using a higher level of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Abstraction_(computer_science)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4491dcc0062b44c681367807c4381bf0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="ad9a307f135f40e2a72607f54c1a70c4"><span data-offset-key="ad9a307f135f40e2a72607f54c1a70c4:0">abstraction</span></span></span></a><span key="8cec6d12ef1645fe8bfc3ad39574fa6e"><span offset-key="8cec6d12ef1645fe8bfc3ad39574fa6e:0">. The earliest programming languages were tied very closely to the underlying hardware of the computer. As new programming languages have developed, features have been added that let programmers express ideas that are more remote from simple translation into underlying hardware instructions. Because programmers are less tied to the complexity of the computer, their programs can do more computing with less effort from the programmer. This lets them write more functionality per time unit.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-54" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="30ac8a941320458eba51a94eb3ddaac5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="c299983df5dd43d5af7aed6791f60317"><span data-offset-key="c299983df5dd43d5af7aed6791f60317:0">[54]</span></span></span></a><span key="f470f8a05b834f508f8ebf75a3134bf5"><span offset-key="f470f8a05b834f508f8ebf75a3134bf5:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="e52b1509b6f34b77931b62a97e6c10e7"><span offset-key="e52b1509b6f34b77931b62a97e6c10e7:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Natural_language_programming" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="76a3167031e448ef93632441d236a3a8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="93db1e36e3914aefbfff3b4ef9115632"><span data-offset-key="93db1e36e3914aefbfff3b4ef9115632:0">Natural language programming</span></span></span></a><span key="4335f25a0a234897b28b61b389bfb5b7"><span offset-key="4335f25a0a234897b28b61b389bfb5b7:0"> has been proposed as a way to eliminate the need for a specialized language for programming. However, this goal remains distant and its benefits are open to debate. </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edsger_W._Dijkstra" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7f20f2f410fa4b29b4dc601c3fde7284" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="dfd4ed463fec45c1aa31db6af881d0ef"><span data-offset-key="dfd4ed463fec45c1aa31db6af881d0ef:0">Edsger W. Dijkstra</span></span></span></a><span key="0aab363ca45547e09bb854a034178510"><span offset-key="0aab363ca45547e09bb854a034178510:0"> took the position that the use of a formal language is essential to prevent the introduction of meaningless constructs, and dismissed </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Natural_language_programming" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="872f80994f794bf690d9efe6a2ac616e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="7b53fe7721304df78538360010ac3637"><span data-offset-key="7b53fe7721304df78538360010ac3637:0">natural language programming</span></span></span></a><span key="04f89e3984f14c989fa399f75451b74c"><span offset-key="04f89e3984f14c989fa399f75451b74c:0"> as "foolish".</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-55" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1fc8ab66fd744200a65fdc41bc4db47a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="67931c2a6a954db9bce813796c48c558"><span data-offset-key="67931c2a6a954db9bce813796c48c558:0">[55]</span></span></span></a><span key="ca7adc22706f4a55a4d8da1c2c34a9e1"><span offset-key="ca7adc22706f4a55a4d8da1c2c34a9e1:0"> </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alan_Perlis" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1acdbb90382f4ec2abb2e39d99137611" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="2d5f04f46c8642dda1b39cf5f97b953f"><span data-offset-key="2d5f04f46c8642dda1b39cf5f97b953f:0">Alan Perlis</span></span></span></a><span key="6248aee0829c4594846019f643a56a96"><span offset-key="6248aee0829c4594846019f643a56a96:0"> was similarly dismissive of the idea.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-56" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="56f2172105914c2caff9e0f0c43173b1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="9bdc4fe8f3f4469583253b1c34b239ee"><span data-offset-key="9bdc4fe8f3f4469583253b1c34b239ee:0">[56]</span></span></span></a><span key="99429d8fb9204af883b9f1bc19ebe22c"><span offset-key="99429d8fb9204af883b9f1bc19ebe22c:0"> Hybrid approaches have been taken in </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Structured_English" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="184255e32d194969b399e94a4301e00f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4acc594a540347908477a942b77bd3c5"><span data-offset-key="4acc594a540347908477a942b77bd3c5:0">Structured English</span></span></span></a><span key="b5b8c32437fc49c0bfabacfaf7e4c11c"><span offset-key="b5b8c32437fc49c0bfabacfaf7e4c11c:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SQL" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bfe545259a914bc58aa7f86380814d8f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4a46af7fbf554ae69dc78941d630d070"><span data-offset-key="4a46af7fbf554ae69dc78941d630d070:0">SQL</span></span></span></a><span key="6123201517c248f089da96c0bfcb4d13"><span offset-key="6123201517c248f089da96c0bfcb4d13:0">.</span></span>

<span key="e0f62aabfa72440b8c5df92c9b753b22"><span offset-key="e0f62aabfa72440b8c5df92c9b753b22:0">A language's designers and users must construct a number of artifacts that govern and enable the practice of programming. The most important of these artifacts are the language specification and implementation.</span></span>

### 

<span key="1bacc6db4b0348058074e3dd940c1109"><span offset-key="1bacc6db4b0348058074e3dd940c1109:0">Specification\[</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Programming_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7878f69a953c4b399fb4193a6529ee6d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="3beaf78b730f4c7aac5ad68526d7b910"><span data-offset-key="3beaf78b730f4c7aac5ad68526d7b910:0">edit</span></span></span></a><span key="cff137f4450e441eaeaf991005347bee"><span offset-key="cff137f4450e441eaeaf991005347bee:0">\]</span></span>

<span key="83b1f887d76c4257b422359231a1b769"><span offset-key="83b1f887d76c4257b422359231a1b769:0">Main article: </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language_specification" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3185e9785ed3447180afc395cc02bf33" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="c64dac9f96374ddbb3df49b5eb56bc0a"><span data-offset-key="c64dac9f96374ddbb3df49b5eb56bc0a:0">Programming language specification</span></span></span></a><span key="228285b2ca4c4750bc2231ca977d617c"><span offset-key="228285b2ca4c4750bc2231ca977d617c:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="8bd88ee7660a4e05919c26f49a8b2b52"><span offset-key="8bd88ee7660a4e05919c26f49a8b2b52:0">The specification of a programming language is an artifact that the language </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programmer" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d1ea3901678f428d863ae790a3e3a573" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="76ddf6946d0e40a5a37bb8a44a89d1d7"><span data-offset-key="76ddf6946d0e40a5a37bb8a44a89d1d7:0">users</span></span></span></a><span key="7edfb28293214bd1b478d9d0625ea8e3"><span offset-key="7edfb28293214bd1b478d9d0625ea8e3:0"> and the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language_implementation" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fa8c6d6e1fd04171a5bddfb21a47cc0e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="cb8c15e74bb54a9c87a617c007139e4d"><span data-offset-key="cb8c15e74bb54a9c87a617c007139e4d:0">implementors</span></span></span></a><span key="0ef5c391faea4dadb3a3a429bff21088"><span offset-key="0ef5c391faea4dadb3a3a429bff21088:0"> can use to agree upon whether a piece of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Source_code" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="459fb6530c3c46ee86142fea5b9ea075" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4b1d083de2dc4733920d992079e17185"><span data-offset-key="4b1d083de2dc4733920d992079e17185:0">source code</span></span></span></a><span key="33e51152869f4bce89466c688ad0044c"><span offset-key="33e51152869f4bce89466c688ad0044c:0"> is a valid </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_program" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3b2a3c4b5a594d43b34c0dc6af7c1480" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="b37006372b074dc891272667b099d483"><span data-offset-key="b37006372b074dc891272667b099d483:0">program</span></span></span></a><span key="4974fa5b9d1f46fa87406b4c9bd810bd"><span offset-key="4974fa5b9d1f46fa87406b4c9bd810bd:0"> in that language, and if so what its behavior shall be.</span></span>

<span key="63691ea756fc492f843c890f25de060b"><span offset-key="63691ea756fc492f843c890f25de060b:0">A programming language specification can take several forms, including the following:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="a72338a740294dd682fae88467e3ac03"><span offset-key="a72338a740294dd682fae88467e3ac03:0">An explicit definition of the syntax, static semantics, and execution semantics of the language. While syntax is commonly specified using a formal grammar, semantic definitions may be written in </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Natural_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fb262bedf284470ea99963b1eaaa37bc" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4956f76c249245a79043ab7a00d4c7bb"><span data-offset-key="4956f76c249245a79043ab7a00d4c7bb:0">natural language</span></span></span></a><span key="58638b3cf69f4a11a2fba2d5b78a7169"><span offset-key="58638b3cf69f4a11a2fba2d5b78a7169:0"> (e.g., as in the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4e0bfc27632b48a392b482a8e94c748f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="5daf9237950947d7aaaf0978a3b9a3c6"><span data-offset-key="5daf9237950947d7aaaf0978a3b9a3c6:0">C language</span></span></span></a><span key="ee13b1fc0e0b4020b56e400802aa4e27"><span offset-key="ee13b1fc0e0b4020b56e400802aa4e27:0">), or a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Formal_semantics_of_programming_languages" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ad1df66dbeed4810856c1c3f5d9426aa" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="7befddeacb644a63902bcefbefffdefb"><span data-offset-key="7befddeacb644a63902bcefbefffdefb:0">formal semantics</span></span></span></a><span key="d9f10d39fd2e45e9b79bf00845c1abb5"><span offset-key="d9f10d39fd2e45e9b79bf00845c1abb5:0"> (e.g., as in </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Standard_ML" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bec76448ff13480f871d315dcb74b1f8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="94b404f4e2fa4f7082e852134b985438"><span data-offset-key="94b404f4e2fa4f7082e852134b985438:0">Standard ML</span></span></span></a><span key="b2a992831d91420183718b2e9c6ac303"><span offset-key="b2a992831d91420183718b2e9c6ac303:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-57" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0f9d6b8c010a4192b1083bd1d4f018f5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="5a933a439e414fa3afe7c43899c0bc78"><span data-offset-key="5a933a439e414fa3afe7c43899c0bc78:0">[57]</span></span></span></a><span key="3df4ebbfcb87499c9f73f1fe55e9e8b4"><span offset-key="3df4ebbfcb87499c9f73f1fe55e9e8b4:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scheme_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ace648d318a54dd5ae04649bf7ac27c2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="0180a1490ac547aaae432b3b6ba3fd11"><span data-offset-key="0180a1490ac547aaae432b3b6ba3fd11:0">Scheme</span></span></span></a><span key="f3fd5e8b5eea4c36aa0a8905a4367c5e"><span offset-key="f3fd5e8b5eea4c36aa0a8905a4367c5e:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-58" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e43b87142a294579b73cade5086567c4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="619ffe7b4b0549a0a575e405d9202a69"><span data-offset-key="619ffe7b4b0549a0a575e405d9202a69:0">[58]</span></span></span></a><span key="ebe2e63b8f6842eaa4223e791e47ca9b"><span offset-key="ebe2e63b8f6842eaa4223e791e47ca9b:0"> specifications).</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="bc4079db64d449a9a033ea773fb33824"><span offset-key="bc4079db64d449a9a033ea773fb33824:0">A description of the behavior of a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Compiler" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="5e20c2cf0650452d94034cb341cb2e66" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a3f7205fe3b34d879a8d4529dfd22674"><span data-offset-key="a3f7205fe3b34d879a8d4529dfd22674:0">translator</span></span></span></a><span key="23d2209543ce48b39a7c85cb692e5f63"><span offset-key="23d2209543ce48b39a7c85cb692e5f63:0"> for the language (e.g., the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C%2B%2B" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3b0c8cd9685c47bab7d780978549974a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="3509b22a43064ede9b66e30332735432"><span data-offset-key="3509b22a43064ede9b66e30332735432:0">C++</span></span></span></a><span key="df6c0759eb254dd38dfbb11537a6b4d7"><span offset-key="df6c0759eb254dd38dfbb11537a6b4d7:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fortran" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c65965539c5147e3bc6ffa5751780596" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="7a86c8fffd8d443b92b9cad1bf701d8b"><span data-offset-key="7a86c8fffd8d443b92b9cad1bf701d8b:0">Fortran</span></span></span></a><span key="7ec71f9012c3441b84a2d3959b98c4f0"><span offset-key="7ec71f9012c3441b84a2d3959b98c4f0:0"> specifications). The syntax and semantics of the language have to be inferred from this description, which may be written in natural or a formal language.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="52e08676a9f548869fa88bca2f50c9ba"><span offset-key="52e08676a9f548869fa88bca2f50c9ba:0">A </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Reference_implementation" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="14f7aff47ffc456f9579dc47d7715b3b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="b8eb59093f5c4daf9e88560343436260"><span data-offset-key="b8eb59093f5c4daf9e88560343436260:0">reference or model implementation</span></span></span></a><span key="6b31b1936f28430eab96de6e464f70ee"><span offset-key="6b31b1936f28430eab96de6e464f70ee:0">, sometimes </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Meta-circular_evaluator" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="175a27018f8d474bbf238c0789ac6413" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="eb36336a33bd470eb1780ae4c16fd9c9"><span data-offset-key="eb36336a33bd470eb1780ae4c16fd9c9:0">written in the language being specified</span></span></span></a><span key="264d14697af148d0b5f027d900b4f88b"><span offset-key="264d14697af148d0b5f027d900b4f88b:0"> (e.g., </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Prolog" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="473c4dcee8f7489d8f543c85e10b1f3c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="5cfb2024e4b248c9b1d5f1cfbf5313c0"><span data-offset-key="5cfb2024e4b248c9b1d5f1cfbf5313c0:0">Prolog</span></span></span></a><span key="1d2d7834a2a1469d9dae9f8826dd1157"><span offset-key="1d2d7834a2a1469d9dae9f8826dd1157:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/REXX" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2c4d16baddbd40f2b458f9e5f8dc33a5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="757ef04fa0ea4c5bb6b4cd0f5d932813"><span data-offset-key="757ef04fa0ea4c5bb6b4cd0f5d932813:0">ANSI REXX</span></span></span></a><span key="46297ebb45fb4c6e963ef3000493dd2d"><span offset-key="46297ebb45fb4c6e963ef3000493dd2d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-59" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ce1f277d78854f7ba8a0b062d8e617bf" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="083294b4f9ed4aa0a5aab41b7a8d3606"><span data-offset-key="083294b4f9ed4aa0a5aab41b7a8d3606:0">[59]</span></span></span></a><span key="3719e7d9925b414ab81472f281627338"><span offset-key="3719e7d9925b414ab81472f281627338:0">). The syntax and semantics of the language are explicit in the behavior of the reference implementation.</span></span>

### 

<span key="9847cababa7040b08001d5c053f4eab7"><span offset-key="9847cababa7040b08001d5c053f4eab7:0">Implementation\[</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Programming_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d45adf4d0d9f4ce9b73d33b38755d56d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="8b981bc56acb4e858a1592b90c6c8b1d"><span data-offset-key="8b981bc56acb4e858a1592b90c6c8b1d:0">edit</span></span></span></a><span key="e464eb041e2f4028bdf0864c1f052de4"><span offset-key="e464eb041e2f4028bdf0864c1f052de4:0">\]</span></span>

<span key="c11ce9b6e0f2462aa5734e47a263c048"><span offset-key="c11ce9b6e0f2462aa5734e47a263c048:0">Main article: </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language_implementation" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0df46c78618748fc92ea86c40fa9c8ad" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="bd0d36265d57423292bd2d39c4529dc3"><span data-offset-key="bd0d36265d57423292bd2d39c4529dc3:0">Programming language implementation</span></span></span></a><span key="68e667208f4a440d9db4719d3e9b9447"><span offset-key="68e667208f4a440d9db4719d3e9b9447:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="6a8d23a185ee4e31a7021349305826ab"><span offset-key="6a8d23a185ee4e31a7021349305826ab:0">An implementation of a programming language provides a way to write programs in that language and execute them on one or more configurations of hardware and software.
