There are, broadly, two approaches to programming language implementation: </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Compiler" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9bf7906e43cb40f993515995e271ece3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="09001b0c83a9456ba0b220bade3cb739"><span data-offset-key="09001b0c83a9456ba0b220bade3cb739:0">compilation</span></span></span></a><span key="ce79cfabc5f54cca94b2f46eab6d6a8d"><span offset-key="ce79cfabc5f54cca94b2f46eab6d6a8d:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Interpreter_(computing)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="201b8d270af04c37982817b0ed4816b9" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="9401f8f4e1704533b14cbace77e005c9"><span data-offset-key="9401f8f4e1704533b14cbace77e005c9:0">interpretation</span></span></span></a><span key="412bfe3989304cda87ecca2532fe77df"><span offset-key="412bfe3989304cda87ecca2532fe77df:0">. It is generally possible to implement a language using either technique.</span></span>

<span key="6f04a25234af41acb2410c167586a0b4"><span offset-key="6f04a25234af41acb2410c167586a0b4:0">The output of a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Compiler" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="66f348633a3e405fb0da90a61ab44357" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="d28ae0be9c5546f59a762f165ef9465c"><span data-offset-key="d28ae0be9c5546f59a762f165ef9465c:0">compiler</span></span></span></a><span key="0dc861a761274ea2bce6c404e866069a"><span offset-key="0dc861a761274ea2bce6c404e866069a:0"> may be executed by hardware or a program called an interpreter. In some implementations that make use of the interpreter approach there is no distinct boundary between compiling and interpreting. For instance, some implementations of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/BASIC" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2fb77ccbedd94be2948642a77c1d58fa" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="743af9cc6d4c4e70af5bdd27857c8eca"><span data-offset-key="743af9cc6d4c4e70af5bdd27857c8eca:0">BASIC</span></span></span></a><span key="67ee9dc1a96b4b41b1d0163a7a2d7da1"><span offset-key="67ee9dc1a96b4b41b1d0163a7a2d7da1:0"> compile and then execute the source a line at a time.</span></span>

<span key="ff90d335d600480a90c512d08f6c4604"><span offset-key="ff90d335d600480a90c512d08f6c4604:0">Programs that are executed directly on the hardware usually run much faster than those that are interpreted in software.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-60" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="197c6bfdbf4a4c018a6cbf7d44ea5487" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="c73a87ee4e324da1b4c71fd3a7d4d38b"><span data-offset-key="c73a87ee4e324da1b4c71fd3a7d4d38b:0">[60]</span></span></span></a><span key="f3b75ddb234c4c9f89a5dff3a82b9b71"><span offset-key="f3b75ddb234c4c9f89a5dff3a82b9b71:0">\[</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:NOTRS" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a2a53be2f2c945d6b68c2122eb0392e5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="68ea634f9a57482c83c5e756ed2e1967"><span data-offset-key="68ea634f9a57482c83c5e756ed2e1967:0">better source needed</span></span></span></a><span key="f56a8c8347df4f7880fc0718fce35f44"><span offset-key="f56a8c8347df4f7880fc0718fce35f44:0">\]</span></span>

<span key="a59c7bbc95fa4d6cb4c99127c5ec180f"><span offset-key="a59c7bbc95fa4d6cb4c99127c5ec180f:0">One technique for improving the performance of interpreted programs is </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Just-in-time_compilation" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="edbddd08782549089c1f1b7156b4206e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="212c608e07ed41f7a1583a1983b7e06e"><span data-offset-key="212c608e07ed41f7a1583a1983b7e06e:0">just-in-time compilation</span></span></span></a><span key="daa83e4f89f94ef6b7fbbdf7c0170252"><span offset-key="daa83e4f89f94ef6b7fbbdf7c0170252:0">. Here the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_machine" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="da5b869bf25b4ed785fd6bf9adc671a6" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="f7f41fd50f9d4cf0a542d59fbd7b542d"><span data-offset-key="f7f41fd50f9d4cf0a542d59fbd7b542d:0">virtual machine</span></span></span></a><span key="e063b1ac67a64b7186d15e3229bbd6f1"><span offset-key="e063b1ac67a64b7186d15e3229bbd6f1:0">, just before execution, translates the blocks of </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bytecode" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="25cce787e284406aba56beb452af5381" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="280ba6a31a28422ea2dc70196cc7a221"><span data-offset-key="280ba6a31a28422ea2dc70196cc7a221:0">bytecode</span></span></span></a><span key="b276e72f19d7444fa2e5f7077bc29898"><span offset-key="b276e72f19d7444fa2e5f7077bc29898:0"> which are going to be used to machine code, for direct execution on the hardware.</span></span>

## 

<span key="f22fc58278744b9ea22ae71aad64f47e"><span offset-key="f22fc58278744b9ea22ae71aad64f47e:0">Proprietary languages\[</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Programming_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7faf08f5dc0b42e4ad05c96a5068abcd" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="9c5db6b01cf843c98c9296b1d5c390ce"><span data-offset-key="9c5db6b01cf843c98c9296b1d5c390ce:0">edit</span></span></span></a><span key="f176db35bd4740b98e270ecfcf44ec61"><span offset-key="f176db35bd4740b98e270ecfcf44ec61:0">\]</span></span>

<span key="f615bac280db4ec0a3ff4293346c6ff2"><span offset-key="f615bac280db4ec0a3ff4293346c6ff2:0">Although most of the most commonly used programming languages have fully open specifications and implementations, many programming languages exist only as proprietary programming languages with the implementation available only from a single vendor, which may claim that such a proprietary language is their intellectual property. Proprietary programming languages are commonly </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Domain_specific_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="63c6d3cba24944c39eb71b8fcf150939" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="717d963b5ba14e71b0479962bfeb8589"><span data-offset-key="717d963b5ba14e71b0479962bfeb8589:0">domain specific languages</span></span></span></a><span key="b0bfdb54b75f4c52aa489678515725a2"><span offset-key="b0bfdb54b75f4c52aa489678515725a2:0"> or internal </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scripting_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="aaaced3d96bb46479315eca3f6627d0d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="dc578461cbb04dd4a8a2b495f2eebe43"><span data-offset-key="dc578461cbb04dd4a8a2b495f2eebe43:0">scripting languages</span></span></span></a><span key="c56bea1cb8564b97933b9fc5e482b2fb"><span offset-key="c56bea1cb8564b97933b9fc5e482b2fb:0"> for a single product; some proprietary languages are used only internally within a vendor, while others are available to external users.</span></span>

<span key="9e991103166e483da41efd01293baa1c"><span offset-key="9e991103166e483da41efd01293baa1c:0">Some programming languages exist on the border between proprietary and open; for example, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oracle_Corporation" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ce5b414220a6452ba87ff3dc82c544e3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="153d6a653c92447d8974231e395a7b86"><span data-offset-key="153d6a653c92447d8974231e395a7b86:0">Oracle Corporation</span></span></span></a><span key="c71735d75c414024bdf00b277e97151c"><span offset-key="c71735d75c414024bdf00b277e97151c:0"> asserts proprietary rights to some aspects of the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Java_programming_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="48157b670afd4e86aedabe3640f40a97" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="e711d301e2d24a0495be5e2deb1f49db"><span data-offset-key="e711d301e2d24a0495be5e2deb1f49db:0">Java programming language</span></span></span></a><span key="e308547af3e84628ba347f968f796e17"><span offset-key="e308547af3e84628ba347f968f796e17:0">,</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-61" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="804e6e993e3741d3870c54647f27ee10" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="123cd88fce2e42eba20394393d03a4ac"><span data-offset-key="123cd88fce2e42eba20394393d03a4ac:0">[61]</span></span></span></a><span key="f1f9aa696cf24aca8dc6a34d5ea7f831"><span offset-key="f1f9aa696cf24aca8dc6a34d5ea7f831:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Microsoft" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ee3eb4b13e9445f787de3bbec6065462" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="8f00d9af30154b1c82eb4dae31f98878"><span data-offset-key="8f00d9af30154b1c82eb4dae31f98878:0">Microsoft</span></span></span></a><span key="1ac37b2ce5ac484e9f16e8783a0244ca"><span offset-key="1ac37b2ce5ac484e9f16e8783a0244ca:0">'s </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C_Sharp_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c8fa4fd1bb604cdaaacdabcbaa6ee262" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="58dc0b46eee64802ba61f1097a560f78"><span data-offset-key="58dc0b46eee64802ba61f1097a560f78:0">C#</span></span></span></a><span key="cd02f3109bad4ca193a5f3ac136e30f0"><span offset-key="cd02f3109bad4ca193a5f3ac136e30f0:0"> programming language, which has open implementations of most parts of the system, also has </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Common_Language_Runtime" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0d93ff10da2b40d7ad3e77cedb2aeb30" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="11c9f78326cb44f6a275d8a6536741ae"><span data-offset-key="11c9f78326cb44f6a275d8a6536741ae:0">Common Language Runtime</span></span></span></a><span key="17bd197150884cabae8efff97ce3e21a"><span offset-key="17bd197150884cabae8efff97ce3e21a:0"> (CLR) as a closed environment.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-62" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ce9bab13a7614239be7a060b90465d18" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="3244f2594bd541b596d8ab44fcd9bb7c"><span data-offset-key="3244f2594bd541b596d8ab44fcd9bb7c:0">[62]</span></span></span></a><span key="801f80160cc84973980d2905bc253e9a"><span offset-key="801f80160cc84973980d2905bc253e9a:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="ec231d21f868452c9cbfc75b618ed0d5"><span offset-key="ec231d21f868452c9cbfc75b618ed0d5:0">Many proprietary languages are widely used, in spite of their proprietary nature; examples include </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/MATLAB" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bc09be0255254a72bbf820969b1d0c03" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="e6df932cdb3546beb1e8bf1c1c33ee9c"><span data-offset-key="e6df932cdb3546beb1e8bf1c1c33ee9c:0">MATLAB</span></span></span></a><span key="ab486857fd814bc79cdc856a30f696e7"><span offset-key="ab486857fd814bc79cdc856a30f696e7:0">, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/VBScript" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f1a4ae680df24eb7a78beea2260917cd" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a52f87a6cf264fefbe4338c03c2b0a12"><span data-offset-key="a52f87a6cf264fefbe4338c03c2b0a12:0">VBScript</span></span></span></a><span key="2925e31df43741ef903c67be0fb9a056"><span offset-key="2925e31df43741ef903c67be0fb9a056:0">, and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wolfram_Language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0040e6bdd6544225839e962a6c759ab8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="94a1432adfba483ca8eb30e10f72f47c"><span data-offset-key="94a1432adfba483ca8eb30e10f72f47c:0">Wolfram Language</span></span></span></a><span key="227fc024eae841b383d2c625bcfb8809"><span offset-key="227fc024eae841b383d2c625bcfb8809:0">. Some languages may make the transition from closed to open; for example, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Erlang_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ae2e10fccf0a454199c69abd3225bc26" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="e45c7b1dcceb4761a568026125bef949"><span data-offset-key="e45c7b1dcceb4761a568026125bef949:0">Erlang</span></span></span></a><span key="8493b2cb6286478983da097e511b2ad4"><span offset-key="8493b2cb6286478983da097e511b2ad4:0"> was originally an Ericsson's internal programming language.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-63" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ff3eea04d73e467f84a1613a2c9ddf13" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4c75d09fcd8b426e893168f94686c58d"><span data-offset-key="4c75d09fcd8b426e893168f94686c58d:0">[63]</span></span></span></a><span key="65d556d82302434386299d0bc110f0f8"><span offset-key="65d556d82302434386299d0bc110f0f8:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

## 

<span key="cb295128098b4ad9af3d090239b1eaa9"><span offset-key="cb295128098b4ad9af3d090239b1eaa9:0">Use\[</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Programming_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8cb2ba2e41684b7282a49cdfc7ee0a37" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="dc6f01e5779d462b8d804a33c7421425"><span data-offset-key="dc6f01e5779d462b8d804a33c7421425:0">edit</span></span></span></a><span key="1d3ab85f01e34b1b939a1e2145c455c4"><span offset-key="1d3ab85f01e34b1b939a1e2145c455c4:0">\]</span></span>

<span key="2155026031a64c5b98db0c4fe418d251"><span offset-key="2155026031a64c5b98db0c4fe418d251:0">Thousands of different programming languages have been created, mainly in the computing field.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-64" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="6d75c6845194413fba92f3e5e2901989" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4ed8a2dd08744fdbb75ac384ffb3f6d1"><span data-offset-key="4ed8a2dd08744fdbb75ac384ffb3f6d1:0">[64]</span></span></span></a><span key="7c4617eac4f649e8b8e34a40bfbdd3ae"><span offset-key="7c4617eac4f649e8b8e34a40bfbdd3ae:0"> Individual software projects commonly use five programming languages or more.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-65" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="be7b9efce604490697e9324c109ba999" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="64ef3b57b03d47f1b096a082a7aac98c"><span data-offset-key="64ef3b57b03d47f1b096a082a7aac98c:0">[65]</span></span></span></a><span key="ae9dc804b5f7444c80235f2af0a42e22"><span offset-key="ae9dc804b5f7444c80235f2af0a42e22:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="c4be78b5d4e74b10b4121b03dfc6d6d3"><span offset-key="c4be78b5d4e74b10b4121b03dfc6d6d3:0">Programming languages differ from most other forms of human expression in that they require a greater degree of precision and completeness. When using a natural language to communicate with other people, human authors and speakers can be ambiguous and make small errors, and still expect their intent to be understood. However, figuratively speaking, computers "do exactly what they are told to do", and cannot "understand" what code the programmer intended to write. The combination of the language definition, a program, and the program's inputs must fully specify the external behavior that occurs when the program is executed, within the domain of control of that program. On the other hand, ideas about an algorithm can be communicated to humans without the precision required for execution by using </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pseudocode" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a2cd41809deb4592bfdf12cc91950e7b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="190bf4c437a140bcbb056091c161af96"><span data-offset-key="190bf4c437a140bcbb056091c161af96:0">pseudocode</span></span></span></a><span key="9843ad8bc4694aeca9abb3a02075f9d2"><span offset-key="9843ad8bc4694aeca9abb3a02075f9d2:0">, which interleaves natural language with code written in a programming language.</span></span>

<span key="7ff831d31bbd4df8a10205fb82b7c51e"><span offset-key="7ff831d31bbd4df8a10205fb82b7c51e:0">A programming language provides a structured mechanism for defining pieces of data, and the operations or transformations that may be carried out automatically on that data. A </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programmer" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="86eb9680a9344f84bb2d6ec11a014d66" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4761dc03a0664db2bf034e906457aa2c"><span data-offset-key="4761dc03a0664db2bf034e906457aa2c:0">programmer</span></span></span></a><span key="9b030bbcf9f542fe986bbdb2a735b312"><span offset-key="9b030bbcf9f542fe986bbdb2a735b312:0"> uses the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Abstraction_(computer_science)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e7ac7f497f61462682e48a30820e5c7a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="1d4df764b2324ead8b8b9740143a27c4"><span data-offset-key="1d4df764b2324ead8b8b9740143a27c4:0">abstractions</span></span></span></a><span key="12f84edd503d4390871895a194c37590"><span offset-key="12f84edd503d4390871895a194c37590:0"> present in the language to represent the concepts involved in a computation. These concepts are represented as a collection of the simplest elements available (called </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Language_primitive" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4d5ee553b6a046d0bc26f44f44e20f32" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="df133efcea0c4d7295e2fde60e622619"><span data-offset-key="df133efcea0c4d7295e2fde60e622619:0">primitives</span></span></span></a><span key="2fb23d89dcd44e1ba53346cb1dfb3c88"><span offset-key="2fb23d89dcd44e1ba53346cb1dfb3c88:0">).</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-66" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c4d0ba384d7544168836d8baa1b0f6d4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="495d5b09836b4b22aac93e70c3e22f79"><span data-offset-key="495d5b09836b4b22aac93e70c3e22f79:0">[66]</span></span></span></a><span key="905971401ee84d889ca14468287c2d5a"><span offset-key="905971401ee84d889ca14468287c2d5a:0"> </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Computer_Programming" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="94a248ecf6464ebbab013f0e0601d08c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="326fd1f2d6d143c3915c58a639ce8126"><span data-offset-key="326fd1f2d6d143c3915c58a639ce8126:0">Programming</span></span></span></a><span key="8dd94a9c939e47b7bf4585f7ac0f31bc"><span offset-key="8dd94a9c939e47b7bf4585f7ac0f31bc:0"> is the process by which programmers combine these primitives to compose new programs, or adapt existing ones to new uses or a changing environment.</span></span>

<span key="9b23aa9c439743ed9a2f7f5c85165125"><span offset-key="9b23aa9c439743ed9a2f7f5c85165125:0">Programs for a computer might be </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Execution_(computing)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c3154cd2abba4e03b6914963af0b91e3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="aec873335fc64d468892deefef3532da"><span data-offset-key="aec873335fc64d468892deefef3532da:0">executed</span></span></span></a><span key="83dcc7bb7d3044828704a1e31706fee5"><span offset-key="83dcc7bb7d3044828704a1e31706fee5:0"> in a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Batch_processing" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a2bdf7c634f6492e9f1575325ac72004" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="5b5777b95e104d129c8ae2bd8878f658"><span data-offset-key="5b5777b95e104d129c8ae2bd8878f658:0">batch process</span></span></span></a><span key="7e39c1f8861440888afa9aeda6e0c425"><span offset-key="7e39c1f8861440888afa9aeda6e0c425:0"> without human interaction, or a user might type </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Command_(computing)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e2ba77924e7240e7bfe308a8e724d8d3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="96758b5196264a449b4173ab124379f1"><span data-offset-key="96758b5196264a449b4173ab124379f1:0">commands</span></span></span></a><span key="f184b28a38594d26ae3beb68235e8b81"><span offset-key="f184b28a38594d26ae3beb68235e8b81:0"> in an </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Session_(computer_science)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="717b3b667cc94e65be57fc8271313c49" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="974d0df932a0407c97cd6b0ca3643d39"><span data-offset-key="974d0df932a0407c97cd6b0ca3643d39:0">interactive session</span></span></span></a><span key="abe0417da04f4f7ead87d95e0a985c23"><span offset-key="abe0417da04f4f7ead87d95e0a985c23:0"> of an </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Interpreter_(computing)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b626c64c661b4d039049af3a3050d1db" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="a66f39c468a54c55b49040eae2a6e16b"><span data-offset-key="a66f39c468a54c55b49040eae2a6e16b:0">interpreter</span></span></span></a><span key="174b6352578641dea1c1bd5383e3fc0b"><span offset-key="174b6352578641dea1c1bd5383e3fc0b:0">. In this case the "commands" are simply programs, whose execution is chained together. When a language can run its commands through an interpreter (such as a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Unix_shell" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b5abc850a9a840c0b8833581fb8b3cd1" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="831da6eee54141559919fd24b96743db"><span data-offset-key="831da6eee54141559919fd24b96743db:0">Unix shell</span></span></span></a><span key="c5db58c3264b4dd28a200b58f89e7565"><span offset-key="c5db58c3264b4dd28a200b58f89e7565:0"> or other </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Command-line_interface" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="320356507e4245a9b59f31b25daa35bc" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="027ca11935b8453799af713009466efe"><span data-offset-key="027ca11935b8453799af713009466efe:0">command-line interface</span></span></span></a><span key="31ef7c82041c4f11b4f85cb6f8076135"><span offset-key="31ef7c82041c4f11b4f85cb6f8076135:0">), without compiling, it is called a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scripting_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="84508e21fc8c4935bb6f71c11589d616" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="3cfb1431c11540479d9cd2834c2d809a"><span data-offset-key="3cfb1431c11540479d9cd2834c2d809a:0">scripting language</span></span></span></a><span key="79ccba0961aa4954953c727715203fdf"><span offset-key="79ccba0961aa4954953c727715203fdf:0">.</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-67" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d2c15d70db3a42b2b241d94784a1396f" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="868e1ea6ecef4ac38999a510a7dae372"><span data-offset-key="868e1ea6ecef4ac38999a510a7dae372:0">[67]</span></span></span></a><span key="61ab805edc704c548876618ce6d91365"><span offset-key="61ab805edc704c548876618ce6d91365:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

### 

<span key="c3dba50182c247f69e8312f2fb806d3f"><span offset-key="c3dba50182c247f69e8312f2fb806d3f:0">Measuring language usage\[</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Programming_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="df2097b135c24fcfa105210a493617df" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="fe79c1e59535478ea0cf6b97d490c427"><span data-offset-key="fe79c1e59535478ea0cf6b97d490c427:0">edit</span></span></span></a><span key="c976118eac9d42b5b5ed9634c075f079"><span offset-key="c976118eac9d42b5b5ed9634c075f079:0">\]</span></span>

<span key="23d87472eacd422096057a63a52e6988"><span offset-key="23d87472eacd422096057a63a52e6988:0">Main article: </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Measuring_programming_language_popularity" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8e9833ab59694fd39c969f269cd45ed2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="5ff7710c3d274407a41a3e5caeac7892"><span data-offset-key="5ff7710c3d274407a41a3e5caeac7892:0">Measuring programming language popularity</span></span></span></a><span key="6737434ad5ee463c8b7e492ff05f6889"><span offset-key="6737434ad5ee463c8b7e492ff05f6889:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="df392364b83c4c3fbf02c813139b14d0"><span offset-key="df392364b83c4c3fbf02c813139b14d0:0">Determining which is the most widely used programming language is difficult since the definition of usage varies by context. One language may occupy the greater number of programmer hours, a different one has more lines of code, and a third may consume the most CPU time. Some languages are very popular for particular kinds of applications. For example, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/COBOL" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8aefd5acf3fb437db801988b2d96d1b0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="03a018ce328348bea57cc06daa2b3122"><span data-offset-key="03a018ce328348bea57cc06daa2b3122:0">COBOL</span></span></span></a><span key="0c4cb6b5056341eebfa8c46a0897b453"><span offset-key="0c4cb6b5056341eebfa8c46a0897b453:0"> is still strong in the corporate data center, often on large </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mainframe_computer" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk transportation, military, real-time and embedded applications; and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/C_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf applications and operating systems. Other languages are regularly used to write many different kinds of applications.</span></span>

<span key="6c91b320209e47af96da731866522712"><span offset-key="6c91b320209e47af96da731866522712:0">Various methods of measuring language popularity, each subject to a different bias over what is measured, have been proposed:</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="174eaf7d493d4411b8543cbb74ae1637"><span offset-key="174eaf7d493d4411b8543cbb74ae1637:0">counting the number of job advertisements that mention the language</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-70" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="119b02e0fe2549eb981ac7eca3a7338d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="4363a775ec674f6a8446769d07239b78"><span data-offset-key="4363a775ec674f6a8446769d07239b78:0">[70]</span></span></span></a><span key="8c924c50d7a34a5681e4c9aa1b768247"><span offset-key="8c924c50d7a34a5681e4c9aa1b768247:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="0badbdf07cac489fa9a6e1090b0f601b"><span offset-key="0badbdf07cac489fa9a6e1090b0f601b:0">the number of books sold that teach or describe the language</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-71" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="869a8accaca34e68a50f9bdcc66ad280" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="271ec232652f44da92fb6a20d3d516b4"><span data-offset-key="271ec232652f44da92fb6a20d3d516b4:0">[71]</span></span></span></a><span key="c39aa246ca574b859bde5fd39e698bdd"><span offset-key="c39aa246ca574b859bde5fd39e698bdd:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="fbfb9a55894b44e3992152ce4cd91103"><span offset-key="fbfb9a55894b44e3992152ce4cd91103:0">estimates of the number of existing lines of code written in the language – which may underestimate languages not often found in public searches</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Programming_language#cite_note-72" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f84659d32d2944488f7cd77b13509935" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="b1ce2d81442646c18f68298cc06a37ac"><span data-offset-key="b1ce2d81442646c18f68298cc06a37ac:0">[72]</span></span></span></a><span key="8e280e23343b4e71b5bb526f2b4a9527"><span offset-key="8e280e23343b4e71b5bb526f2b4a9527:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="7999362dd4a144dfa00fd5b9ce7d9988"><span offset-key="7999362dd4a144dfa00fd5b9ce7d9988:0">counts of language references (i.e., to the name of the language) found using a web search engine.</span></span>

popular programming languages as (in descending order by overall popularity): </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Java_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 ## 

<span key="e9a311519f65448fa097ae12a8a3c974"><span offset-key="e9a311519f65448fa097ae12a8a3c974:0">Dialects, flavors and implementations\[</span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Programming_language&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4c24de5df90341da8a0377352fde6b39" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="bfb5bcae5dd7471b88c21ed1abf04166"><span data-offset-key="bfb5bcae5dd7471b88c21ed1abf04166:0">edit</span></span></span></a><span key="bd0b69e9874b44a59f027a2d742b15e2"><span offset-key="bd0b69e9874b44a59f027a2d742b15e2:0">\]</span></span>

<span key="0edcd9a6e9e447c0973554824b1acce8"><span offset-key="0edcd9a6e9e447c0973554824b1acce8:0">A </span>**dialect**<span offset-key="0edcd9a6e9e447c0973554824b1acce8:2"> of a programming language or a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_exchange_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="620df7e624b84abc9ca0273eaf150ba8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="8beea81bb0d346aa9849ca9c368db3ac"><span data-offset-key="8beea81bb0d346aa9849ca9c368db3ac:0">data exchange language</span></span></span></a><span key="735f692260bc41358247a25de8b7e10b"><span offset-key="735f692260bc41358247a25de8b7e10b:0"> is a (relatively small) variation or extension of the language that does not change its intrinsic nature. With languages such as </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scheme_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="eb99239f01a9471c8cb8d554729dd6f0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="cbea5a7e6f584d1fb910d51746626551"><span data-offset-key="cbea5a7e6f584d1fb910d51746626551:0">Scheme</span></span></span></a><span key="f5ce5c2f418e4dee992de054abab33f4"><span offset-key="f5ce5c2f418e4dee992de054abab33f4:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Forth_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="439c6b590ec34b8ab533418db4aa903e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="78ff5616128a4d04b27a8b8228154118"><span data-offset-key="78ff5616128a4d04b27a8b8228154118:0">Forth</span></span></span></a><span key="b5b99da7530d47a7a34858392327fb45"><span offset-key="b5b99da7530d47a7a34858392327fb45:0">, standards may be considered insufficient, inadequate or illegitimate by implementors, so often they will deviate from the standard, making a new </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dialect" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="58792f9d2f814922ba53f5348b353eb3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="11ecfd2fb23a40e18977a90b1b608e73"><span data-offset-key="11ecfd2fb23a40e18977a90b1b608e73:0">dialect</span></span></span></a><span key="9674bdc44e4e41868489bcabd14b6fec"><span offset-key="9674bdc44e4e41868489bcabd14b6fec:0">. In other cases, a dialect is created for use in a </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Domain-specific_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="9d6dbfc32147459c8310bee6654d5a7c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="71f67cd93eb2411b91703f11c4d68136"><span data-offset-key="71f67cd93eb2411b91703f11c4d68136:0">domain-specific language</span></span></span></a><span key="17cc6ce8cd3b4f02892dfef17950a715"><span offset-key="17cc6ce8cd3b4f02892dfef17950a715:0">, often a subset. In the </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Common_Lisp" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d4be13278426498488d2ce9331daa1ed" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="b2fa9c707bf84ef4a10e4b9ced727804"><span data-offset-key="b2fa9c707bf84ef4a10e4b9ced727804:0">Lisp</span></span></span></a><span key="b4a40c413e3b4c808af23e4a6bbfebcb"><span offset-key="b4a40c413e3b4c808af23e4a6bbfebcb:0"> world, most languages that use basic </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/S-expression" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c55ef310627a48bf96de2006c7e7939b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="e6b5f4c17bf043b09f48e21141e0b601"><span data-offset-key="e6b5f4c17bf043b09f48e21141e0b601:0">S-expression</span></span></span></a><span key="ff53fb3e02f84b2c8ae59094b4c052c9"><span offset-key="ff53fb3e02f84b2c8ae59094b4c052c9:0"> syntax and Lisp-like semantics are considered Lisp dialects, although they vary wildly, as do, say, </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Racket_(programming_language)" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="7722374a2d1a4d83bab2217c9dbe2d1e" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="2e099687e2e54c1187a081b1c722a380"><span data-offset-key="2e099687e2e54c1187a081b1c722a380:0">Racket</span></span></span></a><span key="937fc28d570f432da46de790c12bb74a"><span offset-key="937fc28d570f432da46de790c12bb74a:0"> and </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Clojure" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f68f4043c3ca4e828ab81a6e4c816b29" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="1eceb6586e264707a6c9992c8ab1a8d1"><span data-offset-key="1eceb6586e264707a6c9992c8ab1a8d1:0">Clojure</span></span></span></a><span key="795e60f2de14470ab0672b042a1c296c"><span offset-key="795e60f2de14470ab0672b042a1c296c:0">. As it is common for one language to have several dialects, it can become quite difficult for an inexperienced programmer to find the right documentation. The </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/BASIC_programming_language" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c3f22abf98f6422e9205b1a021b8c246" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="046a36519522466ca05416c43b179710"><span data-offset-key="046a36519522466ca05416c43b179710:0">BASIC programming language</span></span></span></a><span key="5578e1d4c44145ca8faad92099d7ba9c"><span offset-key="5578e1d4c44145ca8faad92099d7ba9c:0"> has </span></span><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_BASIC_dialects" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="53ebb8d2edb744388b3bdbf75b234df2" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_257-12357_259-12358-237__"><span data-key="e98c6788e4fa4b7ba74099b9371ebbfa"><span data-offset-key="e98c6788e4fa4b7ba74099b9371ebbfa:0">many dialects</span></span></span></a><span key="f681c3000cb74dee9901a6cb37dcd380"><span offset-key="f681c3000cb74dee9901a6cb37dcd380:0">.</span></span>

<span key="01bdfe243ecb4376a85056d561213a79"><span offset-key="01bdfe243ecb4376a85056d561213a79:0">The explosion of Forth dialects led to the saying "If you've seen one Forth... you've seen one Forth."</span></span>

<a href="programming-languages/sql/postgresql.html" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1awozwy r-14lw9ot r-190qawg r-z2wwpe r-rs99b7 r-4dj0k7 r-1loqt21 r-1quu1zo r-1ro0kt6 r-18u37iz r-16y2uox r-1wbh5a2 r-nsbfu8 r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"></a>

Dialects, flavors and implementations\[edit\]
